## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar recipe card:**
!

## mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
HEBBARS KITCHEN
mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course sambar
Cuisine south indian
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor daal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 to matoes
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chillies
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

#### seasoning ingredients
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω split urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.
  * once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.
  * meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.
  * bullet idli sambar
  * furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.
  * now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.
  * add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.
  * additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.
  * bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  * furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.
  * prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.
  * finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with bullet idli's dipped in this sambar.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar step by step photo recipe:**
  1. firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.  !
  2. once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.  !
  3. meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.  !
  4. furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.  !
  5. now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.  !
  6. also add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.  !
  7. additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.  !
  8. bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  9. furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.  !
  10. prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.  !
  11. finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with **** dipped in this sambar.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, idlis taste great when dipped in sambar for atleast 5 minutes.
  * furthermore, you can add **** if you wish to make it more spicy.
  * moreover, mash the dal properly so that the consistency is maintained.
  * finally, ad a tsp of ghee to make it more flavourful.

# Recipe 20

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | easy paddu recipe card below:
!

## guliappa recipe / paddu recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
guliyappa recipe / paddu recipe
5 from 188 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 12 hours hrs
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 12 hours hrs 30 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 30 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal / split black lentils
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup sona masuri rice / chawal / dosa rice
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp menthe / fenugreek seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup paper avalakki / beaten rice / poha
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for greasing tawa

### Instructions 
  * soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl and soak for 5 hours.
  * first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter.
  * transfer to a large vessel.
  * now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter.
  * now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender.
  * transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well.
  * cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours.
  * the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented.
  * mix the batter slightly.
  * take required batter in a different bowl.
  * finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.
  * add fried onions and ginger, chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves and mix well.
  * also add in salt and mix the batter well.
  * now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.
  * reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.
  * once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.
  * your paddu recipe is ready


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## easy paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | paddu recipe with step by step photo recipe:
  1. soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl. add in enough water and soak for 5 hours. !
  2. first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter. add water if required to make a smooth paste. !
  3. transfer to a large vessel. and keep aside !
  4. now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter. !
  5. now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender. and grind to a smooth thick paste. !
  6. transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well. !
  7. cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours. !
  8. the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented. !
  9. mix the batter slightly. !
  10. take required batter in a different bowl.
  11. finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa.jpg>)
  12. fry the onions and ginger with a table spoon of oil till they turn translucent.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa-11.jpg>)
  13. now add fried onions and ginger along with finely chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves to the batter and mix well.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa31.jpg>)
  14. also add in salt and mix the batter well. ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa4.jpg>)
  15. heat the guliyappa pan and a drop of oil in all moulds.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa5.jpg>)
  16. now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa6.jpg>)
  17. reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa8.jpg>)
  18. once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa10.jpg>)
  19. remove the cooked guliyappas and serve hot with**** or chutney powder.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa12.jpg>)

## notes:
  * first of all, if your guliyappa is not getting golden brown, add some sugar.
  * in addition, adjust the consistency of the batter by adding required water.
  * furthermore, to make it little spicy, add some chopped chilli.
  * finally, skip the masala step and pour the batter directly to moulds, but these onion masala enhances the taste of guliyappa.

# Recipe 21

####

####

####

####

## recipe card for mini idli recipe | idli batter recipe | button idli recipe:
!

## mini idli recipe| bullet idli recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
mini idli recipe| bullet idli recipe
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 12 hours hrs
Cook Time 8 minutes mins
Total Time 12 hours hrs 8 minutes mins
Course Main
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### ingredients for bullet idli batter
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup idli rava - cream of rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal/spilt & skinned black gram lentils
  * ‚ñ¢ salt as required
  * ‚ñ¢ water for soaking
  * ‚ñ¢ coconut oil to grease

### Instructions

#### mini idli batter recipe:
  * firstly, soak the urad dal in enough water for 4-5 hours.
  * furthermore, drain the water from the urad dal and keep it aside.
  * take the urad dal in the wet grinder / mixer. add some of the urad dal strained water and grind.
  * however, if the batter appears too thick, add some water. grind to a smooth batter.
  * after that pour in a non reactive deep pan or pot.
  * furthermore, rinse the idli rava till the water runs clear of the starch.
  * drain the water well from idli rava by squeezing excess water from idli rava.
  * mix the squeezed idli rava to the batter well.
  * make sure there are enough space for batter to raise when fermented.
  * cover and ferment in warm place for atleast 6 - 8 hours.
  * you can see the batter has raised slightly indicating its well fermented.
  * mix the batter slightly and add salt to taste.

#### steaming mini idli recipe:
  * brush idli moulds with oil.
  * pour the batter in the idli moulds.
  * additionally, place the idli stand in the steamer containing with some boiling water.
  * furthermore, cover with a lid and steam the idlis for 10 minutes.
  * finally, arrange the mini idlis then add more sambar on top.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## mini idli recipe | idli batter recipe | bullet idli step by step photo recipe:

### mini idli batter recipe:
  1. firstly, soak the urad dal in enough water for 4-5 hours. !
  2. furthermore, drain the water from the urad dal and keep it aside. we will use some of this water for grinding the idlis.
  3. take the urad dal in the wet grinder / mixer. add some of the urad dal strained water and grind.  !
  4. however, if the batter appears too thick, add some water. grind to a smooth batter.  !
  5. after that pour in a non reactive deep pan or pot.  !
  6. furthermore, rinse the idli rava till the water runs clear of the starch.  !
  7. drain the water well from idli rava by squeezing excess water from idli rava.  !
  8. mix the squeezed idli rava to the batter well. always mix the batter with your hand to make sure there are no lumps in the batter  !
  9. make sure there are enough space for batter to raise when fermented. !
  10. cover and ferment in warm place for atleast 6 ‚Äì 8 hours. see notes section for tips n fermentation.
  11. you can see the batter has raised slightly indicating its well fermented. !
  12. mix the batter slightly and add salt to taste. !

### steaming mini idli recipe:
  1. brush idli moulds with oil.
  2. pour the batter in the idli moulds. !
  3. additionally, place the idli stand in the steamer containing with some boiling water. !
  4. furthermore, cover with a lid and steam the idlis for 10 minutes. !
  5. finally, arrange the mini idlis then add more **** on top. drizzle ghee. serve hot with  and .  !

## notes:
  * firstly, you can use pressure cooker to steam idlis. but don‚Äôt put the vent weight / whistle.
  * furthermore, do not add salt for the entire batter, if you want to store batter for long time.
  * moreover, always store the batter in airtight container in refrigerator.
  * most noteworthy, do not add too much water while grinding the batter. add only required amount.
  * most of all, if you live in cold countries then cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours.
  * if you live in a warmer place**,** then ferment for 8 hour max.
  * finally, i usually keep my batter in pre heated oven (switch off the oven though) to ferment idli batter well. if possible try to preheat oven ever 3-4 hours.

## banana rasayana recipe card below :

## banana rasayana | balehannu rasayana recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
banana rasayana or balehannu rasayana or banana seehikarne recipe
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course Dessert
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 -5

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 - 11 bananas
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup fresh grated coconut
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 - 5 tbsp of sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 - 4 cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch of salt

### Instructions 
  * finely chop the bananas into small pieces and keep it aside.
  * take 1 cup of grated coconut and grind it to smooth paste with 1/4th cup of water. add 3-4 cardamom extract before grinding.
  * squeeze and extract the coconut milk from the grated coconut.
  * add 4- 5 tbsp of sugar and a pinch of salt to the chopped banana and mix it well.
  * add the extracted coconut milk to the chopped bananas and mix well.
  * banana rasayana is ready. serve it with neer dosa, plain dosa, tuppa dosa and pooris.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## banana rasayana ‚Äì step by step photo recipe :
  1. finely chop the bananas into small pieces and keep it aside.  !
  2. take 1 cup of grated coconut and grind it to smooth paste with 1/4th cup of water. add 3-4 cardamom extract before grinding.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/banana-rasayana-balehannina-rasayana/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/banana-rasayana5.jpg>)
  3. squeeze and extract the coconut milk from the grated coconut.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/banana-rasayana-balehannina-rasayana/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/banana-rasayana6.jpg>)
  4. add 4- 5 tbsp of sugar and a pinch of salt to the chopped banana and mix it well.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/banana-rasayana-balehannina-rasayana/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/banana-rasayana7.jpg>) ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/banana-rasayana-balehannina-rasayana/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/banana-rasayana8.jpg>)
  5. add the extracted coconut milk to the chopped bananas and mix well.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/banana-rasayana-balehannina-rasayana/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/banana-rasayana9.jpg>)

## notes:
  * i have prepared the coconut milk freshly, however store brought coconut milk can also be used.
  * if you do not like coconut milk, replace it with cows milk.

# Recipe 23
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/badam-burfi-recipe-almond-badam-katli/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Badam Burfi
An excellent and tasty Indian sweet recipe made with a combination of powdered almond and desiccated coconut in a one-string sugar syrup. **Badam Burfi,** known as Badam Katli, is an ideal festival recipe for offering Prasadam to beloved gods. It can also be a perfect sweet snack and be served and exchanged with friends and family. In addition, it is also considered a healthy alternative compared to other dry fruits and sweets, significant because of Almonds.
There are many different ways to make this classical **Badam Burfi Recipe**. The variations mainly differ from the supporting ingredients added to this classical dessert. The typical combination is coconut, but it is not limited. It can take other dry fruit powders like cashews, pasta, and dates. Adding these makes it richer and premium, with just badam powder. In addition, adding rava, besan, and even wheat powder can give it a crunchy texture.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Badam Burfi
!

## Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi with Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi Recipe | Badam Katli Recipe**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 1 hour hr
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 15 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 20 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup badam / almonds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp saffron milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cardamom / elachi, powdered
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak almonds in hot water for 1 hour.
  * now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.
  * also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.
  * transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.
  * meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.
  * keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.
  * boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.
  * now add the prepared almond powder, saffron milk and cardamom powder.
  * mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.
  * continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan.
  * transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.
  * and allow to cool for 5 minutes.
  * grease your hand with little ghee and knead for a minute.
  * once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin,.
  * furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.
  * you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  * finally, serve badam burfi / badam katli on diwali or any festival.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Badam Burfi with Step-by-step Photos

### badam powder or almond meal recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak ¬æ cup of almonds in 1 cup of hot water for 1 hour.  !
  2. now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.  !
  3. also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.  !
  4. transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.  !

### badam buri | almond barfi recipe:
  1. meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  2. keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.  !
  3. boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.  !
  4. now add the prepared almond powder.  !
  5. also add saffron milk. to prepare saffron milk, soak few strands of saffron in warm milk for 10 minutes.  !
  6. additionally add cardamom powder for more flavours.  !
  7. mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.  !
  8. once the mixture begins to boil, add a tbsp of . however, it is optional, but do add more flavour to burfi.  !
  9. continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan. if you prefer slightly hard burfi then continue to stir for longer time.  !
  10. transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.  !
  11. add a tsp of **** to make smooth dough.  !
  12. and allow to cool for 5 minutes. do not rest more, as they will turn hard and wont be able to give shape.  !
  13. grease your hand with little  and knead for a minute. be careful as the dough will be very hot. try to knead when its hot, else it will be difficult. and do not over knead as badam will start releasing oil.  !
  14. once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin, adjusting the thickness according to your choice.  !
  15. furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.  !
  16. you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  17. finally, serve **badam burfi / badam katli** on diwali or any festival. !

## Notes
  * firstly, soak the badam well or blanch it for easy removal of skin.
  * also, make sure to get just 1 string consistency of sugar syrup. else it turns burfi hard and brittle.
  * most noteworthy, use nonstick pan for easy and efficient badam katlis.
  * and entire badam burfi has to be prepared on low flame.
  * finally, instead of butter paper, you can also use a plastic sheet or greased plate to prepare **badam burfi.**

# Recipe 24

### Video Recipe

####

####

## Recipe Card for Bengali Mughlai Paratha
!

## mughlai paratha recipe | moglai porota | veg bengali mughlai paratha
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy mughlai paratha recipe | moglai porota | veg bengali mughlai paratha
5 from 215 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course paratha
Cuisine mughal
Servings 6 paratha

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup maida / plain flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water for kneading

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 capsicum, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 carrot, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kashmiri red chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cumin powder / jeera powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur / dry mango powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup paneer, grated

### Instructions 
  * prepare the stuffing by heating 2 tsp oil.
  * saute ¬Ω onion, 2 chilli and 1 tsp ginger garlic paste for 2 minutes.
  * further add 1 capsicum, 1 carrot and saute till the vegetables shrink.
  * additionally, add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬º tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, ¬º tsp garam masala and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * saute for a minute or till spices turn aromatic.
  * keep aside and allow to cool the paneer stuffing completely.
  * after the dough has rested for 20 minutes, knead slightly and pinch a ball sized dough.
  * roll the dough to slightly thin thickness.
  * further, spread the prepared paneer stuffing in centre.
  * now carefully fold and close all sides of paratha forming a square. press gently.
  * roast the paratha on hot tawa or shallow fry the parathas.
  * spread a tsp of oil on both sides and roast to golden and crisp from all sides.
  * finally, serve veg mughlai paratha along with raita or curry.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Mughlai Paratha with Step-by-step photos
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cups maida, 2 tbsp oil and ¬Ω tsp salt. mix well. !
  2. now add water in batches and knead for 5 minutes. !
  3. knead to a smooth and soft dough. !
  4. grease the dough with a tsp of oil, cover and rest for 20 minutes. !
  5. meanwhile, prepare the stuffing by heating 2 tsp oil. !
  6. saute ¬Ω onion, 2 chilli and 1 tsp ginger garlic paste for 2 minutes. !
  7. further add 1 capsicum, 1 carrot and saute till the vegetables shrink. !
  8. additionally, add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬º tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, ¬º tsp  and ¬Ω tsp salt. !
  9. saute for a minute or till spices turn aromatic. !
  10. now add 2 cup grated paneer and mix well. !
  11. keep aside and allow to cool the paneer stuffing completely. !
  12. after the dough has rested for 20 minutes, knead slightly and pinch a ball sized dough. !
  13. dust the dough with little maida and flatten. !
  14. roll the dough to slightly thin thickness. !
  15. further, spread the prepared paneer stuffing in centre. !
  16. now carefully fold and close all sides of paratha forming a square. press gently. !
  17. roast the paratha on hot tawa or shallow fry the parathas. !
  18. spread a tsp of oil on both sides and roast to golden and crisp from all sides. !
  19. finally, serve **veg** **mughlai paratha** along with  or . !

## Notes
  * firstly, add boiled and potato along with paneer for variation.
  * also, you can use boiled kidney beans (rajma) in the stuffing.
  * additionally, roast/shallow fry the paratha on low flame to get the flaky texture.
  * furthermore, replace maida with wheat flour for healthier version.
  * finally, **veg mughlai paratha** tastes great when prepared spicy.

# Recipe 25
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/veg-frankie-recipe-kathi-frankie-roll/

####

####

## About Veg Frankie
It is a popular and tasty street food recipe from India with a combination of flavors it has to offer. There are myriad types or variations within the Frankie or Roll recipes, but the most popular one is the **Veg Frankie** or **Veg Kathi Roll recipe**. Typically, the roll is made with vegetable patties which are made with a combination of vegetables like carrots, beans, potatoes, and peas. The choice of vegetable is open-ended and it is up to individual taste and preference. Additionally, the patties or rolled inside flatbread or roti with sliced onions and herbs with a range of chutney and condiments sauces.
There are different types of roll or Frankie recipes across India and the variations depend upon the place it is prepared. The most common is **Veg Frankie** and Meat-based Frankie recipe. The choice of patties makes it a filling, complete, and balanced meal. It also makes it an ideal lunch or dinner meal or even a kid‚Äôs tiffin box meal. Typically, Kathi Roll is made with tomato sauce and mayo sauce. But this recipe can take any type of sauce to have different flavors and tastes.

## Chef Tips for Veg Frankie
The recipe is no rocket science and takes only basic ingredients to make it. Yet some important and basic tips and suggestions are ‚Äì
  1. **Wrap Quality ‚Äì** The wrap should be soft and moist so that it can be easily rolled. If the roti wrap turns hard, it may not be usable or to shape it.
  2. **Rolling Technique ‚Äì** Place the vegetables and patties at the center. Also, wrap it tightly so that the stuffing and sauce do not ooze out while eating it.
  3. **Condiments ‚Äì** Try to mix and match the sauce so that all flavors are combined to make it lip-smacking. In short, try to have the sweet, spicy, and savory flavors added to it.
  4. **Vegetables Stuffing ‚Äì** Keep it simple and use basic vegetables like onions, carrots, and shredded lettuce.
  5. **Spice Mix ‚Äì** You may top it up with Frankie masala to make it more flavored and exciting.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Veg Frankie

## Veg Frankie Recipe | Veg Kathi Roll Recipe | Veg Frankie Roll Recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Veg Frankie Recipe | Veg Kathi Roll Recipe | Veg Frankie Roll Recipe**
5 from 234 votes

Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine street food

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cloves garlic, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp chilli sauce
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 potato, boiled & mashed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

#### for chilli vinegar:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt

#### for roll:
  * ‚ñ¢ 
  * ‚ñ¢ coriander
  * ‚ñ¢ chaat masala
  * ‚ñ¢ onion
  * ‚ñ¢

### Instructions

#### How to make roti for frankie:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup maida, ¬Ω cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬º cup curd.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Now add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.
  * Grease the dough with oil, cover and rest for 20 minutes.
  * After the dough has rested well, knead the dough again and pinch a ball-sized dough.
  * Dust with maida and roll thin.
  * Now cook the roti on hot pan spreading oil.
  * Flip over and cook both sides.
  * Also, spread the oil and cook until the roti is cooked from both sides. Keep aside.

#### How to make stuffing for kathi roll:
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, 2 chilli, 2 cloves garlic and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste. Saute well until the raw aroma goes off.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, 2 tbsp chilli sauce and 2 tbsp tomato sauce.
  * Saute on low flame until the spices are well combined.
  * Now add 3 potato, ¬Ω tsp salt and mix well.
  * Mix until the spices are well combined.
  * Now add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tsp lemon juice and mix well.
  * Once the mixture is cooled slightly, shape the tikki.
  * Roast on hot pan adding oil as required.
  * Roast both the sides until the tikki turns golden brown and crispy. Keep aside.

#### How to make chilli vinegar:
  * In a small bowl take 3 tbsp vinegar, 2 chilli and ¬º tsp salt.
  * Mix well, and chilli vinegar is ready to use.

#### How to assemble veg frankie.
  * Firstly, take roti and spread green chutney.
  * Place the prepared aloo tikki, and top with coriander, chaat masala, onion, chilli vinegar and tomato sauce.
  * Roll tight and wrap in butter paper.
  * Finally, Veg Frankie Recipe is ready to enjoy with tomato sauce.

## How To Make Veg Kathi Roll with Step-by-step Photos

### How to make roti for frankie:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup maida, ¬Ω cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt, and ¬º cup curd.  !
  2. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Now add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.  !
  4. Grease the dough with oil, cover and rest for 20 minutes.  !
  5. After the dough has rested well, knead the dough again and pinch a ball-sized dough.  !
  6. Dust with maida and roll thin.  !
  7. Now cook the roti on hot pan spreading oil.  !
  8. Flip over and cook both sides. Also, spread the oil and cook until the roti is cooked from both sides. Keep aside.  !

### How to make stuffing for kathi roll:
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, 2 chilli, 2 cloves garlic and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste. Saute well until the raw aroma goes off.  !
  2. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, 2 tbsp chilli sauce and 2 tbsp tomato sauce.  !
  3. Saute on low flame until the spices are well combined.  !
  4. Now add 3 potato, ¬Ω tsp salt and mix well.  !
  5. Mix until the spices are well combined.  !
  6. Now add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tsp lemon juice and mix well.  !
  7. Once the mixture is cooled slightly, shape the tikki.  !
  8. Roast on hot pan adding oil as required.  !
  9. Roast both sides until the tikki turns golden brown and crispy. Keep aside.  !

### How to make chilli vinegar:
  1. In a small bowl take 3 tbsp vinegar, 2 chilli and ¬º tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well, and chilli vinegar is ready to use.  !

### How to assemble veg frankie.
  1. Firstly, take roti and spread green chutney.  !
  2. Place the prepared aloo tikki, and top with coriander, chaat masala, onion, chilli vinegar and tomato sauce.  !
  3. Roll tight and wrap in butter paper.  !
  4. Finally, **Veg Frankie Recipe** is ready to enjoy with tomato sauce.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to not overcook the roti as it hardens and does not remain soft after some time.
  * Also, you can use frankie masala instead of using chaat masala.
  * Additionally, you can top it with cheese to make a cheesy kathi roll.
  * Finally, **Veg Frankie Recipe** tastes great when it is made spicy and served hot.

# Recipe 26
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/basanti-pulao-recipe-sweet-spicy-pulao/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Basanti Pulao
It is a simple and traditional pulao rice recipe made with a combination of sweet and spicy flavors. Generally, the Basanti Pulao recipe is prepared and served for celebration feasts and auspicious occasions. However, it can also be a perfect and ideal lunch box recipe when served with spicy meat or any coconut-based curries. Alternatively, it can also be an ideal 2-in-one dessert rice recipe like Kesari bath or even zarda rice recipe.
There are many ways this simple and easy Basanti Pulao Rice Recipe is prepared. Traditionally it is prepared with  Rice which is very similar to basmati or long-grained rice. It can be tricky to get this rice and hence it can also be prepared with basmati rice which is easy and simple to source. In addition, the rice can also be prepared with the addition of vegetables, which makes it a complete pulao. However, not recommended when this rice is made as dessert.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Basanti Pulao:
!

## Basanti Pulao Recipe | Sweet & Spicy Pulao Rice
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Basanti Pulao Recipe | Sweet & Spicy Pulao Rice
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course pulao
Cuisine bengali
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 396 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 pod cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cashew
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp raisins
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 6 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup sugar

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup rice and soak for 30 minutes. Traditionally, Bengali Pulao is made with Gobindobhog Rice. However, you can use any short-grain rice or basmati rice.
  * Drain off the water and transfer to the plate.
  * Add 1 tsp ginger paste, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tbsp ghee.
  * Mix gently, making sure the spices are well coated in the rice.
  * Now in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil, 1 tsp ghee.
  * Add 1 bay leaf, 4 pods cardamom, 5 cloves, 1 inch cinnamon, 2 tbsp cashew and 2 tbsp raisins.
  * Roast on low flame until the cashews turn golden brown.
  * Add in soaked rice and cook for 2 minutes. Make sure not to break the rice grains.
  * Once the rice turns shiny, add ¬æ tsp salt and 2 cup water.
  * Mix well, cover and simmer for 10 minutes.
  * After 10 minutes, mix gently, and you can see the rice would be half cooked.
  * Now place 6 chilli and ¬º cup sugar.
  * Cover and simmer for 10 more minutes, or until the rice is cooked well.
  * Remove the kadai from the heat and let the rice rest for 5 minutes before serving.
  * Finally, enjoy Basanti Pulao with Kosha Mangsho (Bengali Mutton Curry) or any spicy veg curry.

### Nutrition
Calories: 396kcalCarbohydrates: 64gProtein: 6gFat: 14gSaturated Fat: 3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 7gTrans Fat: 0.03gCholesterol: 10mgSodium: 455mgPotassium: 387mgFiber: 3gSugar: 16gVitamin A: 645IUVitamin C: 98mgCalcium: 39mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Basanti Pulao with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup rice and soak for 30 minutes. Traditionally, Bengali Pulao is made with Gobindobhog Rice. However, you can use any short-grain rice or basmati rice.  !
  2. Drain off the water and transfer to the plate.  !
  3. Add 1 tsp ginger paste, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tbsp ghee.  !
  4. Mix gently, making sure the spices are well coated in the rice.  !
  5. Now in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil, 1 tsp ghee.  !
  6. Add 1 bay leaf, 4 pods cardamom, 5 cloves, 1 inch cinnamon, 2 tbsp cashew and 2 tbsp raisins.  !
  7. Roast on low flame until the cashews turn golden brown.  !
  8. Add in soaked rice and cook for 2 minutes. Make sure not to break the rice grains.  !
  9. Once the rice turns shiny, add ¬æ tsp salt and 2 cup water.  !
  10. Mix well, cover and simmer for 10 minutes.  !
  11. After 10 minutes, mix gently, and you can see the rice would be half cooked. Now place 6 chilli and ¬º cup sugar.  !
  12. Cover and simmer for 10 more minutes, or until the rice is cooked well.  !
  13. Remove the kadai from the heat and let the rice rest for 5 minutes before serving.  !
  14. Finally, enjoy Basanti Pulao with Kosha Mangsho (Bengali Mutton Curry) or any spicy veg curry.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to use aged rice, or else the rice will turn sticky.
  * Additionally, adjust the rice and water ratio depending on the quality of the rice you are using.
  * Also, cooking on low flame helps to cook rice grains perfectly.
  * Finally, the **Basanti Pulao** tastes great when served the next day when flavors are absorbed.

## Recipe Card for Raw Papaya Transparent Chutney :

## Plastic Chutney Recipe | Raw Papaya Transparent Chutney - Wedding Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Plastic Chutney Recipe | Raw Papaya Transparent Chutney - Wedding Style
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course chutney
Cuisine bengali
Servings 1 Bowl
Calories 1174 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω raw papaya
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kalonji seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cashew
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp raisins
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

### Instructions 
  * firstly, remove the seeds and peel the skin of raw papaya.
  * slice the papaya as thin as possible.
  * rinse and soak in water to remove the latex.
  * heat 1 tbsp oil, and saute the sliced papaya for a minute.
  * add 1 cup water and boil for 10 minutes.
  * now add 1 cup sugar and mix well.
  * now add ¬º tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp kalonji seeds, 2 tbsp cashew, and 2 tbsp raisins.
  * mix well and boil for 10 minutes or until the papaya turns translucent.
  * add ¬Ω lemon to prevent sugar syrup from caramelizing.
  * continue to cook until the papaya turns translucent and slightly yellowish.
  * finally, enjoy Plastic Chutney with rice or roti.

### Nutrition
Calories: 1174kcalCarbohydrates: 250gProtein: 6gFat: 24gSaturated Fat: 3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 6gMonounsaturated Fat: 14gTrans Fat: 0.1gSodium: 619mgPotassium: 735mgFiber: 7gSugar: 214gVitamin A: 1456IUVitamin C: 123mgCalcium: 70mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make plastic chutney with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, remove the seeds and peel the skin of raw papaya.  !
  2. slice the papaya as thin as possible.  !
  3. rinse and soak in water to remove the latex.  !
  4. heat 1 tbsp oil, and saute the sliced papaya for a minute.  !
  5. add 1 cup water and boil for 10 minutes.  !
  6. now add 1 cup sugar and mix well.  !
  7. now add ¬º tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp kalonji seeds, 2 tbsp cashew, and 2 tbsp raisins.  !
  8. mix well and boil for 10 minutes or until the papaya turns translucent.  !
  9. add ¬Ω lemon to prevent sugar syrup from caramelizing.  !
  10. continue to cook until the papaya turns translucent and slightly yellowish.  !
  11. finally, enjoy **Plastic Chutney** with rice or roti.  !

## Notes:
  * firstly, make sure to cut into a uniform thickness, else it will not get cooked easily.
  * also, adjust the amount of sugar based on the sweetness you are looking for.
  * additionally, add more water if the papaya is uncooked.
  * finally, **Plastic Chutney Recipe** tastes great when served with little sugar syrup.

# Recipe 28
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/rasgulla-recipe-bengali-rosogulla/

### rasgulla video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for bengali rosogulla recipe:
!

## rasgulla recipe | bengali rosogulla | how to make sponge rasgulla
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy rasgulla recipe | bengali rosogulla | how to make sponge rasgulla
5 from 241 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Resting Time 1 hour hr
Total Time 1 hour hr 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine bengali
Servings 17 rasgulla

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 litre milk, full cream
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 pod cardamom

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large vessel get 2 litre milk of milk to a boil stirring occasionally.
  * once the milk comes to a boil, pour 2 tbsp lemon juice and stir well. you can alternatively use curd or vinegar.
  * stir until the milk curdles keeping the flame on low to medium.
  * do not boil further once water separates completely.
  * drain the curdled milk over a cloth-lined over a colander. you can use the leftover water to make soup or knead the dough as they are very nutritious.
  * squeeze off the water completely. be careful as the curdled milk will be very hot.
  * rinse off the curdled milk with fresh water to remove sourness from lemon juice.
  * squeeze off the water completely. do not over squeeze as the moisture in paneer will be lost.
  * hang for 1 hour making sure the water is drained completely, yet remain the moisture.
  * after 1 hour, start to mash the paneer for 5 minutes.
  * mash the paneer till it turns out smooth texture without any grains of paneer.
  * now prepare small ball sized paneer and keep aside. cover and keep to prevent from drying.
  * in a large vessel take 1 cup sugar, 5 cup water and 3 pod cardamom.
  * stir and dissolve the sugar completely.
  * now boil the water for 5 minutes.
  * drop in rolled paneer balls one by one into boiling sugar water.
  * cover and boil for 10 minutes or until rasgulla doubles in size.
  * now drop into ice-cold water immediately, to prevent from shrinking in size.
  * once cooled completely, take into a serving bowl and pour in leftover sugar water.
  * finally, enjoy rasgulla chilled or as it is.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make rasgulla with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large vessel get 2 litre milk of milk to a boil stirring occasionally. !
  2. once the milk comes to a boil, pour 2 tbsp lemon juice and stir well. you can alternatively use curd or vinegar. !
  3. stir until the milk curdles keeping the flame on low to medium. do not boil further once water separates completely. !
  4. drain the curdled milk over a cloth-lined over a colander. you can use the leftover water to make  or knead the dough as they are very nutritious. !
  5. rinse off the curdled milk with fresh water to remove sourness from lemon juice. !
  6. squeeze off the water completely. do not over squeeze as the moisture in paneer will be lost. hang for 1 hour making sure the water is drained completely, yet remain the moisture. !
  7. after 1 hour, start to mash the paneer for 5 minutes. !
  8. mash the paneer till it turns out smooth texture without any grains of paneer. now prepare small ball sized paneer and keep aside. cover and keep to prevent from drying. !
  9. in a large vessel take 1 cup sugar, 5 cup water and 3 pod cardamom. !
  10. stir and dissolve the sugar completely. !
  11. now boil the water for 5 minutes. !
  12. drop in rolled paneer balls one by one into boiling sugar water. !
  13. cover and boil for 10 minutes or until rasgulla doubles in size. !
  14. now drop into ice-cold water immediately, to prevent from shrinking in size. !
  15. once cooled completely, take into a serving bowl and pour in leftover sugar water. !
  16. finally, enjoy **rasgulla** chilled or as it is. !

## notes:
  * firstly, use fresh full cream cows milk to get good quality paneer.
  * also, make sure not to have any cracks on paneer balls. else they may break while boiling.
  * additionally, do not open the lid while boiling, as the temperature will drop and rasgulla may fall flat.
  * finally, **rasgulla recipe** can be served with slightly concentrated sugar syrup if you prefer.

# Recipe 29
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/rasmalai-rabdi-recipe-secret-8-tips/

### Rasmalai Recipe video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for Rasamali Halwai Style:
!

## Rasmalai Recipe | Soft Rasamali & Rabdi Halwai Style 9 Secret Tips
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy Rasmalai Recipe | Soft Rasamali & Rabdi Halwai Style 9 Secret Tips
5 from 1 vote
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 45 minutes mins
Resting Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 25 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine bengali
Servings 18 Servings
Calories 93 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for chenna:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 litre  milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 pod cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 7 cup water

#### for rabdi:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 litre  milk
  * ‚ñ¢ few saffron
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch saffron food colour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp nuts, chopped

### Instructions

#### how to prepare chenna for rasmalai:
  * firstly, get 2 litre to a boil stirring in between to prevent it from burning.
  * add 2 tbsp vinegar and give stir. you will notice the milk starts to curdle.
  * add 1 more tbsp of vinegar and stir until the milk curdles fully separating water.
  * drain off the water over the cheesecloth. you can use any clean cloth here.
  * rinse with cold water to remove sourness and stop cooking.
  * squeeze the paneer gently and hang for 30 minutes.
  * now take the moist paneer and crumble gently.
  * using the palm, start to knead gently.
  * knead until the paneer mixture turns smooth without any grains. do not over-knead here as the rasgulla will turn hard.
  * pinch a small ball sized chenna and prepare smooth crack free balls, flatten slightly.
  * keep the flattened paneer ball aside and cover with a moist cloth.

#### how to boil rasmalai in sugar syrup:
  * firstly, in a large vessel, take 1¬Ω cup sugar, 3 pods cardamom and 7 cup water.
  * stir and dissolve sugar.
  * now boil the water for 5 minutes or until the syrup turns slightly sticky.
  * drop in a prepared flattened paneer ball keeping the flame on high.
  * cover and boil for 7 minutes or until the size of the ball doubles.
  * chenna has been cooked well. keep aside.

#### how to make rabdi:
  * firstly, in a large kadai heat 1-litre milk, few saffron and pinch of saffron food colour.
  * stir and get the milk to a boil.
  * continue to cook until the milk thickens slightly.
  * now add ¬Ω cup sugar and continue to boil.
  * do not make very thick milk as it will be difficult for chenna to absorb milk.
  * also, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and 2 tbsp nuts. mix well.

#### how to soak rasmalai in rabdi:
  * squeeze off the sugar syrup from the cooked paneer balls.
  * place them in a tray and pour in prepared rabdi.
  * rest for at least 4 hours or until the rasmali is soaked well.
  * finally, enjoy rasmalai slightly warmed or chilled.

### Nutrition
Calories: 93kcalCarbohydrates: 23gProtein: 1gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 1mgSodium: 5mgPotassium: 10mgFiber: 1gSugar: 22gVitamin A: 1IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 5mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make Rasmalai with step by step photo:

#### how to prepare chenna for rasmalai:
  1. firstly, get 2 litre to a boil stirring in between to prevent it from burning.  !
  2. add 2 tbsp vinegar and give stir. you will notice the milk starts to curdle.  !
  3. add 1 more tbsp of vinegar and stir until the milk curdles fully separating water.  !
  4. drain off the water over the cheesecloth. you can use any clean cloth here. rinse with cold water to remove sourness and stop cooking.  !
  5. squeeze the paneer gently and hang for 30 minutes.  !
  6. now take the moist paneer and crumble gently.  !
  7. using the palm, start to knead gently.  !
  8. knead until the paneer mixture turns smooth without any grains. do not over-knead here as the rasgulla will turn hard.  !
  9. pinch a small ball sized chenna and prepare smooth crack free balls, flatten slightly.  !
  10. keep the flattened paneer ball aside and cover with a moist cloth.  !

#### how to boil rasmalai in sugar syrup:
  1. firstly, in a large vessel, take 1¬Ω cup sugar, 3 pods cardamom and 7 cup water.  !
  2. stir and dissolve sugar.  !
  3. now boil the water for 5 minutes or until the syrup turns slightly sticky.  !
  4. drop in a prepared flattened paneer ball keeping the flame on high.  !
  5. cover and boil for 7 minutes or until the size of the ball doubles.  !
  6. chenna has been cooked well. keep aside.  !

### how to make rabdi:
  1. firstly, in a large kadai heat 1-litre milk, few saffron and pinch of saffron food colour.  !
  2. stir and get the milk to a boil.  !
  3. continue to cook until the milk thickens slightly.  !
  4. now add ¬Ω cup sugar and continue to boil.  !
  5. do not make very thick milk as it will be difficult for chenna to absorb milk.  !
  6. also, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and 2 tbsp nuts. mix well.  !

### how to soak rasmalai in rabdi:
  1. squeeze off the sugar syrup from the cooked paneer balls.  !
  2. place them in a tray and pour in prepared rabdi.  !
  3. rest for at least 4 hours or until the rasmali is soaked well.  !
  4. finally, enjoy **rasmalai** slightly warmed or chilled.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, the rasmalai stays good for 5-7 days when refrigerated.
  * also, use full cream cows milk for the best quality chenna.
  * additionally, the rabdi is slightly over-sweet as it should be absorbed by chenna.
  * finally, do not overcook the **rasmalai recipe** as it turns hard.

## recipe card for bengali chenna raabari recipe:
!

## mini rasgulla recipe | bengali chenna rasbari | angoor rasgulla
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy mini rasgulla recipe | bengali chenna rasbari | angoor rasgulla
5 from 223 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Resting Time 1 hour hr
Total Time 1 hour hr 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine bengali
Servings 50 pieces
Calories 24 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 litre milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 7¬Ω cup water

### Instructions

#### how to prepare chenna for rasgulla:
  * firstly, get 2 litre to a boil stirring in between to prevent from burning.
  * add 2 tbsp lemon juice and give a stir. you will notice the milk starts to curdle.
  * add 1 more tbsp of lemon juice and stir until the milk curdles fully separating water.
  * drain off the water over cheesecloth. you can use any clean cloth here.
  * rinse with cold water to remove sourness and stop cooking.
  * squeeze the paneer gently and hang for 1 hour.
  * now take the moist paneer and crumble gently.
  * using the palm, start to knead gently.
  * knead until the paneer mixture turns smooth without any grains. do not over-knead here as the rasgulla will turn hard.
  * pinch a small ball sized chenna and prepare smooth crack free balls.
  * keep the paneer ball aside and cover with a moist cloth.

#### how to boil rasgulla in sugar syrup:
  * firstly, in a large vessel, take 1¬Ω cup sugar, 2 pods cardamom and 7¬Ω cup water.
  * stir and dissolve sugar.
  * now boil the water for 5 minutes or until the syrup turns slightly sticky.
  * drop in prepared paneer ball keeping the flame on high.
  * cover and boil for 10 minutes or until the size of ball doubles.
  * drain off the rasgulla immediately into ice-cold water to prevent from losing its shape.
  * finally, enjoy rasgulla with sugar syrup.

### Nutrition
Calories: 24kcalCarbohydrates: 6gProtein: 1gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 1mgSodium: 2mgPotassium: 1mgFiber: 1gSugar: 6gVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 1mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make mini rasgulla with step by step photo:

### how to prepare chenna for rasgulla:
  1. firstly, get 2 litre to a boil stirring in between to prevent from burning. !
  2. add 2 tbsp lemon juice and give a stir. you will notice the milk starts to curdle. !
  3. add 1 more tbsp of lemon juice and stir until the milk curdles fully separating water. !
  4. drain off the water over cheesecloth. you can use any clean cloth here. !
  5. rinse with cold water to remove sourness and stop cooking. !
  6. squeeze the paneer gently and hang for 1 hour. !
  7. now take the moist paneer and crumble gently. !
  8. using the palm, start to knead gently. !
  9. knead until the paneer mixture turns smooth without any grains. do not over-knead here as the rasgulla will turn hard. !
  10. pinch a small ball sized chenna and prepare smooth crack free balls. !
  11. keep the paneer ball aside and cover with a moist cloth. !

### how to boil rasgulla in sugar syrup:
  1. firstly, in a large vessel, take 1¬Ω cup sugar, 2 pods cardamom and 7¬Ω cup water. !
  2. stir and dissolve sugar. !
  3. now boil the water for 5 minutes or until the syrup turns slightly sticky. !
  4. drop in prepared paneer ball keeping the flame on high. !
  5. cover and boil for 10 minutes or until the size of ball doubles. !
  6. drain off the rasgulla immediately into ice-cold water to prevent from losing its shape. !
  7. finally, enjoy **rasgulla** with sugar syrup. !

## notes:
  * firstly, the rasgulla stays good for 5-7 days when refrigerated.
  * also, use full cream cows milk for best quality paneer.
  * additionally, do not open the lid while rasgullas are boiling. when the temperature drops there is a high chance for rasgulla to fall flat.
  * finally, **mini rasgulla recipe** can be also converted to .

# Recipe 31
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/rosh-bora-recipe-rava-sweet-recipe/

### rosh bora video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for rava sweet recipe:
!

## rosh bora recipe | rava sweet recipe | bengali rasbora recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy rosh bora recipe | rava sweet recipe | bengali rasbora recipe
5 from 191 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Soaking Time 2 hours hrs
Total Time 2 hours hrs 40 minutes mins
Course Dessert
Cuisine Indian
Servings 12 pieces
Calories 216 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for rava mixture:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rava / semolina / suji, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup milk powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp baking soda

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp saffron food colour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup mix nuts powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp milk

#### for sugar syrup:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pod cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ few thread saffron / kesar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp rose water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp lemon juice

### Instructions

#### sugar syrup preparation:
  * firstly, in a large vessel take 2 cup sugar, 2 pod cardamom, few thread saffron and 2 cup water.
  * stir and dissolve sugar syrup completely.
  * boil for 5 minutes or until the sugar syrup turns slightly sticky.
  * now add 1 tsp rose water and 1 tsp lemon juice. lemon juice is added to prevent sugar syrup from crystalising.
  * mix well, cover and keep sugar syrup aside.

#### rava sweet preparation:
  * firstly, in a kadai heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 1 cup rava on low flame until it turns aromatic.
  * now add 1¬Ω cup milk and mix continuously.
  * keeping the flame on medium, keep stirring until the rava absorbs the milk.
  * the mixture will thicken and starts to separate from the pan.
  * cover and keep aside for 10 minutes.
  * after 10 minutes, transfer the mixture to a large bowl.
  * add ¬º cup milk powder, ¬º tsp cardamom powder and ¬º tsp baking soda.
  * squeeze and mix well until everything is well combined.
  * form a smooth and soft dough. if the mixture seems dry, add a tsp of milk and knead.
  * now take ¬º of the dough into a small bowl to prepare the stuffing.
  * add ¬º tsp saffron food colour, ¬º cup mix nuts powder and 1 tbsp milk.
  * mix well forming a smooth and soft stuffing dough. keep aside.
  * pinch a small ball sized rava mixture and prepare a smooth ball.
  * also prepare a small ball sized stuffing.
  * now stuff the stuffing ball into the rava mixture.
  * grease hands with ghee and prepare an oval-shaped or shape of your choice.
  * deep fry the sweet in medium hot ghee or oil.
  * keeping the flame on low, stir occasionally.
  * fry until the rava sweet turns golden brown. drain off.
  * transfer the fried doughnut into the hot sugar syrup.
  * make sure the sugar syrup is coated well. cover and rest for 2 hours.
  * finally, enjoy rava sweet or suji sweet or rosh bora hot or chilled.

### Nutrition
Calories: 216kcalCarbohydrates: 46gProtein: 4gFat: 2gSaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 7mgSodium: 52mgPotassium: 105mgFiber: 1gSugar: 36gVitamin A: 85IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 65mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make rosh bora with step by step photo:

### sugar syrup preparation:
  1. firstly, in a large vessel take 2 cup sugar, 2 pod cardamom, few thread saffron and 2 cup water. !
  2. stir and dissolve sugar syrup completely. !
  3. boil for 5 minutes or until the sugar syrup turns slightly sticky. !
  4. now add 1 tsp rose water and 1 tsp lemon juice.  lemon juice is added to prevent sugar syrup from crystalising. !
  5. mix well, cover and keep sugar syrup aside. !

### rava sweet preparation:
  1. firstly, in a kadai heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 1 cup rava on low flame until it turns aromatic. !
  2. now add 1¬Ω cup milk and mix continuously. !
  3. keeping the flame on medium, keep stirring until the rava absorbs the milk. !
  4. the mixture will thicken and starts to separate from the pan. !
  5. cover and keep aside for 10 minutes. !
  6. after 10 minutes, transfer the mixture to a large bowl. !
  7. add ¬º cup milk powder, ¬º tsp cardamom powder and ¬º tsp baking soda. !
  8. squeeze and mix well until everything is well combined. !
  9. form a smooth and soft dough. if the mixture seems dry, add a tsp of milk and knead. !
  10. now take ¬º of the dough into a small bowl to prepare the stuffing. !
  11. add ¬º tsp saffron food colour, ¬º cup mix nuts powder and 1 tbsp milk. i have used almonds and cashew nuts here. !
  12. mix well forming a smooth and soft stuffing dough. keep aside. !
  13. pinch a small ball sized rava mixture and prepare a smooth ball. !
  14. also prepare a small ball sized stuffing. !
  15. now stuff the stuffing ball into the rava mixture. !
  16. grease hands with ghee and prepare an oval-shaped or shape of your choice. !
  17. deep fry the sweet in medium hot ghee or oil. !
  18. keeping the flame on low, stir occasionally. !
  19. fry until the rava sweet turns golden brown. drain off. !
  20. transfer the fried doughnut into the hot sugar syrup. !
  21. make sure the sugar syrup is coated well. cover and rest for 2 hours. !
  22. finally, enjoy**rava sweet** or**suji sweet** or **rosh bora** hot or chilled. !

## notes:
  * firstly, if you do not have access to milk powder then replace it with maida.
  * also, stuffing is completely optional. however, it will enhance the taste.
  * additionally, fry on low flame else the doughnuts will remain raw from inside.
  * finally, **rava sweet** or**suji sweet** or**rosh bora** tastes great when served with ice cream.

# Recipe 33
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/brinjal-fry-recipe-brinjal-rava-fry/

### brinjal fry video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for brinjal rava fry recipe:
!

## brinjal fry recipe | brinjal rava fry | baingan rava fry | fried eggplant
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy brinjal fry recipe | brinjal rava fry | baingan rava fry | fried eggplant
4.96 from 22 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 20 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course Side Dish
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 10 pieces

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp kashmiri red chilli powder / lal mirch powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric / haldi
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch of hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 brinjal / baingan / eggplant, thickly sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for deep frying

#### for rava coating:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup rava / semolina / sooji
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kashmiri red chilli powder / lal mirch powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large mixing bowl take 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, pinch of hing, 2 tbsp rice flour and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * combine well making sure the spices are mixed.
  * now add 2 tbsp water and prepare a masala paste.
  * add in 1 brinjal thickly slices and coat with masala paste.
  * coat well and rest for 20 minutes.
  * meanwhile prepare rava mixture by mixing ¬º cup rava, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and ¬º tsp salt.
  * now coat the marinated baingan with rava on both sides.
  * shallow fry or pan fry in hot oil.
  * fry on low flame making sure to cook well.
  * now flip over and cook brinjal on both the sides. do not over cook as then brinjal will loose shape.
  * finally, serve brinjal fry recipe / brinjal rava fry as a side dish.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make brinjal fry with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large mixing bowl take 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, pinch of hing, 2 tbsp rice flour and ¬Ω tsp salt. !
  2. combine well making sure the spices are mixed. !
  3. now add 2 tbsp water and prepare a masala paste. !
  4. add in 1 brinjal thickly slices and coat with masala paste. !
  5. coat well and rest for 20 minutes. !
  6. meanwhile prepare rava mixture by mixing ¬º cup rava, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and ¬º tsp salt. !
  7. now coat the marinated baingan with rava on both sides. !
  8. shallow fry or pan fry in hot oil. !
  9. fry on low flame making sure to cook well. !
  10. now flip over and cook brinjal on both the sides. do not over cook as then brinjal will loose shape. !
  11. finally, serve **brinjal fry recipe** /**brinjal rava fry** as a side dish. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to slice brinjal uniformly, else they take different time to cook.
  * also fry on low flame, else brinjal will not get cooked from inside.
  * additionally, add rice flour or corn flour helps to get crispy brinjal fry.
  * finally, **brinjal fry recipe** /**brinjal rava fry** taste great when served hot.

## recipe card for dali toyi recipe:
!

## dali toyi recipe | dal tove recipe | dal recipe - konkani style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy dali toyi recipe | dal tove recipe | dal recipe - konkani style
5 from 15 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course dal
Cuisine goan
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for pressure cooking:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup toor dal, rinsed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup water

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp coconut oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli, broken
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a pressure cooker take ¬Ω cup toor dal, 2 chilli and 1 tsp oil.
  * pressure cook for 5 whistles adding 1¬Ω cup water.
  * now whisk the dal to smooth texture.
  * further add ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬º tsp hing and ¬Ω cup water.
  * mix well and get to a boil attaining a soupy consistency.
  * further in a small kadai heat 3 tsp coconut oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, few curry leaves, 2 dried red chilli.
  * pour the tempering over dal and also add 2 tbsp coriander. mix well.
  * finally, enjoy dal toye with hot steamed rice.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make dal tove with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a pressure cooker take ¬Ω cup toor dal, 2 chilli and 1 tsp oil. !
  2. pressure cook for 5 whistles adding 1¬Ω cup water. !
  3. now whisk the dal to smooth texture. !
  4. further add ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬º tsp hing and ¬Ω cup water. !
  5. mix well and get to a boil attaining a soupy consistency. !
  6. further in a small kadai heat 3 tsp coconut oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, few curry leaves, 2 dried red chilli. !
  7. pour the tempering over dal and also add 2 tbsp coriander. mix well. !
  8. finally, enjoy **dal toyi** with hot steamed rice. !

## notes:
  * firstly, adjust the consistency of dal by adding water as required. traditionally, it is prepared in a smooth soupy consistency.
  * also, you can blend the dal in a blender to get a more creamy texture.
  * additionally, turmeric is not added in this recipe. however, you can add if you are looking for a bright colour.
  * finally, **dal toyi recipe** thickens once cooled, so adjust the consistency as required.

# Recipe 35
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/eggless-omelette-tomato-omelette-besan-ka-cheela/

## eggless omelette | tomato omelette | besan ka cheela recipe card:
!

## eggless omelette | tomato omelette | besan ka cheela
HEBBARS KITCHEN
eggless omelette | tomato omelette | besan ka cheela
5 from 32 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course Main
Cuisine north indian
Servings 2 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup gram flour / besan
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 medium size tomato, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 medium size onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp red chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp oma / ajwain / carom seeds, optional
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp kasoori methi, optional
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ oil as required

### Instructions 
  * in a bowl and finely chopped onions, tomato, coriander leaves and chilli.
  * now add 1 cup of besan and ¬º cup of rice flour to the same bowl.
  * add red chilli powder, coriander powder, cumin seeds, ajwain, kasoori methi and salt to taste.
  * cautiously add water bit by bit so that no lumps are formed. mixing water to besan can easily form lumps. you need to avoid it.
  * heat a tawa or non-stick pan. grease it with few drops of oil or butter.
  * pour and spread a ladle of batter on tawa to form a round dosa. spread some oil on top of the dosa.
  * cover the omelette with a lid and let it cook.
  * once cooked in one side, flip over and cook on the other side.
  * both the side should be cooked and should be crisp.
  * your tomato omelette is ready and serve it with coconut chutney or any other chutney recipes.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## eggless omelette | tomato omelette | besan ka cheela step by step photo recipe:
  1. in a bowl and finely chopped onions, tomato, coriander leaves and chilli.  !
  2. now add 1 cup of besan and ¬º cup of rice flour to the same bowl.  !
  3. add red chilli powder, coriander powder, cumin seeds, ajwain, kasoori methi and salt to taste.  !
  4. cautiously add water bit by bit so that no lumps are formed. mixing water to besan can easily form lumps. you need to avoid it.  !
  5. heat a tawa or non-stick pan. grease it with few drops of oil or butter.
  6. pour and spread a ladle of batter on tawa to form a round dosa. spread some oil on top of the dosa.  !
  7. cover the omelette with a lid and let it cook.  !
  8. once cooked in one side, flip over and cook on the other side.  !
  9. both the side should be cooked and should be crisp.
  10. your tomato omelette is ready and serve it with **** or any other ****.  !

## notes
  * do not forget to ajwain or carom seeds. this will help in digestion.
  * you can add grated carrot as an extra toppings.

# Recipe 36

### sol kadhi recipe | kokum curry video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for sol kadhi or kokum curry recipe:
!

## sol kadhi recipe | kokum curry recipe | kokum kadhi recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy sol kadhi recipe | kokum curry recipe | kokum kadhi recipe
5 from 15 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 30 minutes mins
Cook Time 5 minutes mins
Total Time 35 minutes mins
Course beverages, rasam
Cuisine goan
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 8 kokum / kokam / punarpuli, fresh / dried
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cups water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin seeds / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 curry leaves / kadi patta
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cloves garlic, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup coconut milk, thick
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp crushed pepper, optional
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a bowl soak kokam in hot water for atleast 30 minutes.
  * further, squeeze the juice from kokam and keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat oil and add cumin seeds.
  * further add curry leaves, garlic and green chilli. saute well.
  * now add squeezed kokam juice discarding the pulp.
  * get kokam juice to a boil.
  * further add coconut milk. make sure to keep flame on low-medium else coconut milk might curdle.
  * stir well and add salt.
  * also get to a boil and give a good stir.
  * furthermore, simmer the curry for a minute or two.
  * then add chopped coriander leaves.
  * also add crushed pepper to enhance the flavour. however pepper is optional.
  * finally, serve sol kadi with plain rice or drink it plain.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make sol kadhi or kokum curry with step by step photo recipe:
  1. firstly, in a bowl soak kokam in hot water for atleast 30 minutes.  !
  2. further, squeeze the juice from kokam and keep aside.  !
  3. in a large kadai heat oil and add cumin seeds.  !
  4. further add curry leaves, garlic and green chilli. saute well.  !
  5. now add squeezed kokam juice discarding the pulp.  !
  6. get kokam juice to a boil.
  7. further add coconut milk. make sure to keep flame on low-medium else coconut milk might curdle.  !
  8. stir well and add salt.  !
  9. also get to a boil and give a good stir.  !
  10. furthermore, simmer the curry for a minute or two.  !
  11. then add chopped coriander leaves.  !
  12. also add crushed pepper to enhance the flavour. however pepper is optional.  !
  13. finally, serve sol kadhi with plain rice or drink it plain.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, using hot water to soak kokum helps to release juice quickly.
  * furthermore, as a variation, skip the boiling step and just mix kokum juice and coconut milk along with some garlic and green chilli.
  * also, add garlic and green chilli while extracting milk from coconut.
  * finally, do not boil sol kadhi too much as they might curdle.

# Recipe 37
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/jalebi-recipe-instant-crispy-jalebi/

### instant jalebi recipe | homemade crispy jalebi video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for instant jalebi recipe | homemade crispy jalebi:
!

## instant jalebi recipe | homemade crispy jalebi recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy instant jalebi recipe | homemade crispy jalebi recipe
4.99 from 219 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course sweets
Cuisine Indian
Servings 10 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for jalebi batter:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup all purpose flour / maida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp corn flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp baking soda
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp yogurt / curd
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 tbsp water, or as required
  * ‚ñ¢ ‚Öõ tsp turmeric powder / haldi / yellow food colour, optional

#### for sugar syrup:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp saffron strands / kesar, optional
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder / elachi powder

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for deep frying

### Instructions 
  * in a mixing bowl, mix maida, corn flour, curd.
  * then add half tsp vinegar and water.
  * mix well in round circular directions for 4 minutes.
  * now add baking soda and give a gentle mix.
  * now pour this batter in the tomato ketchup bottles carefully.
  * heat oil in a pan and add 1 tbsp of ghee.
  * squeeze the bottle and make round spirals with the batter.
  * when one side is partly cooked, turn over and fry the other side.
  * fry till the jalebis are a light golden.
  * then immediately drop the fried jalebis in the warm sugar syrup for 30 seconds (1 string consistency).
  * finally, serve jalebis hot, warm or at room temperature.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## instant jalebi recipe | homemade crispy jalebi step by step photo recipe:

### preparing sugar syrup:
  1. firstly, take 1 cup sugar in a pan and add ¬º cup water.  !
  2. keep stirring on low flame, so that the sugar dissolves. !
  3. boil the sugar syrup and add saffron.  !
  4. cook till you get one string consistency in the sugar syrup.  !
  5. once one string consistency is attained, switch off the flame and add ¬Ω tsp lemon juice and cardamom powder. lemon helps to avoid crystallizing sugar syrup and keeps your jalebis crispy.  !

### **preparing jalebi batter:**
  1. firstly, in a mixing bowl, take ¬Ω cup all purpose flour or maida, 1 tsp corn flour, 1 tsp curd and 1/8th tsp of food colour.  !
  2. mix all the above ingredients with a spoon.  !
  3. then add half tsp vinegar and 5 ‚Äì 6 tsp water. the amount of water to be added slowly and as required.  !
  4. whisk well in round circular directions for 5 minutes. this adds volume to the batter and makes it even and smooth.  !
  5. now add ¬º tsp of baking soda and give a gentle mix.  !
  6. further small bubbles appear on the top. stir the batter lightly and it should have a flowing consistency.  !
  7. now pour this batter in the tomato ketchup bottles carefully.  !

### **frying jalebis:**
  1. firstly, heat oil in a pan and add 1 tbsp of ghee. ghee gives a better flavour. make sure your pan is not too shallow and should be approximately 1 inch deep for frying jalebis.  !
  2. now squeeze the bottle and make round spirals with the batter.  !
  3. furthermore, when one side is partly cooked, turn over and fry the other side.  !
  4. also fry till the jalebis are a light golden. remove with a tongs and shake to drain the extra oil.  !
  5. then immediately drop the fried jalebis in the warm sugar syrup.  !
  6. dip and turn over so that both sides are coated with the syrup.  !
  7. remove and shake lightly and place them in a plate.  !
  8. finally, serve **jalebi****recipe** hot, warm or at room temperature. store the leftovers jalebi in an airtight container and refrigerated.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, to get rich yellow colour to your jalebis, add yellow food colour. however it is optional.
  * in addition, make sure your pan is not too shallow and should be approximately 1 inch deep for frying jalebis.
  * furthermore, don‚Äôt worry if you won‚Äôt get perfect shapes in first attempt as the jalebis keep on moving while you make the circles. you need to be quick and this does require some practice.
  * finally, if you like your **jalebi recipe** too sweety then keep in sugar syrup for about 2 to 3 minutes.

# Recipe 38
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/tomato-saar-recipe-tomato-curry-recipe/

### tomato saar video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for tomato curry for rice:
!

## tomato saar recipe | tomato curry for rice | konkani style tomato saar
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy tomato saar recipe | tomato curry for rice | konkani style tomato saar
5 from 28 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course rasam
Cuisine goan
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for masala paste:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω tomato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup coconut, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 dried red chilli, deseed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 clove garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ small piece tamarind
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water

#### !for saar / konkan curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp coconut oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp jaggery / gud
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 piece kokum / punarpuli / muragalu / kaatampi / bhirand / aamsul
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, slit

### Instructions 
  * firstly, prepare masala paste by blending masala paste ingredients.
  * in a large kadai heat 1 tbsp coconut oil.
  * now add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, pinch hing, 1 dried red chilli and few curry leaves.
  * saute and splutter tempering.
  * further add ¬Ω onion and saute till they shrink slightly.
  * add in prepared masala paste and saute for a minute.
  * pour 3 cup water or use coconut milk for more flavours.
  * also add 1 tsp salt, ¬º tsp jaggery, 5 piece kokum and 1 chilli. mix well.
  * simmer and boil for 10 minutes or till raw flavour disappears.
  * also the oil floats on top, indicating tomato saar is cooked completely.
  * finally, serve tomato saar / konkan style tomato curry with hot steamed rice.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make tomato saar recipe with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, to prepare masala paste take 1¬Ω tomato in a blender. !
  2. also add ¬æ cup coconut, 2 tsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin, ¬º tsp pepper, ¬º tsp turmeric and 4 dried red chilli. !
  3. additionally add ¬º onion, 2 clove garlic, ¬Ω inch ginger and small piece tamarind. !
  4. blend to smooth paste adding ¬Ω cup water. keep aside. !
  5. in a large kadai heat 1 tbsp coconut oil. alternatively use any cooking oil. !
  6. now add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, pinch hing, 1 dried red chilli and few curry leaves. !
  7. saute and splutter tempering. !
  8. further add ¬Ω onion and saute till they shrink slightly. !
  9. add in prepared masala paste and saute for a minute. !
  10. pour 3 cup water or use coconut milk for more flavours. !
  11. also add 1 tsp salt, ¬º tsp jaggery, 5 piece kokum and 1 chilli. mix well. !
  12. simmer and boil for 10 minutes or till raw flavour disappears. !
  13. also the oil floats on top, indicating tomato saar is cooked completely. !
  14. finally, serve **tomato saar / konkan style tomato curry** with hot steamed rice. !

## notes:
  * firstly, use well ripened tomatoes for great flavour and colour.
  * also recommend to deseed the red chilli to avoid spiciness.
  * furthermore, adding tamarind is optional as kokum gives sourness.
  * finally, **tomato saar / konkan style tomato curry** tastes great when made with coconut oil.
