# Recipe 39
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/badam-burfi-recipe-almond-badam-katli/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Badam Burfi
An excellent and tasty Indian sweet recipe made with a combination of powdered almond and desiccated coconut in a one-string sugar syrup. **Badam Burfi,** known as Badam Katli, is an ideal festival recipe for offering Prasadam to beloved gods. It can also be a perfect sweet snack and be served and exchanged with friends and family. In addition, it is also considered a healthy alternative compared to other dry fruits and sweets, significant because of Almonds.
There are many different ways to make this classical **Badam Burfi Recipe**. The variations mainly differ from the supporting ingredients added to this classical dessert. The typical combination is coconut, but it is not limited. It can take other dry fruit powders like cashews, pasta, and dates. Adding these makes it richer and premium, with just badam powder. In addition, adding rava, besan, and even wheat powder can give it a crunchy texture.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Badam Burfi
!

## Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi with Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi Recipe | Badam Katli Recipe**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 1 hour hr
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 15 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 20 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup badam / almonds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp saffron milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cardamom / elachi, powdered
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak almonds in hot water for 1 hour.
  * now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.
  * also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.
  * transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.
  * meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.
  * keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.
  * boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.
  * now add the prepared almond powder, saffron milk and cardamom powder.
  * mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.
  * continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan.
  * transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.
  * and allow to cool for 5 minutes.
  * grease your hand with little ghee and knead for a minute.
  * once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin,.
  * furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.
  * you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  * finally, serve badam burfi / badam katli on diwali or any festival.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Badam Burfi with Step-by-step Photos

### badam powder or almond meal recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak ¬æ cup of almonds in 1 cup of hot water for 1 hour.  !
  2. now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.  !
  3. also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.  !
  4. transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.  !

### badam buri | almond barfi recipe:
  1. meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  2. keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.  !
  3. boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.  !
  4. now add the prepared almond powder.  !
  5. also add saffron milk. to prepare saffron milk, soak few strands of saffron in warm milk for 10 minutes.  !
  6. additionally add cardamom powder for more flavours.  !
  7. mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.  !
  8. once the mixture begins to boil, add a tbsp of . however, it is optional, but do add more flavour to burfi.  !
  9. continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan. if you prefer slightly hard burfi then continue to stir for longer time.  !
  10. transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.  !
  11. add a tsp of **** to make smooth dough.  !
  12. and allow to cool for 5 minutes. do not rest more, as they will turn hard and wont be able to give shape.  !
  13. grease your hand with little  and knead for a minute. be careful as the dough will be very hot. try to knead when its hot, else it will be difficult. and do not over knead as badam will start releasing oil.  !
  14. once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin, adjusting the thickness according to your choice.  !
  15. furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.  !
  16. you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  17. finally, serve **badam burfi / badam katli** on diwali or any festival. !

## Notes
  * firstly, soak the badam well or blanch it for easy removal of skin.
  * also, make sure to get just 1 string consistency of sugar syrup. else it turns burfi hard and brittle.
  * most noteworthy, use nonstick pan for easy and efficient badam katlis.
  * and entire badam burfi has to be prepared on low flame.
  * finally, instead of butter paper, you can also use a plastic sheet or greased plate to prepare **badam burfi.**

# Recipe 40

## About Gathiya Snack
It is a popular savory snack from Western Indian cuisine particularly from the Gujarati Cuisine. **Gathiya** or **Ganthiya snack** is known for its light and crispy texture but more importantly, the aroma and flavor of the ajwain or carrom seeds added to it. It is most commonly served as a tea-time snack but is not limited to it. It can also be served as a side dish to lunch and dinner and also as a topping to any desired curries.
There are many different variations of the **Gathiya snack** , but the most common way is to make it with besan flour. The addition or topping of other aromatic herbs and spices makes it unique and special. In addition, the shape of these adds different names and the way it is served. You may find Mota Gathiya (thick shape), Papdi Gathiya (thin & flat), Masala Gathiya (spicy version) and Nylon Gathia (thin shape).

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card For Bhavnagari Tikha Gathiya
!

## Gathiya Recipe | Bhavnagari Tikha Gathia Sev Recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Gathiya Recipe | Bhavnagari Tikha Gathia Sev Recipe
5 from 30 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 35 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine gujarat
Servings 1 box
Calories 1944 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp baking soda
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ajwain / carom seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp crushed pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp water
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a mixer jar take ¬Ω cup oil, ¬Ω cup water, ¬Ω tsp baking soda and 1 tsp salt.
  * Blend till the mixture turns creamy consistency. Keep aside.
  * In a large plate, sieve 2 cup besan, ¬Ω tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp crushed pepper and pinch hing. Mix well.
  * Now add the prepared oil-water mixture and knead the dough.
  * Knead well making sure the dough is well combined and soft.
  * Further, add 2 tbsp water and start to knead again.
  * Knead until the dough changes colour slightly and turns soft.
  * Take the flower mould and fix it to chakli maker.
  * Stuff the dough into the chakli maker and press into hot oil.
  * Stir occasionally, until the sev turns crispy.
  * Drain off to remove excess oil.
  * Finally, enjoy Crispy Gathiya for a month when stored in an airtight container.

### Nutrition
Calories: 1944kcalCarbohydrates: 141gProtein: 54gFat: 130gSaturated Fat: 11gPolyunsaturated Fat: 39gMonounsaturated Fat: 75gTrans Fat: 0.4gSodium: 3035mgPotassium: 2031mgFiber: 27gSugar: 27gVitamin A: 98IUCalcium: 118mgIron: 12mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Gathiya Recipe with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a mixer jar take ¬Ω cup oil, ¬Ω cup water, ¬Ω tsp baking soda and 1 tsp salt.  !
  2. Blend till the mixture turns creamy consistency. Keep aside.  !
  3. In a large plate, sieve 2 cup besan, ¬Ω tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp crushed pepper and pinch hing. Mix well.  !
  4. Now add the prepared oil-water mixture and knead the dough.  !
  5. Knead well making sure the dough is well combined and soft.  !
  6. Further, add 2 tbsp water and start to knead again.  !
  7. Knead until the dough changes colour slightly and turns soft.  !
  8. Take the flower mould and fix it to chakli maker.  !
  9. Stuff the dough into the chakli maker and press into hot oil.  !
  10. Stir occasionally, until the sev turns crispy.  !
  11. Drain off to remove excess oil.  !
  12. Finally, enjoy **Crispy Gathiya** for a month when stored in an airtight container.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to blend oil, water and soda into the blender. This helps the sev to be soft from the inside and crispy from the outside.
  * Also, using fresh oil helps keep the gathiya fresh for longer.
  * Additionally, you can use the mould of your choice.
  * Finally, **Crispy Gathiya recipe** tastes great for evening snacks.

## Recipe Card for Pudla Besan Chilla

## Pudla Recipe | Pudala Besan Chilla | Savory Pancake
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy **Pudla Recipe | Pudala Besan Chilla | Savory Pancake**
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine gujarat
Servings 8 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for batter
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω capsicum, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tomato, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup paneer, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, pinch hing, ¬Ω tsp ajwain and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.
  * Add 1 cup water and mix using a whisk.
  * Prepare a smooth batter and mix continuously for 5 minutes.
  * Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω capsicum, ¬Ω tomato, ¬Ω cup paneer, 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp coriander and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Rest for 10 minutes, or until the besan are absorbed well.
  * Now heat the pan, and pour the batter. spread gently making sure the chilla is as thin as possible.
  * Spread half tsp oil.
  * Cook on medium flame making sure the base is cooked well.
  * Flip over and roast both sides.
  * Finally, enjoy Besan Pudla Recipe with chutney and raita.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Pudla with step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, pinch hing, ¬Ω tsp ajwain and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.  !
  3. Add 1 cup water and mix using a whisk.  !
  4. Prepare a smooth batter and mix continuously for 5 minutes.  !
  5. Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω capsicum, ¬Ω tomato, ¬Ω cup paneer, 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp coriander and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste.  !
  6. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  7. Rest for 10 to 15 minutes, or until the besan is absorbed well.  !
  8. Now heat the pan, and pour the batter. spread gently making sure the chilla is as thin as possible.  !
  9. Spread half tsp oil.  !
  10. Cook on medium flame making sure the base is cooked well.  !
  11. Flip over and roast both sides.  !
  12. Finally, enjoy **Besan Pudla Recipe** with chutney and raita.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, grate the paneer and add it to the batter to soften the chilla and increase the protein content.
  * Also, roast both sides to get crispy and soft from the inside.
  * Additionally, beating the batter well makes the besan light and not dense.
  * Finally, **Besan Pudla Recipe** tastes great when served with spicy chutney.

## Recipe Card for 7 Seed Mukhwas
!

## Mukhwas Recipe | Homemade Mouth Freshener & Digestive Aid
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Mukhwas Recipe | Homemade Mouth Freshener & Digestive Aid
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 25 minutes mins
Soaking Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr
Course Condiments
Cuisine gujarati
Servings 1 Box
Calories 1.171 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup white sesame seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup black sesame seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup fennel seeds / saunf
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup pumpkin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup sunflower seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup flaxseeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup chia seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ajwain / carom seeds

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 2 tbsp lemon juice, 2 tbsp water, 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Further add ¬º cup white sesame seeds, ¬º cup black sesame seeds, ¬º cup fennel seeds, ¬º cup pumpkin seeds, ¬º cup sunflower seeds, ¬º cup flaxseeds and ¬º cup chia seeds.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Allow the seeds to soak for 30 minutes so that the seeds turn moist from the inside.
  * After 30 minutes, the water was well absorbed by the seeds.
  * Transfer the soaked seeds to the heavy pan and roast on low flame.
  * Continue to roast on low flame until the seeds turn dry.
  * Once the seeds are almost dried, add ¬Ω tsp ajwain.
  * Continue to roast until the seeds turn crunchy and dry off completely.
  * Cool the seeds and transfer them to the airtight container.
  * Finally, enjoy Mukhwas Recipe for a month.

### Nutrition
Calories: 1.171kcalCarbohydrates: 60gProtein: 40gFat: 94gSaturated Fat: 11gPolyunsaturated Fat: 50gMonounsaturated Fat: 27gTrans Fat: 0.1gSodium: 2.36mgPotassium: 1.293mgFiber: 40gSugar: 3gVitamin A: 51IUVitamin C: 14mgCalcium: 1.148mgIron: 21mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Mukhwas with step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 2 tbsp lemon juice, 2 tbsp water, 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Further add ¬º cup white sesame seeds, ¬º cup black sesame seeds, ¬º cup fennel seeds, ¬º cup pumpkin seeds, ¬º cup sunflower seeds, ¬º cup flaxseeds and ¬º cup chia seeds.  !
  4. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  5. Allow the seeds to soak for 30 minutes so that the seeds turn moist from the inside.  !
  6. After 30 minutes, the water was well absorbed by the seeds.  !
  7. Transfer the soaked seeds to the heavy pan and roast on low flame.  !
  8. Continue to roast on low flame until the seeds turn dry.  !
  9. Once the seeds are almost dried, add ¬Ω tsp ajwain.  !
  10. Continue to roast until the seeds turn crunchy and dry off completely.  !
  11. Cool the seeds and transfer them to the airtight container.  !
  12. Finally, enjoy **Mukhwas Recipe** for a month.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, you can use the seeds of your choice to make the mukhwas nutritious.
  * Also, if you are doing it in large quantities, soak the seeds separately as each seed differs in roasting time.
  * Additonally, do not keep under sunlight as the seeds will fade. Make sure to keep it in a dry place.
  * Finally, **Mukhwas Recipe** can be eaten at any time as they have the ability to aid digestion.

# Recipe 43
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/badam-pak-recipe-gujarati-almond-fudge/

### Video Recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

## Recipe Card for Badam Pak
!

## Badam Pak Recipe | Gujarati Almond Fudge
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Badam Pak Recipe | Gujarati Almond Fudge
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 45 minutes mins
Total Time 55 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine gujarat
Servings 16 Servings
Calories 147 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup badam / almond
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp gond / edible gum
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sunflower seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp dry coconut, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ badam powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup milk powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch saffron food colour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp poppy seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kesar / saffron
  * ‚ñ¢ badam / almonds, chopped

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a mixer jar take 1 cup badam and grind to coarse powder. Keep aside.
  * In a pan heat ¬º cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond.
  * Fry the gond till they puff up and turn crystal.
  * Drain the gond and crunch them in a plate.
  * Now in the same ghee, fry 2 tbsp sunflower seeds and 2 tbsp dry coconut.
  * Transfer them to the plate and keep them aside.
  * Heat ¬º cup ghee and add prepared badam powder and roast well.
  * Roast until the badam powder turns aromatic and changes colour slightly.
  * Add in ¬æ cup milk powder and roast until the mixture turns aromatic. Instead of milk powder, you can use khova.
  * transfer the roasted badam and milk powder onto the plate and mix well. Keep aside.
  * In a large kadai take 1 cup jaggery and ¬Ω cup water.
  * Stir and dissolve the jaggery. Continue to boil until the jaggery syrup attains 1 string consistency.
  * Add in pinch of saffron food colour, 2 tbsp poppy seeds and mix well.
  * Further add roasted badam mixture, ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and ¬Ω tsp kesar.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Transfer the burfi mixture to the tray lined with baking paper.
  * Top with 2 tbsp almonds and press gently.
  * Rest the pak for 1 hour to set well. Now cut into pieces and enjoy.
  * Finally, Badam Pak Recipe is ready to enjoy for a month.

### Nutrition
Calories: 147kcalCarbohydrates: 16gProtein: 2gFat: 9gSaturated Fat: 5gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gCholesterol: 20mgSodium: 23mgPotassium: 99mgFiber: 0.4gSugar: 15gVitamin A: 57IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 77mgIron: 0.3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Badam Pak with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, in a mixer jar take 1 cup badam and grind to coarse powder. Keep aside.  !
  2. In a pan heat ¬º cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond.  !
  3. Fry the gond till they puff up and turn crystal.  !
  4. Drain the gond and crunch them in a plate. !
  5. Now in the same ghee, fry 2 tbsp sunflower seeds and 2 tbsp dry coconut.  !
  6. Transfer them to the plate and keep them aside.  !
  7. Heat ¬º cup ghee and add prepared badam powder and roast well.  !
  8. Roast until the badam powder turns aromatic and changes colour slightly.  !
  9. Add in ¬æ cup milk powder and roast until the mixture turns aromatic. Instead of milk powder, you can use khova.  !
  10. transfer the roasted badam and milk powder onto the plate and mix well. Keep aside.  !
  11. In a large kadai take 1 cup jaggery and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  12. Stir and dissolve the jaggery. Continue to boil until the jaggery syrup attains 1 string consistency.  !
  13. Add in pinch of saffron food colour, 2 tbsp poppy seeds and mix well.  !
  14. Further add roasted badam mixture, ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and ¬Ω tsp kesar.  !
  15. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  16. Transfer the burfi mixture to the tray lined with baking paper.  !
  17. Top with 2 tbsp almonds and press gently.  !
  18. Rest the pak for 1 hour to set well. Now cut into pieces and enjoy.  !
  19. Finally, **Badam Pak Recipe** is ready to enjoy for a month.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, instead of milk powder, you can use mava or khova for rich milk flavour.
  * Also, you can add chopped almonds in the pak to get crunchy bites.
  * Additionally, roasting with ghee will increase the flavour and also increase the health benefits.
  * Finally, **Badam Pak Recipe** tastes great when gond is added as it adds crunch.

# Recipe 44
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/sabudana-khichdi-recipe-sago-ki-khichdi/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Sabudana Khichdi
It is a popular and healthy dish from Indian cuisine made with tapioca pearls, potatoes, herbs, and spices. **Sabudana Khichdi** is known for its fast energy boost and hence it is typically served as a meal replacement during festival fasting seasons. In addition, it is also most commonly served as breakfast or even a tiffin box meal. The recipe is extremely simple and easy to prepare but can take some practice to make a nonstick and nonmushy khichdi.
There are many different ways to make this simple **Sabudana ki khichadi,** which mainly varies with the region it is prepared. The most common and basic way to prepare for this khichdi is by using the soaked sago pearls and boiled potatoes tossed with spices and herbs. The other easy way is to make it via soup which is most commonly known as liquid soup. The soaked tapioca pearls can also be made like upma which is known as Sabudana Upma.

## Tips for Sabudana Khichdi
The recipe is super simple to make this recipe with very less and basic ingredients used to make this khichdi recipe. Yet basic tips to make this perfect are ‚Äì
  1. **Proper Sabudana ‚Äì** Choosing the right sized and best quality of Sabudana or sago pearls is essential to any Sabudana Recipe. Typically small to medium-sized sago pearls are best for this recipe.
  2. **Soaking ‚Äì** The water to Sabudana ratio while soaking is very critical. I generally follow a 1:3/4 ratio of Sabudana and water, but you can increase it depending on the quality of Sabudana used. Also, rinse and wash the Sabudana thoroughly till all excess starch is removed.
  3. **Potatoes ‚Äì** Generally pressured cooked/boiled and diced potatoes are just added to the khichdi. This helps to hasten the cooking process. But you may add directly to the cooking pan or even microwave them before using it.
  4. **Cooking Time ‚Äì** The cooking can be an overwhelming process as it has to be cooked on low to medium flame. Keep patience and stir gently so that it does not damage the sago pearls.
  5. **Experiment ‚Äì** The recipe is mainly prepared during the fasting season with fasting ingredients. However, it is not limited to it. It can be extended to other ingredients like coconut, curry leaves, onions, etc.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card Sabudana Ki Khichadi:
!

## Sabudana Khichdi Recipe | 6 Tips For NonSticky Sabudana Ki Khichadi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Sabudana khichdi recipe | 6 tips to make perfect nonsticky Sabudana ki khichadi
5 from 3 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Soaking Time 6 hours hrs
Total Time 6 hours hrs 15 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine maharashtra
Servings 2 Servings
Calories 385 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sabudana
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup peanut
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 potato, boiled & cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, to soak the sabudana, take 1 cup sabudana in a bowl and rinse with water.
  * make sure to rub the sabudana to remove excess starch.
  * rinse the sabudana twice and add ¬æ cup water.
  * dip the sago completely, and rest for 6 hours. soaking time varies on the quality of sabudana.
  * once the sabudana is soaked well, make sure to check there is no water at the bottom. else the khichdi will turn mushy.
  * the sabudana must be able to mash easily when pressed between fingers. if it is still hard, then sprinkle some water and soak for 30 more minutes.
  * now in a heavy-bottomed pan roast ¬Ω cup peanut.
  * roast on low flame until the peanuts turn crunchy.
  * cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.
  * pulse and powder to a coarse peanut powder.
  * add the peanut powder to the soaked sabudana. adding peanut powder will help to absorb any excess moisture if present.
  * also, add 1 tsp sugar and ¬æ tsp salt. mix well combining everything well. keep aside.
  * now in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. splutter 1 tsp cumin and few curry leaves.
  * add 1 inch ginger, 2 chilli and 1 potato.
  * fry until the potato turn slightly golden brown.
  * further, add sabudana peanut mixture and mix gently.
  * make sure to mix by scarping the pan. this helps to prevent any sabudana from sticking.
  * also, be very gentle else there are chances for sabudana to be mashed out.
  * cook until the sago pearls turn translucent.
  * now add ¬Ω lemon and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well.
  * finally, enjoy sabudana khichdi or pack to your lunch box.

### Nutrition
Calories: 385kcalCarbohydrates: 16gProtein: 11gFat: 34gSaturated Fat: 12gPolyunsaturated Fat: 7gMonounsaturated Fat: 13gCholesterol: 38mgSodium: 896mgPotassium: 576mgFiber: 5gSugar: 5gVitamin A: 564IUVitamin C: 91mgCalcium: 90mgIron: 4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Sabudana Khichdi with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, to soak the Sabudana, take 1 cup of Sabudana in a bowl and rinse with water. !
  2. Make sure to rub the Sabudana to remove excess starch. !
  3. Rinse the Sabudana twice and add ¬æ cup water. !
  4. Dip the sago completely, and rest for 6 hours. Soaking time varies on the quality of Sabudana. !
  5. Once the Sabudana is soaked well, ensure there is no water at the bottom. Else the khichdi will turn mushy. !
  6. The Sabudana must be able to mash easily when pressed between fingers. If it is still hard, then sprinkle some water and soak for 30 more minutes. !
  7. Now in a heavy-bottomed pan roast ¬Ω cup peanut. !
  8. Roast on low flame until the peanuts turn crunchy. !
  9. Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar. !
  10. Pulse and powder to a coarse peanut powder. !
  11. Add the peanut powder to the soaked Sabudana. Adding peanut powder will help to absorb any excess moisture if present. !
  12. Also, add 1 tsp sugar and ¬æ tsp salt. Mix well combining everything well. Keep aside. !
  13. Now in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. Splutter 1 tsp cumin and a few curry leaves. !
  14. Add 1-inch ginger, 2 chili, and 1 potato. !
  15. Fry until the potato turns slightly golden brown. !
  16. Furthermore, add Sabudana peanut mixture and mix gently. !
  17. Make sure to mix by scraping the pan. this helps to prevent any Sabudana from sticking. !
  18. Also, be very gentle else there are chances for Sabudana to be mashed out. !
  19. Cook until the sago pearls turn translucent. !
  20. Now add ¬Ω lemon and 2 tbsp coriander. Mix well. !
  21. Finally, enjoy**Sabudana khichdi** or pack in your lunch box. !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to rinse the Sabudana really well else the khichadi may turn sticky.
  * Also, if you are not eating curry leaves during vrat then you can skip it.
  * Additionally, the soaking time of Sabudana completely depends on the quality of the Sabudana. so when you are making it for the first time keep an eye on it.
  * Finally, the **Sabudana khichdi recipe** tastes great when prepared with desi ghee.

# Recipe 45
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-nylon-khaman-dhokla-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Nylon Khaman Dhokla:
It is basically a soft and spongy instant dhokla recipe prepared with chickpea flour or besan atta with herbs & spices seasonings. In other words, **Nylon Khaman Dhokla** is an instant or easy cheat version of the traditional dhokla recipe without the hassle of fermentation and overnight preparation. It is super popular for its softness and sponginess which is mainly achieved by the combination of eno powder and citric acid. Thus making a super easy breakfast or snack meal option for any age group.
Gujarati Cuisine Snacks are known for their simplicity and easiness of preparation without the use of any complex ingredients. The **Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe** is not different from it and can be made within 30 minutes. This recipe is instant and more importantly does not require any additional preparation and fermentation. Hence the recipe can be an ideal breakfast or snack meal for any time and any age group. Moreover, it is served as it is without any additional side. But when served with spicy green chutney and Imli chutney, the combination is just lip-smacking.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Instant Gujarati Nylon Dhokla:
!

## Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe | Instant Gujarati Nylon Dhokla
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe | Instant Gujarati Nylon Dhokla
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Soaking Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 50 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine gujarat
Servings 15 pieces
Calories 124 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp eno fruit salt

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 chilli, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt

#### for garnishing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coconut, grated

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬º cup sugar and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Now add 1 cup water and mix well using a whisk.
  * Add water as required and whisk for 5 minutes.
  * Prepare a fluffy and light batter.
  * Cover and rest for 15 minutes.
  * Now add 2 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tbsp oil.
  * Continue to whisk for 5 more minutes to get a fluffy batter.
  * Further, add 1 tsp eno fruit salt and 2 tbsp water.
  * Mix gently until the batter turns frothy.
  * Transfer the batter immediately to the greased tray.
  * Place in a steamer and steam for 20 minutes.
  * Now cut the dhokla into pieces.
  * To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, 5 chilli, a few curry leaves, pinch hing, and splutter the tempering.
  * Further add ¬Ω cup water, 2 tbsp sugar, and ¬º tsp salt.
  * Mix and boil for 2 minutes, making sure everything is well combined.
  * Pour the tempering over the dhokla and rest for 20 minutes so that the dhokla absorbs all the water.
  * Before serving, top with 2 tbsp coriander and 2 tbsp coconut.
  * Finally, enjoy Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe with green chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 124kcalCarbohydrates: 16gProtein: 4gFat: 5gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 2gMonounsaturated Fat: 3gTrans Fat: 0.01gSodium: 133mgPotassium: 201mgFiber: 2gSugar: 8gVitamin A: 165IUVitamin C: 24mgCalcium: 14mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Nylon Khaman Dhokla with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cups of besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬º cup sugar, and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Now add 1 cup water and mix well using a whisk.  !
  4. Add water as required and whisk for 5 minutes.  !
  5. Prepare a fluffy and light batter.  !
  6. Cover and rest for 15 minutes.  !
  7. Now add 2 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tbsp oil.  !
  8. Continue to whisk for 5 more minutes to get a fluffy batter.  !
  9. Further, add 1 tsp of eno fruit salt and 2 tbsp water.  !
  10. Mix gently until the batter turns frothy.  !
  11. Transfer the batter immediately to the greased tray.  !
  12. Place in a steamer and steam for 20 minutes.  !
  13. Now cut the dhokla into pieces.  !
  14. To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, 5 chilli, a few curry leaves, pinch hing, and splutter the tempering.  !
  15. Further add ¬Ω cup water, 2 tbsp sugar, and ¬º tsp salt.  !
  16. Mix and boil for 2 minutes, making sure everything is well combined. Pour the tempering over the dhokla and rest for 20 minutes so that the dhokla absorbs all the water.  !
  17. Before serving, top with 2 tbsp coriander and 2 tbsp coconut.  !
  18. Finally, enjoy the **Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe** with green chutney.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to add water slowly, as the consistency of the batter is very important.
  * Also, after adding Eno fruit salt, steam the batter immediately, or else the dhokla will not be soft and fluffy.
  * Additionally, instead of lemon juice, you can use citric acid. And in place of eno fruit salt add baking soda.
  * Finally, **Nylon Khaman Dhokla Recipe** has to be steamed well, or else the dhokla will remain raw in the center.

# Recipe 46
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/gujarati-sukhdi-recipe-gond-pak-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Sukhdi or Gond Pak:
It is basically a simple sweet dessert snack recipe made with just 3 ingredients i.e. wheat, jaggery, and ghee. However, this **sukhdi recipe** is slightly extended with a few more additional ingredients like gond, cardamom and also cashews, and almonds. This is typically made in Gujarati cuisine and is typically served for auspicious occasions and festivals. Also compared to other premium dry sweets, it is much simpler to make due to the minimal set of ingredients used in it.
The main selling point of this **gond pak recipe** is its texture. Due to the use of roasted wheat flour mixed with melted jaggery and hot ghee, it gains a crispy or crunchy texture. In addition, when gond  are mixed, it elevates the taste and eating experience. In addition, some variations also include a generous topping of finely chopped dry fruits making it more attractive.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Gond Pak:
!

## Sukhdi Recipe | Gond Pak Recipe | Gujarati Gond Gur Papdi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Sukhdi Recipe | Gond Pak Recipe | Gujarati Gond Gur Papdi
3 from 2 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 40 minutes mins
Total Time 50 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine gujarati
Servings 25 pieces
Calories 128 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup gond
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup cashew
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup badam
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup dry coconut, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a mixer jar take ¬Ω cup gond, ¬º cup cashew and ¬Ω cup badam.
  * pulse and grind to a coarse powder. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 1 cup ghee. add 1 cup wheat flour and roast on low flame.
  * roast for 15 to 20 minutes or until the wheat flour turns aromatic.
  * add in powdered nuts and gond powder.
  * continue to fry until the gond starts to pop.
  * roast until the mixture turns aromatic.
  * further, add ¬Ω cup dry coconut and roast well.
  * cool the mixture slightly. make sure to stir in between to prevent it from burning.
  * the mixture should be lukewarm before adding the jaggery. if the mixture is too hot, then jaggery will melt and sukhdi will turn hard.
  * once the mixture turns warm, add 1 cup jaggery and ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder.
  * mix well making sure the jaggery is well combined.
  * the mixture will start to hold the shape.
  * now transfer to the plate greased with ghee.
  * level out making sure it is of uniform thickness.
  * cool for 20. to 30 minutes, and cut into pieces.
  * finally, enjoy Sukhdi Recipe or Gond Pak Recipe for a month when stored in an airtight container.

### Nutrition
Calories: 128kcalCarbohydrates: 13gProtein: 1gFat: 8gSaturated Fat: 5gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.4gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gCholesterol: 18mgSodium: 1mgPotassium: 20mgFiber: 0.3gSugar: 8gVitamin C: 0.1mgCalcium: 4mgIron: 0.4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Sukhdi with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, in a mixer jar take ¬Ω cup gond, ¬º cup cashew and ¬Ω cup badam.  !
  2. pulse and grind to a coarse powder. keep aside.  !
  3. in a large kadai heat 1 cup ghee. add 1 cup wheat flour and roast on low flame.  !
  4. roast for 15 to 20 minutes or until the wheat flour turns aromatic.  !
  5. add in powdered nuts and gond powder.  !
  6. continue to fry until the gond starts to pop.  !
  7. roast until the mixture turns aromatic.  !
  8. further, add ¬Ω cup dry coconut and roast well.  !
  9. cool the mixture slightly. make sure to stir in between to prevent it from burning. the mixture should be lukewarm before adding the jaggery. if the mixture is too hot, then jaggery will melt and sukhdi will turn hard.  !
  10. once the mixture turns warm, add 1 cup jaggery and ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder.  !
  11. mix well making sure the jaggery is well combined.  !
  12. the mixture will start to hold the shape.  !
  13. now transfer to the plate greased with ghee.  !
  14. level out making sure it is of uniform thickness.  !
  15. cool for 20 to 30 minutes, and cut into pieces.  !
  16. finally, enjoy **Sukhdi Recipe** or **Gond Pak Recipe** for a month when stored in an airtight container.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to roast the wheat flour really well. else the atta will taste raw and sticky.
  * Additionally, adding gond makes the sukhdi flavourful and nutritious.
  * Also, you can add khova or mawa to the mixture to make the gond pak moist and soft.
  * Finally, use fresh homemade ghee for preparing **Sukhdi Recipe** or **Gond Pak Recipe**

# Recipe 47
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mohanthal-sweet-recipe-halwai-style/

### Mohanthal Video Recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## Recipe card for Halwai Style Mohanthal Sweet:
!

## Mohanthal Recipe | Halwai Style Mohanthal Mihai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy mohanthal recipe | halwai style mohanthal sweet | mohanthal mithai
4.78 from 9 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 1 hour hr 30 minutes mins
Resting Time 4 hours hrs
Total Time 5 hours hrs 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine gujarati
Servings 9 pieces
Calories 515 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for besan mixture:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup milk

#### for roasting:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup milk

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch saffron food colour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup khova / mawa
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ silver vark, for garnishing
  * ‚ñ¢ dry fruits, chopped

### Instructions

#### how to make danedar besan:
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cup besan, ¬º cup ghee and ¬º cup milk.
  * crumble and mix until the besan turns moist.
  * keep rubbing, until the besan turns grainy texture.
  * now sieve the besan using a large holes sieve.
  * the besan turns grainy texture. keep aside.

#### how to roast besan:
  * in a large kadai heat 1 cup ghee and add besan mixture.
  * keep roasting the besan on low flame.
  * after roasting for 20 minutes, the besan turns golden brown and ghee releases from sides.
  * now add ¬Ω cup milk and mix continuously.
  * the mixture turns frothy forming a more grainy texture.
  * keep cooking the besan until the milk is absorbed completely.
  * transfer to a bowl and keep aside.

#### how to make sugar syrup:
  * in a large kadai add 1¬Ω cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.
  * boil until 1 string consistency of sugar syrup is attained.
  * add pinch saffron food colour and mix well. adding colour is optional, however, it enhances the colour of burfi.
  * further, add ¬Ω cup khova and mix well. mix until the khova is well combined in sugar syrup.
  * now add roasted besan mixture into the sugar syrup.
  * mix well making sure the besan is well combined.
  * continue to cook until the mixture starts to separate the pan.
  * also, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and mix well.
  * transfer the mixture into the tray lined with baking paper.
  * tap and level up forming an even top.
  * rest for 4 hours, or you can refrigerate to set quickly.
  * once the burfi has set completely, unmould and decorate with silver vark.
  * chop into the desired shape and garnish with dry fruits.
  * finally, enjoy mohanthal for a week when refrigerated.

### Nutrition
Calories: 515kcalCarbohydrates: 57gProtein: 10gFat: 28gSaturated Fat: 16gPolyunsaturated Fat: 2gMonounsaturated Fat: 8gCholesterol: 66mgSodium: 36mgPotassium: 367mgFiber: 4gSugar: 39gVitamin A: 49IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 42mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Mohanthal with step by step photos:

### How to make danedar besan:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cups besan, ¬º cup ghee and ¬º cup milk.  !
  2. crumble and mix until the besan turns moist.  !
  3. keep rubbing, until the besan turns a grainy texture.  !
  4. now sieve the besan using a large holes sieve.  !
  5. the besan turns grainy texture. keep aside.  !

### How to roast besan:
  1. In a large kadai heat 1 cup ghee and add the besan mixture.  !
  2. keep roasting the besan on low flame.  !
  3. after roasting for 20 minutes, the besan turns golden brown and ghee is releases from the sides.  !
  4. now add ¬Ω cup milk and mix continuously.  !
  5. the mixture turns frothy forming a more grainy texture.  !
  6. keep cooking the besan until the milk is absorbed completely.  !
  7. transfer to a bowl and keep aside.  !

### How to make sugar syrup:
  1. In a large kadai add 1¬Ω cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  2. boil until 1 string of consistency of sugar syrup is attained.  !
  3. add a pinch of saffron food colour and mix well. adding colour is optional, however, it enhances the colour of the burfi.  !
  4. further, add ¬Ω cup khova and mix well. mix until the khova is well combined with sugar syrup.  !
  5. now add the roasted besan mixture to the sugar syrup.  !
  6. mix well making sure the besan is well combined.  !
  7. continue to cook until the mixture starts to separate from the pan.  !
  8. also, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and mix well.  !
  9. transfer the mixture to the tray lined with baking paper.  !
  10. tap and level up forming an even top.  !
  11. rest for 4 hours, or you can refrigerate to set quickly.  !
  12. once the burfi has set completely, unmould and decorate with silver vark.  !
  13. chop into the desired shape and garnish with dry fruits.  !
  14. Finally, enjoy **mohanthal** for a week when refrigerated.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to roast on low flame, else the besan will burn and not turn aromatic.
  * Also, adding khova is optional. however, it enhances the flavour of mithai.
  * Additionally, do not skip rubbing besan with milk and ghee. it helps to make grainy besan.
  * Finally, **mohanthal recipe** tastes great when prepared with fresh ghee and khova.

# Recipe 48
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/khatti-dal-recipe-hyderabadi-special/

### Video Recipe

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## Recipe Card for Hyderabadi Special Khatti Dal
!

## Khatti Dal Recipe | Hyderabadi Special Khatti Dhal
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Khatti Dal Recipe | Hyderabadi Special Khatti Dhal
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course dal
Cuisine Andhra Pradesh
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 249 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ball sized tamarind
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 cloves garlic, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl soak ball sized tamarind for 15 minutes. Keep aside.
  * In a pressure cooker, take 1 cup toor dal, 2 tomato, 5 chilli, few curry leaves, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp ghee.
  * Pour in 3 cup water and pressure cook for 9 whistles.
  * Once the pressure settles down, mash the dal slightly.
  * Add 2 tbsp coriander and squeeze the tamarind extract.
  * Mix well and boil for 5 minutes or until the raw flavour of tamarind is gone.
  * Also add 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp salt and 1 cup water.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Continue to boil for 5 minutes or until the dal turns aromatic.
  * To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp ghee. Add ¬Ω tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 10 cloves garlic, 3 dried red chilli, pinch hing and few curry leaves.
  * Splutter the tempering.
  * Pour the tempering over the dal and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Khatti Dal Recipe with hot steamed rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 249kcalCarbohydrates: 33gProtein: 10gFat: 10gSaturated Fat: 5gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 3gCholesterol: 22mgSodium: 943mgPotassium: 425mgFiber: 8gSugar: 6gVitamin A: 1281IUVitamin C: 97mgCalcium: 73mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Khatti Dal with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl soak ball sized tamarind for 15 minutes. Keep aside.  !
  2. In a pressure cooker, take 1 cup toor dal, 2 tomato, 5 chilli, few curry leaves, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp ghee.  !
  3. Pour in 3 cup water and pressure cook for 9 whistles.  !
  4. Once the pressure settles down, mash the dal slightly.  !
  5. Add 2 tbsp coriander and squeeze the tamarind extract.  !
  6. Mix well and boil for 5 minutes or until the raw flavour of tamarind is gone.  !
  7. Also add 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp salt and 1 cup water.  !
  8. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  9. Continue to boil for 5 minutes or until the dal turns aromatic.  !
  10. To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp ghee. Add ¬Ω tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 10 cloves garlic, 3 dried red chilli, pinch hing and few curry leaves.  !
  11. Splutter the tempering.  !
  12. Pour the tempering over the dal and mix well.  !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Khatti Dal Recipe** with hot steamed rice.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to cook the dal well and mash smoothly adjusting the consistency as required.
  * Also, you can increase the amount of chilli depending on the spice level.
  * Additionally, you can also add onion while pressure cooking.
  * Finally, **Khatti Dal Recipe** tastes great when prepared spicy and tangy.

# Recipe 49
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/hyderabadi-veg-biryani-veg-dum-biryani/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Veg Biriyani
It is basically a vegetarian alternative to the popular meat-based rice biriyani dedicated to vegetarian or non-meat eaters. In other **Veg Biriyani** most commonly known as Veg Dum Biriyani is made with a combination of vegetables as an alternative to meat variants like chicken or mutton options. The concept of Veg Biriyani was introduced very recently but has gained a lot of popularity among both veg and non-vegetarians. It is mainly due to the combination of authentic flavor, taste, and the range of spices it has to offer.
There are myriad ways to make this simple and tasty rice-based dish, but the most common way is the **Hyderabadi Dum Biriyani Recipe**. In this variant, the rice and gravy are cooked separately but then layered and slow-cooked. This style of slow cooking is known as Dum cooking. This also helps to infuse a lot of flavor to the long grain rice from the gravy, yet keeping the integrity of the rice. The other popular ways include mixing rice and gravy together to make moist and flavored rice. This can be either pressure-cooked or pan-cooked.

## Chef Tips for Veg Biriyani
There are many variables to be considered while preparing the biriyani recipe. Some simple and effective tips should really help to make it better
  1. **Rice selection ‚Äì** The typical choice for any biriyani recipe is long-grain basmati rice. Particularly it is cooked in such a fashion that, it remains long, non-sticky, and not mushy. There are other types of biriyani where other types of rice can be chosen. However, basmati rice is most recommended.
  2. **Slow cooking ‚Äì** The taste of biriyani builds as it gets cooked slowly in a slow flame. Particularly the dum biriyani has to be cooked in that way. More importantly, the biriyani tastes great when rested.
  3. **Vegetables ‚Äì** The choice of vegetables is super important for veg biriyani. The most basic combination is potatoes, carrots, beans, peas and mushrooms. Also, do not overpower each other and keep it balanced.
  4. **Biriyani Masala ‚Äì** Biriyani Spice Mix plays a huge role in this rice-based dish. I typically use homemade or Shaan Brand Bombay Biriyani Mix for most of my biriyani recipes. However, any tried and tested spice mix can be used with the below-mentioned recipe.
  5. **Accompaniments ‚Äì** Typically the dum biriyani is served with spicy gravy Mirchi ka Salan and raita. Salan, helps t make raise more flavored and moist whereas the raita helps to lower the spice level.

## Why does this recipe work
There are many simple and complex reasons why the biriyani recipe is super popular across India if not globally. Some major reasons are
  1. **Premium Flavor ‚Äì** In Indian cuisine, the rice biriyani is considered to be the most flavored and tasty rice recipe. There are various instant and traditional rice-based pulao and fried rice, but nothing comes close to the flavors of the biriyani recipe.
  2. **One Pot Meal ‚Äì** Compared to the other rice or bread recipes, which typically require curry, dal, or sambar. The biriyani recipes do not require any additional main dishes to serve with it.
  3. **Comfort Food ‚Äì** Traditionally, biriyani recipes were considered as premium limited to celebrations and festivals. However, due to its popularity, it is now used in day-to-day meals due to its comfort and pleasing appetite.
  4. **Versatility ‚Äì** The rice and biryani gravy can be cooked in multiple ways. The most common way is the dum style with rice and gravy cooked in layers. Alternatively, you can mix it all together and pressure cook it. Also, it can take, meat, veggies, and a combination of mixed herbs.
  5. **Healthy ‚Äì** Due to the combination of spices used with rice and fresh herbs, it is considered to be digestion-friendly and improves gut health. Particularly, the meat biriyani is a packaged meal with all proteins, carbs, and fiber in one meal.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Veg Dum Biryani:
!

## Veg Dum Biryani | Hyderabadi Veg Biryani Recipe | Hyderabadi Biryani
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Veg Dum Biryani | Hyderabadi Veg Biryani Recipe | Hyderabadi Biryani
4.99 from 258 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 30 minutes mins
Cook Time 40 minutes mins
Soaking Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 40 minutes mins
Course biryani
Cuisine hyderabadi
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 667 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for marination:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 potato, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 beans, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 carrot, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp peas
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 mushroom, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp mint, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp coriander, chopped

#### for rice:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup basmati rice
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for soaking & boiling
  * ‚ñ¢ spices
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp mint, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ghee

#### for biryani:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 capsicum, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ fried onion
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup saffron milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp ghee

### Instructions

#### How to marinate vegetables for biryani:
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup curd, 2 tbsp ginger garlic paste, 2 chilli, 2 tsp lemon juice, 2 tsp oil, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, 2 tbsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt.
  * Whisk and mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Add 2 potato, 5 beans, 1 carrot, 3 tbsp peas, 10 mushroom, 3 tbsp mint and 3 tbsp coriander.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined. cover and marinate for 30 minutes.

#### How to make biryani base:
  * Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee and 2 tbsp oil.
  * Add 1 onion and fry until the onions turn golden brown.
  * Add 1 capsicum and fry until the capsicum turns crunchy.
  * Furthermore, add the prepared marination mixture and mix well.
  * Cover and cook for 10 minutes, or until the vegetables are cooked almost. Keep aside.
  * How to cook rice for biryani:
  * Firstly, rinse and soak 2 cup basmati rice for 30 minutes.
  * Now in a large vessel take enough water.
  * Add mixed spices, 3 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tbsp salt, 2 tsp lemon juice and 1 tsp ghee.
  * Boil for 5 minutes, or until the water turns flavourful.
  * Now add in soaked basmati rice and mix gently.
  * Boil for 5. minutes, or until the rice is 80% cooked.
  * Further, drain off the rice, and the rice is ready for layering in the biryani.

#### How to layer the dum biryani:
  * Firstly, spread out the biyani gravy base onto the kadai. Top with fried onion, coriander, and mint.
  * Further top with cooked rice and level out uniformly.
  * Also top with fried onion, coriander, and mint.
  * Pour ¬Ω cup saffron milk, 1 tsp biryani masala and 2 tsp ghee.
  * Cover and seal using almunium foil.
  * Simmer for 20 minutes, or until the rice is cooked well. make sure to rest for at least 30 minutes, before serving the veg dum biryani.
  * Finally, enjoy Veg Dum Biryani with salan and raita.

## How to Make Veg Biryani with step-by-step photos:

### How to marinate vegetables for biryani:
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup curd, 2 tbsp ginger garlic paste, 2 chilli, 2 tsp lemon juice, 2 tsp oil, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, 2 tbsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt.  !
  2. Whisk and mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Add 2 potato, 5 beans, 1 carrot, 3 tbsp peas, 10 mushroom, 3 tbsp mint and 3 tbsp coriander.  !
  4. Mix well making sure everything is well combined. cover and marinate for 30 minutes.  !

### How to make biryani base:
  1. Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee and 2 tbsp oil.  !
  2. Add 1 onion and fry until the onions turn golden brown.  !
  3. Add 1 capsicum and fry until the capsicum turns crunchy.  !
  4. Furthermore, add the prepared marination mixture and mix well.  !
  5. Cover and cook for 10 minutes, or until the vegetables are cooked almost. Keep aside.  !

### How to cook rice for biryani:
  1. Firstly, rinse and soak 2 cup basmati rice for 30 minutes.  !
  2. Now in a large vessel take enough water.  !
  3. Add mixed spices, 3 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tbsp salt, 2 tsp lemon juice and 1 tsp ghee.  !
  4. Boil for 5 minutes, or until the water turns flavourful.  !
  5. Now add in soaked basmati rice and mix gently.  !
  6. Boil for 5 minutes, or until the rice is 80% cooked.  !
  7. Further, drain off the rice, and the rice is ready for layering in the biryani.  !

### How to layer the dum biryani:
  1. Firstly, spread out the biyani gravy base onto the kadai. Top with fried onion, coriander, and mint.  !
  2. Further top with cooked rice and level out uniformly.  !
  3. Also top with fried onion, coriander, and mint.  !
  4. Pour ¬Ω cup saffron milk, 1 tsp biryani masala and 2 tsp ghee.  !
  5. Cover and seal using almunium foil.  !
  6. Simmer for 20 minutes, or until the rice is cooked well. make sure to rest for at least 30 minutes, before serving the veg dum biryani.  !
  7. Finally, enjoy **Veg Dum Biryani** with salan and raita.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, you can also seal the vessel with dough to make sure the steam doesn‚Äôt escape.
  * Also, add vegetables of your choice to make it more nutritious.
  * Additionally, use a thick-bottomed vessel and cook the biryani on low flame, or else the biryani might burn at the bottom.
  * Finally, **Hyderabadi Veg Dum Biryani** tastes great when served after 2-3 hours of preparation.

# Recipe 50

## About Hyderabadi Dum Chai:
It is basically a spice and herb-rich flavored tea recipe with a unique and pressurized cooking way. **Dum ki chai** has become an internet sensation lately, but it carries a lot of tradition and history. Moreover, it has become a popular hot beverage, especially with street food vendors due to its fancy cooking process and the strong flavored taste. This can be a perfect beverage after a comforting snack meal.
There are myriad ways to make milk-based tea using different sets of ingredients, but this recipe of dum ki chai has to be one of the **premium tea recipes**. Particularly, the blend of spices used in this recipe makes it a perfect hot drink with any type of heavy meal or a filling snack meal.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Hyderabadi Dum Chai:
!

## Hyderabadi Dum Chai Recipe | Irani Dum Chai | Dum Tea Recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Hyderabadi Dum Chai Recipe | Irani Dum Chai | Dum Tea Recipe
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 5 minutes mins
Total Time 10 minutes mins
Course beverage
Cuisine south indian
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 153 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp tea powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 6 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup milk

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a small vessel take 1 cup water.
  * tie a cloth on top using a rubber band or thread.
  * add 2 tbsp tea powder, 1 tbsp sugar, 1 inch ginger, 6 pods cardamom, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 inch cinnamon and ¬Ω tsp cloves.
  * place the vessel in the cooker.
  * add some water on the bottom of the cooker.
  * cover and pressure cook for 1 whistle or until all the flavours are absorbed by the water.
  * after the pressure settles down, sqeeze off the decoction from the cloth.
  * a strong tea decoction is ready.
  * in a saucepan take 2 cup milk and get to a boil.
  * add prepared tea decoction and mix well.
  * get the tea to a boil.
  * finally, enjoy Dum Ki Chai Recipe with some biscuits.

### Nutrition
Calories: 153kcalCarbohydrates: 14gProtein: 11gFat: 5gSaturated Fat: 3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.2gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 20mgSodium: 67mgPotassium: 284mgFiber: 1gSugar: 12gVitamin A: 767IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 216mgIron: 2mg

## How to make Irani Dum Chai with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, in a small vessel take 1 cup water.  !
  2. tie a cloth on top using a rubber band or thread.  !
  3. add 2 tbsp tea powder, 1 tbsp sugar, 1 inch ginger, 6 pods cardamom, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 inch cinnamon, and ¬Ω tsp cloves.  !
  4. place the vessel in the cooker. add some water to the bottom of the cooker.  !
  5. cover and pressure cook for 1 whistle or until all the flavors are absorbed by the water.  !
  6. after the pressure settles down, squeeze off the decoction from the cloth.  !
  7. a strong tea decoction is ready.  !
  8. in a saucepan take 2 cup milk and get to a boil.  !
  9. add prepared tea decoction and mix well.  !
  10. get the tea to a boil.  !
  11. finally, enjoy **Dum Ki Chai Recipe** with some biscuits.  !

## Notes:
  * firstly, make pressure cooking the decoction helps to give more flavor.
  * also, you can add more sugar if you prefer the chai sweeter.
  * additionally, you can prepare the decoction in hand and mix it with hot milk just before serving.
  * finally, **Dum Ki Chai Recipe** tastes great when served hot and strong.

# Recipe 51

## About Tomato Salan:
It is basically a simple flavored curry recipe prepared with whole tomatoes dipped and cooked in a peanut and coconut-based gravy. **Tomato salan curry** is an ideal side dish with flavored rice like biriyani and pulao, but can also be served with different types of Indian flatbread. The addition of tomatoes to a salan gravy makes it more flavored and thick with a sweet and tangy taste to it.
As the name suggests **Bagare Tamatar Salan** is a traditional Hyderabadi curry. It is traditionally served with biriyani rice but due to its taste and thickness, it can also be served with any other Indian meal recipes. As of today, this is mainly prepared on various occasions like a marriage feast with any choice of rice and bread. Particularly the combination of sweet, , and spicy taste makes it unique and special.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Bagare Tamatar Salan:
!

## Tomato Salan Recipe | Bagare Tamatar Salan | Hyderabadi Tomato Curry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Tomato Salan Recipe | Bagare Tamatar Salan | Hyderabadi Tomato Curry
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine hyderabadi
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 172 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for masala paste:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp peanut
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp dry coconut
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water

#### for salan:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 cloves garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ small piece jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, half
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup tamarind extract
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a pan dry roast 2 tbsp peanut until it turns crunchy.
  * add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp dry coconut, 1 tsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.
  * add ¬Ω cup water and grind to smooth paste. keep aside.
  * in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. splutter 1 tsp mustard, pinch hing and 1 tsp cumin.
  * add ¬Ω onion, 10 cloves garlic and saute until onion softens.
  * further add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * also, add the prepared masala paste and cook until the oil separates.
  * now add 2 cup water, few curry leaves and small piece of jaggery.
  * mix well adjusting the consistency as required.
  * boil for 10 minutes, or until the oil separates.
  * now add 2 tomato, 2 chilli and ¬Ω cup tamarind extract.
  * cover and boil for 5 minutes or until the tomato softens.
  * finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy tomato curry with biryani or roti.

### Nutrition
Calories: 172kcalCarbohydrates: 12gProtein: 4gFat: 13gSaturated Fat: 2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 4gMonounsaturated Fat: 7gTrans Fat: 0.03gSodium: 624mgPotassium: 420mgFiber: 3gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 948IUVitamin C: 50mgCalcium: 104mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Tomato Salan with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, in a pan dry roast 2 tbsp peanut until it turns crunchy.  !
  2. add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp dry coconut, 1 tsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin.  !
  3. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  4. cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.  !
  5. add ¬Ω cup water and grind to smooth paste. keep aside.  !
  6. in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. splutter 1 tsp mustard, pinch hing and 1 tsp cumin.  !
  7. add ¬Ω onion, 10 cloves garlic and saute until onion softens.  !
  8. further add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt.  !
  9. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  10. also, add the prepared masala paste and cook until the oil separates.  !
  11. now add 2 cup water, few curry leaves and small piece of jaggery.  !
  12. mix well adjusting the consistency as required.  !
  13. boil for 10 minutes, or until the oil separates.  !
  14. now add 2 tomato, 2 chilli and ¬Ω cup tamarind extract.  !
  15. cover and boil for 5 minutes or until the tomato softens.  !
  16. finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy **tomato curry** with biryani or roti.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to cook the curry really well, or else the curry tastes raw.
  * Additionally, you can add whole tomato, however cooking time increases.
  * Also, adding dry coconut gives a nice flavour to the salan.
  * Finally, **Tomato Curry** or**Tomato Salan** tastes great when served spicy.

# Recipe 52

## Recipe Card for Hyderabadi Instant Spicy Idli on Tawa:

## Spot Idli Recipe | Hyderabadi Instant Spicy Idli On Tawa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Spot Idli Recipe | Hyderabadi Instant Spicy Idli On Tawa
5 from 1 vote
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine indian street food
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 406 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for milagai podi:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup sesame seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 20 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ handful curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ lemon sized tamarind
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp turmeric

#### for spot idli:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp tomato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp curry leaves, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp milagai podi
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp butter
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bowl idli batter
  * ‚ñ¢ butter, for roasting

### Instructions

#### how to make milagai podi:
  * firstly, in a pan heat 2 tsp oil. roast ¬æ cup chana dal, 1 cup urad dal, and ¬º cup sesame seeds until it turns aromatic.
  * once the dal turns golden brown and aromatic, transfer it to a plate and cool it completely.
  * heat 1 tsp oil and add 20 dried red chilli, a handful of curry leaves, and lemon-sized tamarind.
  * roast until the chilli puffs up and turns crunchy.
  * transfer to the plate and cool completely.
  * once everything is cooled completely, transfer to the mixer jar.
  * add 2 tsp jaggery, 1¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp hing.
  * grind to a fine powder without adding water.
  * finally, milagai podi is ready to enjoy.

#### how to make spot idli:
  * in a large cast iron pan, heat 1 tbsp oil.
  * add 2 tbsp onion, ¬Ω tsp ginger, 1 chilli and 1 tsp coriander. saute until the onion softens.
  * further add 2 tbsp tomato, 1 tsp curry leaves and saute until the tomato softens.
  * now add 2 tsp milagai podi and 1 tsp butter. roast until everything is well combined.
  * divide into 4 parts giving good space in between.
  * pour in a ladleful of idli batter.
  * also sprinkle some milagai podi, butter and coriander.
  * cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the idli batter is cooked well.
  * now carefully flip over without breaking the idli.
  * roast on both sides until it turns golden brown and crisp.
  * finally, enjoy spot idli with chutney and milagai podi.

### Nutrition
Calories: 406kcalCarbohydrates: 53gProtein: 19gFat: 14gSaturated Fat: 2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 4gMonounsaturated Fat: 6gTrans Fat: 0.1gCholesterol: 3mgSodium: 894mgPotassium: 130mgFiber: 20gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 446IUVitamin C: 69mgCalcium: 200mgIron: 7mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make spot idli with step-by-step photos:

### how to make milagai podi:
  1. firstly, in a pan heat 2 tsp oil. roast ¬æ cup chana dal, 1 cup urad dal, and ¬º cup sesame seeds until it turns aromatic.  !
  2. once the dal turns golden brown and aromatic, transfer it to a plate and cool it completely.  !
  3. heat 1 tsp oil and add 20 dried red chilli, a handful of curry leaves, and lemon-sized tamarind.  !
  4. roast until the chilli puffs up and turns crunchy.  !
  5. transfer to the plate and cool completely.  !
  6. once everything is cooled completely, transfer to the mixer jar.  !
  7. add 2 tsp jaggery, 1¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp hing.  !
  8. grind to a fine powder without adding water.  !
  9. finally, **milagai podi** is ready to enjoy.  !

### how to make spot idli:
  1. in a large cast iron pan, heat 1 tbsp oil.  !
  2. add 2 tbsp onion, ¬Ω tsp ginger, 1 chilli and 1 tsp coriander. saute until the onion softens.  !
  3. further add 2 tbsp tomato, 1 tsp curry leaves and saute until the tomato softens.  !
  4. now add 2 tsp milagai podi and 1 tsp butter. roast until everything is well combined.  !
  5. divide into 4 parts giving good space in between.  !
  6. pour in a ladleful of idli batter.  !
  7. also sprinkle some milagai podi, butter and coriander.  !
  8. cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the idli batter is cooked well.  !
  9. now carefully flip over without breaking the idli.  !
  10. roast on both sides until it turns golden brown and crisp.  !
  11. finally, enjoy **spot idli** with chutney and milagai podi.  !

## Notes:
  * firstly, make sure not to overcook the masala, as it will burn while further cooking with batter.
  * also adding butter gives a nice flavour to the idli.
  * additonally, you can use suji batter if you do not have idli batter.
  * finally, **spot idli recip** e tastes great when the milagai podi is spicy.

# Recipe 53
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/kaddu-ki-kheer-recipe-hyderabadi-style/

### Kaddu Ki Kheer video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## Recipe Card for Pumpkin Kheer:
!

## Kaddu Ki Kheer Recipe | Hyderabadi Style Pumpkin Milk Pudding
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Kaddu Ki Kheer Recipe | Hyderabadi Style Pumpkin Milk Pudding
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 40 minutes mins
Total Time 50 minutes mins
Course Dessert
Cuisine hyderabadi
Servings 10 Servings
Calories 174 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup lauki / kaddu / bottle gourd, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup sabudana, soaked 30 minutes
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup cream
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup mawa / khoya, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp nuts
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 drops green food color
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ silver vark, for decoration

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large kadai heat 1 tsp ghee and add 1¬Ω cup lauki.
  * saute for 2 minutes or until the lauki turns aromatic.
  * now add 5 cup of milk and get to a boil stirring in between.
  * also, add ¬º cup sabudana and mix well.
  * boil for 5 minutes or until the sabudana and sago gets cooked well.
  * further add ¬º cup cream, ¬Ω cup mawa, and 3 tbsp nuts. stir well.
  * add 3 drops of green food color and mix well. adding food color is optional.
  * simmer for 15 minutes or until the kheer thickens.
  * now add ¬æ cup sugar and mix well.
  * boil for 5 minutes or until the kheer thickens and turns creamy.
  * further, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well.
  * cool completely, and transfer to a large bowl.
  * refrigerate for 2 hours or until the kheer thickens.
  * now add nuts and decorate with silver vark.
  * finally, enjoy kaddu ki kheer chilled or you can warm it up.

### Nutrition
Calories: 174kcalCarbohydrates: 22gProtein: 5gFat: 8gSaturated Fat: 4gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gCholesterol: 23mgSodium: 49mgPotassium: 208mgFiber: 0.3gSugar: 21gVitamin A: 286IUVitamin C: 0.1mgCalcium: 157mgIron: 0.1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Kaddu Ki Kheer with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, in a large kadai heat 1 tsp ghee and add 1¬Ω cups lauki.  !
  2. saute for 2 minutes or until the lauki turns aromatic.  !
  3. now add 5 cup of milk and get to a boil stirring in between.  !
  4. also, add ¬º cup sabudana and mix well.  !
  5. boil for 5 minutes or until the sabudana and sago gets cooked well.  !
  6. further add ¬º cup cream, ¬Ω cup mawa, and 3 tbsp nuts. stir well.  !
  7. add 3 drops of green food color and mix well. adding food color is optional.  !
  8. simmer for 15 minutes or until the kheer thickens.  !
  9. now add ¬æ cup sugar and mix well.  !
  10. boil for 5 minutes or until the kheer thickens and turns creamy.  !
  11. further, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well.  !
  12. cool completely, and transfer to a large bowl.  !
  13. refrigerate for 2 hours or until the kheer thickens.  !
  14. now add nuts and decorate with silver vark.  !
  15. finally, enjoy **kaddu ki kheer** chilled or you can warm it up.  !

## Notes:
  * firstly, grate the lauki really fine else it will not taste good in kheer.
  * also, adding sabudana makes kheer thick and gives a nice bubble bite.
  * additionally, you can add custard powder instead of cream to thicken the kheer.
  * finally,**kaddu ki kheer recipe** tastes great when served chilled.

# Recipe 54
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/vermicelli-pudding-recipe-nawabi-semai/

### vermicelli pudding video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for vermicelli pudding recipe:
!

## vermicelli pudding recipe | nawabi semai recipe | nawabi sawai dessert
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy vermicelli pudding recipe | nawabi semai recipe | nawabi sawai dessert
4.84 from 6 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 40 minutes mins
Refrigerating Time 4 hours hrs
Total Time 4 hours hrs 50 minutes mins
Course Dessert
Cuisine hyderabadi
Servings  Servings
Calories 308 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for roasting semiya:
  * ‚ñ¢ 300 grams semiya / vermicelli, fine
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp butter
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup khova / mawa
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup powdered sugar

#### for custard:
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup custard powder, vanilla flavour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup condensed milk

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp almonds, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp pistachios, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cashew, chopped

### Instructions

#### how to roast semiya:
  * firstly, in a pan heat 3 tbsp butter and roast 300 grams semia.
  * roast on low flame until it turns crunchy and light golden brown.
  * turn off the flame, add 1 cup khova and ¬Ω cup powdered sugar.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined. keep aside.

#### how to make an eggless custard recipe:
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 4 cup milk.
  * add ¬Ω cup custard powder, 1 cup condensed milk and mix well.
  * mix well making sure there are no lumps.
  * pour the mixture into large kadai and cook on low flame.
  * keep stirring on a low flame until the mixture thickens.
  * cook until the mixture turns creamy thick. it thickens once cooled completely.

#### how to layer the nawabi semiya:
  * firstly, in pan transfer half the amount of roasted semiya.
  * press and level it up, making sure it will be tight.
  * pour in prepared custard, leaving some gap for semiya to top it up.
  * now top up with roasted semiya and then roasted nuts (almonds, pistachios and cashews).
  * cover and refrigerate for 4 hours or until the custard sets completely.
  * finally, cut the nawabi semiya into pieces and enjoy.

### Nutrition
Calories: 308kcalCarbohydrates: 37gProtein: 8gFat: 15gSaturated Fat: 7gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 5gTrans Fat: 1gCholesterol: 40mgSodium: 143mgPotassium: 365mgFiber: 1gSugar: 35gVitamin A: 442IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 260mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make nawabi semai with step by step photo:

### how to roast semiya:
  1. firstly, in a pan heat 3 tbsp butter and roast 300 grams semia.  !
  2. roast on low flame until it turns crunchy and light golden brown.  !
  3. turn off the flame, add 1 cup khova and ¬Ω cup powdered sugar.  !
  4. mix well making sure everything is well combined. keep aside.  !

### how to make an eggless custard recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 4 cup milk.  !
  2. add ¬Ω cup custard powder, 1 cup condensed milk and mix well. mix well making sure there are no lumps.  !
  3. pour the mixture into large kadai and cook on low flame. keep stirring on a low flame until the mixture thickens.  !
  4. cook until the mixture turns creamy thick. it thickens once cooled completely.  !

### how to layer the nawabi semiya:
  1. firstly, in pan transfer half the amount of roasted semiya.  !
  2. press and level it up, making sure it will be tight.  !
  3. pour in prepared custard, leaving some gap for semiya to top it up.  !
  4. now top up with roasted semiya and then roasted nuts (almonds, pistachios and cashews).  !
  5. cover and refrigerate for 4 hours or until the custard sets completely.  !
  6. finally, cut the**nawabi semiya** into pieces and enjoy.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to roast on low flame until the semiya turns crunchy. over roasting makes semiya burn.
  * also, if you are not using condensed milk in custard then add ¬Ω cup sugar.
  * additionally, you can use any flavour of custard powder to make it flavourful.
  * finally, **nawabi semiya recipe** tastes great when served chilled.
