## Potato Sagu Recipe | Bombay Sagu - Aloo Saagu for Poori
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Potato Sagu Recipe | Bombay Sagu - Aloo Saagu for Poori
5 from 189 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 servings
Calories 107 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 boiled potato
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tomato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp gram flour / besan
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, roughly mash 3 boiled potato making sure there are little pieces in it. Keep aside.
  * In a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 1 tsp urad dal, 1 tsp chana dal, 1 dried red chilli, pinch hing and few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.
  * Add 1 inch ginger, 2 chilli and saute slightly.
  * Further, add 1 onion and saute until the onion softens slightly.
  * keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and 1 tsp salt.
  * Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Further, add 1 tomato and cook till the tomato softens.
  * Add in mashed potato, 2 cup water and mix well. Adjust the salt to your preference.
  * In a small bowl mix 2 tbsp gram flour with ¬Ω cup water. Make sure there are no lumps.
  * Pour the besan slurry and mix continuously until the curry boils.
  * Continue to boil for 5 minutes, or until the raw smell of besan is gone.
  * Further add 2 tbsp coriander, ¬Ω lemon and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Bombay Sagu Recipe with poori or roti.

### Nutrition
Calories: 107kcalCarbohydrates: 10gProtein: 2gFat: 8gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 2gMonounsaturated Fat: 5gTrans Fat: 0.03gSodium: 615mgPotassium: 274mgFiber: 2gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 618IUVitamin C: 52mgCalcium: 41mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Potato Sagu with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, roughly mash 3 boiled potato making sure there are little pieces in it. Keep aside.  !
  2. In a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 1 tsp urad dal, 1 tsp chana dal, 1 dried red chilli, pinch hing and few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.  !
  3. Add 1 inch ginger, 2 chilli and saute slightly.  !
  4. Further, add 1 onion and saute until the onion softens slightly.  !
  5. keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and 1 tsp salt.  !
  6. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  7. Further, add 1 tomato and cook till the tomato softens.  !
  8. Add in mashed potato, 2 cup water and mix well. Adjust the salt to your preference.  !
  9. In a small bowl mix 2 tbsp gram flour with ¬Ω cup water. Make sure there are no lumps.  !
  10. Pour the besan slurry and mix continuously until the curry boils.  !
  11. Continue to boil for 5 minutes, or until the raw smell of besan is gone.  !
  12. Further add 2 tbsp coriander, ¬Ω lemon and mix well.  !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Bombay Sagu Recipe** with poori or roti.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, the consistency of sagu thickens once cooled. So adjust it by adding water as requried.
  * Additionally, make sure to keep stirring once the besan slrry is added to prevent any lumps from forming.
  * Also, you can increase the chilli to make the sagu spicy.
  * Finally, **Bombay Sagu Recipe** tastes great when made slightly watery.

# Recipe 92
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/shepu-bhaji-recipe-healthy-dill-bhaji/

### Video Recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## Recipe Card for Healthy Dill Bhaji:
!

## Shepu Bhaji Recipe | Healthy Dill Bhaji | Shepu Ki Bhaji
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Shepu Bhaji Recipe | Healthy Dill Bhaji | Shepu Ki Bhaji
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course sabzi
Cuisine maharashtra
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 239 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bunch dill leaves / shepu / suva / sabsige, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup moong dal, soaked 30 minutes
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 3 chilli, pinch hing and splutter on medium flame.
  * Add 1 onion and saute until the onion softens.
  * Also add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt and saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Now add in ¬Ω cup soaked moong dal and stir fry until the dal turns aromatic. Make sure to soak the moong dal for 30 minutes and drain off the water before adding.
  * Add in 1 bunch chopped dill leaves and saute for 2 minutes.
  * Further add ¬Ω cup water and mix well.
  * Cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the dal is cooked well.
  * Finally, enjoy Shepu Bhaji Recipe with roti or rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 239kcalCarbohydrates: 29gProtein: 10gFat: 10gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 6gTrans Fat: 0.04gSodium: 424mgPotassium: 215mgFiber: 5gSugar: 5gVitamin A: 501IUVitamin C: 67mgCalcium: 34mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Shepu Bhaji with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 3 chilli, pinch hing and splutter on medium flame.  !
  2. Add 1 onion and saute until the onion softens.  !
  3. Also add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt and saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  4. Now add in ¬Ω cup soaked moong dal and stir fry until the dal turns aromatic. Make sure to soak the moong dal for 30 minutes and drain off the water before adding.  !
  5. Add in 1 bunch chopped dill leaves and saute for 2 minutes.  !
  6. Further add ¬Ω cup water and mix well.  !
  7. Cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the dal is cooked well.  !
  8. Finally, enjoy **Shepu Bhaji Recipe** with roti or rice.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, as a variation, you can top it with fresh coconut or roasted peanut powder.
  * Also, do not add any masala, as the flavour of actual dill leaves will be lost.
  * Additionally, since we have soaked the dal, it does not take much time to cook.
  * Finally, **Shepu Bhaji Recipe** is a healthy sabzi and can be eaten as a diabetic diet.

# Recipe 93

####

## About Tawa Pulao
It is a simple fried rice recipe made with pre-cooked rice mixed with pav bhaji masala and cooked vegetables. **Tawa Pulao** or **Pav Bhaji Pulao** is a popular Mumbai-originated street food that has it fan following across India. Typically it is served after appetizer meals like Pav Bhaji or Vada pav as a main meal. But it can also be served as a lunch box or a tiffin box meal for kids and adults. It tastes great when served with a simple yogurt-based raita.
There are many different types of **Mumbai Tawa Pulao** , but the most common is a simple mix of pav bhaji masala and vegetables. Typically pre-cooked basmati rice is just tossed with either pre-cooked pav bhaji curry or mixed with masala and vegetables. It can also be prepared as a pot meal in a pressure . This needs more attention as it may turn mushy and sticky. The other types of rice can also be used, but it has to be dry and moisture-free.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Street Style Tawa Pulao
!

## Tawa Pulao Recipe | Mumbai Tawa Pulao | Pav Bhaji Pulao
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Tawa Pulao Recipe | Mumbai Tawa Pulao | Pav Bhaji Pulao
5 from 205 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course rice
Cuisine indian street food
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 533 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp butter
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω capsicum, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp peas
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 carrot, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 potato, boiled
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cup cooked rice, basmati
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil, 1 tbsp butter and splutter 1 tsp cumin.
  * Add ¬Ω onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until onion softens.
  * Now add ¬Ω capsicum, 3 tbsp peas, 1 carrot, 2 tomato and stir fry until the vegetables turn crunchy.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 3 tsp pav bhaji masala and 1 tsp salt.
  * Saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Also, add 2 tbsp water and cook until all the masala are cooked well.
  * Add in 1 potato, 2 tbsp coriander and mix until the masala is coated well.
  * Further, add 5 cup cooked rice and mix gently.
  * Now add 2 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander and ¬Ω lemon. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Finally, enjoy Tawa Pulao Recipe with raita.

### Nutrition
Calories: 533kcalCarbohydrates: 90gProtein: 11gFat: 15gSaturated Fat: 3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 7gTrans Fat: 0.2gCholesterol: 10mgSodium: 847mgPotassium: 668mgFiber: 6gSugar: 8gVitamin A: 5506IUVitamin C: 105mgCalcium: 87mgIron: 3mg

## How to make Tawa Pulao with step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil, 1 tbsp butter and splutter 1 tsp cumin.  !
  2. Add ¬Ω onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until onion softens.  !
  3. Now add ¬Ω capsicum, 3 tbsp peas, 1 carrot, 2 tomato and stir fry until the vegetables turn crunchy.  !
  4. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 3 tsp pav bhaji masala and 1 tsp salt.  !
  5. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  6. Also, add 2 tbsp water and cook until all the masala is cooked well.  !
  7. Add in 1 potato, 2 tbsp coriander and mix until the masala is coated well.  !
  8. Further, add 5 cup cooked rice and mix gently.  !
  9. Now add 2 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander and ¬Ω lemon. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  10. Finally, enjoy **Tawa Pulao Recipe** with raita.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, do not skip adding pav bhaji masala, as it is a key ingredient in this recipe.
  * Additionally, keep the vegetables slightly crunchy to give a crunchy bite in pulao.
  * Also, you can add chilli paste to make it extra hot.
  * Finally, **Tawa Pulao Recipe** also tastes great for a lunch box.

## About Veg Frankie
It is a popular and tasty street food recipe from India with a combination of flavors it has to offer. There are myriad types or variations within the Frankie or Roll recipes, but the most popular one is the **Veg Frankie** or **Veg Kathi Roll recipe**. Typically, the roll is made with vegetable patties which are made with a combination of vegetables like carrots, beans, potatoes, and peas. The choice of vegetable is open-ended and it is up to individual taste and preference. Additionally, the patties or rolled inside flatbread or roti with sliced onions and herbs with a range of chutney and condiments sauces.
There are different types of roll or Frankie recipes across India and the variations depend upon the place it is prepared. The most common is **Veg Frankie** and Meat-based Frankie recipe. The choice of patties makes it a filling, complete, and balanced meal. It also makes it an ideal lunch or dinner meal or even a kid‚Äôs tiffin box meal. Typically, Kathi Roll is made with tomato sauce and mayo sauce. But this recipe can take any type of sauce to have different flavors and tastes.

## Chef Tips for Veg Frankie
The recipe is no rocket science and takes only basic ingredients to make it. Yet some important and basic tips and suggestions are ‚Äì
  1. **Wrap Quality ‚Äì** The wrap should be soft and moist so that it can be easily rolled. If the roti wrap turns hard, it may not be usable or to shape it.
  2. **Rolling Technique ‚Äì** Place the vegetables and patties at the center. Also, wrap it tightly so that the stuffing and sauce do not ooze out while eating it.
  3. **Condiments ‚Äì** Try to mix and match the sauce so that all flavors are combined to make it lip-smacking. In short, try to have the sweet, spicy, and savory flavors added to it.
  4. **Vegetables Stuffing ‚Äì** Keep it simple and use basic vegetables like onions, carrots, and shredded lettuce.
  5. **Spice Mix ‚Äì** You may top it up with Frankie masala to make it more flavored and exciting.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Veg Frankie
!

## Veg Frankie Recipe | Veg Kathi Roll Recipe | Veg Frankie Roll Recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Veg Frankie Recipe | Veg Kathi Roll Recipe | Veg Frankie Roll Recipe**
5 from 234 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine street food
Servings 5 Servings
Calories 330 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cloves garlic, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp chilli sauce
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 potato, boiled & mashed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

#### for chilli vinegar:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt

#### for roll:
  * ‚ñ¢ 
  * ‚ñ¢ coriander
  * ‚ñ¢ chaat masala
  * ‚ñ¢ onion
  * ‚ñ¢

### Instructions

#### How to make roti for frankie:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup maida, ¬Ω cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬º cup curd.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Now add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.
  * Grease the dough with oil, cover and rest for 20 minutes.
  * After the dough has rested well, knead the dough again and pinch a ball-sized dough.
  * Dust with maida and roll thin.
  * Now cook the roti on hot pan spreading oil.
  * Flip over and cook both sides.
  * Also, spread the oil and cook until the roti is cooked from both sides. Keep aside.

#### How to make stuffing for kathi roll:
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, 2 chilli, 2 cloves garlic and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste. Saute well until the raw aroma goes off.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, 2 tbsp chilli sauce and 2 tbsp tomato sauce.
  * Saute on low flame until the spices are well combined.
  * Now add 3 potato, ¬Ω tsp salt and mix well.
  * Mix until the spices are well combined.
  * Now add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tsp lemon juice and mix well.
  * Once the mixture is cooled slightly, shape the tikki.
  * Roast on hot pan adding oil as required.
  * Roast both the sides until the tikki turns golden brown and crispy. Keep aside.

#### How to make chilli vinegar:
  * In a small bowl take 3 tbsp vinegar, 2 chilli and ¬º tsp salt.
  * Mix well, and chilli vinegar is ready to use.

#### How to assemble veg frankie.
  * Firstly, take roti and spread green chutney.
  * Place the prepared aloo tikki, and top with coriander, chaat masala, onion, chilli vinegar and tomato sauce.
  * Roll tight and wrap in butter paper.
  * Finally, Veg Frankie Recipe is ready to enjoy with tomato sauce.

### Nutrition
Calories: 330kcalCarbohydrates: 57gProtein: 9gFat: 7gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 2gMonounsaturated Fat: 4gTrans Fat: 0.02gSodium: 693mgPotassium: 270mgFiber: 3gSugar: 6gVitamin A: 542IUVitamin C: 58mgCalcium: 53mgIron: 4mg

## How To Make Veg Kathi Roll with Step-by-step Photos

### How to make roti for frankie:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup maida, ¬Ω cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt, and ¬º cup curd.  !
  2. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Now add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.  !
  4. Grease the dough with oil, cover and rest for 20 minutes.  !
  5. After the dough has rested well, knead the dough again and pinch a ball-sized dough.  !
  6. Dust with maida and roll thin.  !
  7. Now cook the roti on hot pan spreading oil.  !
  8. Flip over and cook both sides. Also, spread the oil and cook until the roti is cooked from both sides. Keep aside.  !

### How to make stuffing for kathi roll:
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, 2 chilli, 2 cloves garlic and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste. Saute well until the raw aroma goes off.  !
  2. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, 2 tbsp chilli sauce and 2 tbsp tomato sauce.  !
  3. Saute on low flame until the spices are well combined.  !
  4. Now add 3 potato, ¬Ω tsp salt and mix well.  !
  5. Mix until the spices are well combined.  !
  6. Now add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tsp lemon juice and mix well.  !
  7. Once the mixture is cooled slightly, shape the tikki.  !
  8. Roast on hot pan adding oil as required.  !
  9. Roast both sides until the tikki turns golden brown and crispy. Keep aside.  !

### How to make chilli vinegar:
  1. In a small bowl take 3 tbsp vinegar, 2 chilli and ¬º tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well, and chilli vinegar is ready to use.  !

### How to assemble veg frankie.
  1. Firstly, take roti and spread green chutney.  !
  2. Place the prepared aloo tikki, and top with coriander, chaat masala, onion, chilli vinegar and tomato sauce.  !
  3. Roll tight and wrap in butter paper.  !
  4. Finally, **Veg Frankie Recipe** is ready to enjoy with tomato sauce.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to not overcook the roti as it hardens and does not remain soft after some time.
  * Also, you can use frankie masala instead of using chaat masala.
  * Additionally, you can top it with cheese to make a cheesy kathi roll.
  * Finally, **Veg Frankie Recipe** tastes great when it is made spicy and served hot.

## About Cutting Chai
It is a simple and popular hot beverage from the bustling city of Mumbai. **Cutting Chai** means ginger and spice-infused milk tea served in small, purpose-based glass tea cups. It is also known as cutting which means half or a small amount of tea served in small batches. Due to the small quantity of tea served, it is affordable economical, yet the flavored refreshments can be enjoyed.
There are many types and variations to the popular **Cutting Chai Recipe**. The variations are mainly applied to the tea or chai recipe. So in other words, any customization to the tea can be happily applied to this tea. Moreover, you may generously add tea masala powder while making this tea for spicy masala cutting chai. In addition, the tea also can be made with sugar less, so that you can enjoy the tea flavor.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Mumbai Cutting Chai
!

## Cutting Chai Recipe | Mumbai Cutting Tea Recipe | How to Make Cutting Chai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Cutting Chai Recipe | Mumbai Cutting Tea Recipe | How to Make Cutting Chai**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 1 minute min
Cook Time 9 minutes mins
Total Time 10 minutes mins
Course beverages
Cuisine Indian
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 83 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp tea powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup milk

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a mortar pestle take 1 inch ginger, 3 pods cardamom, 4 cloves, ¬Ω tsp pepper, and ¬Ω inch cinnamon.
  * Gently pound the pestle into the mortar to help masala release its flavors. Keep aside.
  * In a saucepan take 3 cup water and warm it on medium flame.
  * Once the water is hot enough, add prepared chai masala and boil for 3 minutes or until the flavors are infused in water.
  * Now add 3 tsp tea powder and boil for 2 minutes.
  * Once the tea flavors are infused in water, add 3 tsp sugar and boil until the sugar is melted.
  * Further, add 1 cup milk and get to a boil.
  * Just mix it and boil for 2 minutes for the aroma to be absorbed by the chai.
  * Finally, filter out the chai and serve Cutting Chai with biscuits.

### Nutrition
Calories: 83kcalCarbohydrates: 9gProtein: 5gFat: 3gSaturated Fat: 2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 10mgSodium: 44mgPotassium: 151mgFiber: 1gSugar: 8gVitamin A: 335IUVitamin C: 0.3mgCalcium: 116mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Masala Cutting Chai with step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a mortar pestle take 1 inch ginger, 3 pods cardamom, 4 cloves, ¬Ω tsp pepper, and ¬Ω inch cinnamon.  !
  2. Gently pound the pestle into the mortar to help masala release its flavors. Keep aside.  !
  3. In a saucepan take 3 cup water and warm it on medium flame.  !
  4. Once the water is hot enough, add prepared chai masala and boil for 3 minutes or until the flavors are infused in water.  !
  5. Now add 3 tsp tea powder and boil for 2 minutes.  !
  6. Once the tea flavors are infused in water, add 3 tsp sugar and boil until the sugar is melted.  !
  7. Further, add 1 cup of milk and get to a boil.  !
  8. Just mix it and boil for 2 minutes for the aroma to be absorbed by the chai.  !
  9. Finally, filter out the chai and serve **Cutting Chai** with biscuits.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, if you are looking for kadak chai then boil the tea decoction a little more.
  * Also, adjust the amount the sugar depending on your sweet tooth.
  * Additionally, before adding milk, boil the tea leaves in water for more flavor.
  * Finally, do not skip ginger as the ginger gives flavor and warmth to the **Cutting Chai**.

# Recipe 96
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/veg-fish-fry-recipe-raw-banana-fish-fry/

### Veg Fish Fry video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## Recipe Card for raw banana fish fry:
!

## veg fish fry recipe | raw banana fish fry | vegan fish rava fry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy veg fish fry recipe | raw banana fish fry | vegan fish rava fry
4 from 2 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Resting Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 55 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 197 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for marination:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 raw banana
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil

#### for rava coating:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rava / semolina / suji, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * firstly, peel the skin of raw banana. make sure to take fresh plantain else the kabab will be on the sweeter side.
  * slice thick making sure they are of uniform thickness. keep aside.
  * in a large plate take 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp coriander powder and ¬Ω tsp cumin powder.
  * also add ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tbsp ginger garlic paste, ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tsp oil.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined. this masala paste is called "meet mirsang" in Mangalore.
  * now spread the masala on the sliced raw banana.
  * allow marinating for 30 minutes or more.
  * now top prepare the coating, in a plate take 1 cup rava, and 2 tbsp rice flour.
  * also, add ¬º tsp chilli powder and ¬Ω tsp salt. mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * take the marinated raw banana and coat in rava.
  * deep fry in hot oil keeping the flame on medium.
  * make sure to not touch the kabab pieces for at least 1 minute. else there are chances for rava to disintegrate.
  * stir occasionally, and fry on medium flame until the banana turns golden brown and crisp.
  * drain off over a kitchen towel to remove excess oil.
  * finally, enjoy raw banana rava fry with green chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 197kcalCarbohydrates: 36gProtein: 6gFat: 3gSaturated Fat: 0.4gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gTrans Fat: 0.01gSodium: 619mgPotassium: 147mgFiber: 3gSugar: 0.4gVitamin A: 634IUVitamin C: 3mgCalcium: 22mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make veg fish fry with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, peel the skin of raw banana. make sure to take fresh plantain else the kabab will be on the sweeter side.  !
  2. slice thick making sure they are of uniform thickness. keep aside.  !
  3. in a large plate take 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp coriander powder and ¬Ω tsp cumin powder.  !
  4. also add ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tbsp ginger garlic paste, ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tsp oil.  !
  5. mix well making sure everything is well combined. this masala paste is called ‚Äúmeet mirsang‚Äù in Mangalore.  !
  6. now spread the masala on the sliced raw banana.  !
  7. allow marinating for 30 minutes or more.  !
  8. now top prepare the coating, in a plate take 1 cup rava, and 2 tbsp rice flour.  !
  9. also, add ¬º tsp chilli powder and ¬Ω tsp salt. mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  10. take the marinated raw banana and coat in rava.  !
  11. deep fry in hot oil keeping the flame on medium.  !
  12. make sure to not touch the kabab pieces for at least 1 minute. else there are chances for rava to disintegrate.  !
  13. stir occasionally, and fry on medium flame until the banana turns golden brown and crisp.  !
  14. drain off over a kitchen towel to remove excess oil.  !
  15. finally, enjoy **Raw Banana Fish Fry** with green chutney.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to slice the banana of uniform thickness, else the cooking time will vary.
  * also, the masala is really spicy, so adjust the spiciness to your choice.
  * instead of lemon juice you can also use tamarind pulp for sourness.
  * finally, **Raw Banana Fish Fry** tastes great when served hot, crispy, and spicy.

# Recipe 97
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/heerekai-dosa-recipe-ridge-gourd-dosa/

### heerekai dosa video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## recipe card for ridge gourd dosa recipe:
!

## heerekai dosa recipe | ridge gourd dosa recipe | beerakaya dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy heerekai dosa recipe | ridge gourd dosa recipe | beerakaya dosa
5 from 227 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Soaking Time 4 hours hrs
Total Time 4 hours hrs 40 minutes mins
Course dosa
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 4 dosa
Calories 294 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for soaking
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp methi
  * ‚ñ¢ 7 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for soaking

#### for grinding:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup coconut
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ small ball sized tamarind
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 large ridge gourd
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak 1 cup rice, 2 tbsp urad dal, ¬Ω tsp methi and 7 dried red chilli for 4 hours.
  * drain off the water and transfer to the mixi.
  * add ¬Ω cup coconut, 2 tbsp coriander seeds and 1 tbsp cumin.
  * also, add ¬º cup jaggery, small ball sized tamarind, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt.
  * blend to smooth paste adding water as required.
  * transfer the batter into a large bowl. this batter is called as uppu puli dose batter or uppu huli dosa batter.
  * now take 1 large ridge gourd and peel the skin of it.
  * slice the ridge gourd to medium thickness. you can keep it slightly thin if you wish.
  * now dip the heerekai slice into batter and place on tawa.
  * start placing the slices forming a circle dosa.
  * add 1 tsp oil and cover the dosa and cook on a medium flame for 2 minutes.
  * once the dosa is cooked from the bottom, flip over and roast.
  * roast both the sides until the dosa is cooked completely.
  * finally, enjoy heerekai dosa with coconut oil or butter.

### Nutrition
Calories: 294kcalCarbohydrates: 57gProtein: 6gFat: 5gSaturated Fat: 3gSodium: 592mgPotassium: 147mgFiber: 4gSugar: 13gVitamin A: 71IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 53mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make heerekai dosa with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak 1 cup rice, 2 tbsp urad dal, ¬Ω tsp methi and 7 dried red chilli for 4 hours. !
  2. drain off the water and transfer to the mixi. !
  3. add ¬Ω cup coconut, 2 tbsp coriander seeds and 1 tbsp cumin. !
  4. also, add ¬º cup jaggery, small ball sized tamarind, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt. !
  5. blend to smooth paste adding water as required. !
  6. transfer the batter into a large bowl. this batter is called as uppu puli dose batter or uppu huli dosa batter. !
  7. now take 1 large ridge gourd and peel the skin of it. !
  8. slice the ridge gourd to medium thickness. you can keep it slightly thin if you wish. !
  9. now dip the heerekai slice into batter and place on tawa. !
  10. start placing the slices forming a circle dosa. !
  11. add 1 tsp oil and cover the dosa and cook on a medium flame for 2 minutes. !
  12. once the dosa is cooked from the bottom, flip over and roast. !
  13. roast both the sides until the dosa is cooked completely. !
  14. finally, enjoy **heerekai dosa** with coconut oil or butter. !

## notes:
  * firstly, the batter of dosa must be the balance of spiciness, sourness and sweetness.
  * also, you can use onion, tomato, methi leaves, brinjal in place of ridge gourd.
  * additionally, cooking the dosa in coconut oil will enhance the flavour.
  * finally, **heerekai dosa recipe** doesn‚Äôt need any side dish, however, tastes great when served with coconut oil or butter.

## recipe card for mangalore bajji recipe:
!

## goli baje recipe | mangalore bajji | how to make goli baje recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy goli baje recipe | mangalore bajji | how to make goli baje recipe
5 from 199 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Resting Time 3 hours hrs
Total Time 3 hours hrs 25 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine udupi
Servings 25 pieces

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup maida / plain flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp baking soda
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup buttermilk
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coconut, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 1¬Ω cup maida, ¬º tsp baking soda, pinch hing and ¬æ tsp salt.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * now add 1 cup buttermilk. you can alternatively use curd.
  * mix well with your hand in one direction.
  * beat the batter making sure to incorporate air well.
  * now add 2 tbsp curry leaves, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coconut.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * cover and rest for 3 hours for best results.
  * after 3 hours, mix the batter again.
  * now dip your hand in cold water and pinch a small ball sized batter.
  * drop it in hot oil keeping the flame on medium.
  * stir and fry uniformly on medium flame.
  * drain off the goli baje once it turns golden brown and crisp.
  * finally, goli baje is ready to enjoy with coconut chutney.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make goli baje with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 1¬Ω cup maida, ¬º tsp baking soda, pinch hing and ¬æ tsp salt. !
  2. mix well making sure everything is well combined. !
  3. now add 1 cup buttermilk. you can alternatively use curd. !
  4. mix well with your hand in one direction. !
  5. beat the batter making sure to incorporate air well. !
  6. now add 2 tbsp curry leaves, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coconut. !
  7. mix well making sure everything is well combined. !
  8. cover and rest for 3 hours for best results. !
  9. after 3 hours, mix the batter again. !
  10. now dip your hand in cold water and pinch a small ball sized batter. !
  11. drop it in hot oil keeping the flame on medium. !
  12. stir and fry uniformly on medium flame. !
  13. drain off the goli baje once it turns golden brown and crisp. !
  14. finally, **goli baje** is ready to enjoy with . !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to beat the batter well, else the goli baje will be chewy.
  * also, using sour buttermilk will yield good results.
  * additionally, fry on medium flame else the bajji will remain raw from inside.
  * finally, **goli baje recipe** tastes great when served instantly.

# Recipe 99
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/paneer-ghee-roast-recipe-veg-ghee-roast/

### paneer ghee roast video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for paneer ghee roast recipe:
!

## paneer ghee roast recipe | veg ghee roast recipe | how to make paneer roast
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy paneer ghee roast recipe | veg ghee roast recipe | how to make paneer roast
5 from 187 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Course Appetizer, Side Dish
Cuisine mangalore
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for masala paste:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp methi / fenugreek
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp fennel / saunf
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 clove garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp tamarind extract
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup water

#### for roasting:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 15 cubes

#### for ghee roast:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp , whisked
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp jaggery

### Instructions 
  * firstly, to prepare masala paste heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 5 dried red chill, 1 tbsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin, ¬º tsp methi, ¬Ω tsp fennel and ¬Ω tsp pepper.
  * roast on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * further, add 4 clove garlic and saute slightly without burning.
  * transfer the spices into a blender and allow to cool completely.
  * also add 2 tbsp tamarind extract and ¬º cup water.
  * blend to smooth paste. masala paste is ready, keep aside.
  * in another pan heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 15 cubes paneer.
  * roast on low to medium flame or until it turns golden brown. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee and add ¬Ω onion and few curry leaves.
  * saute until onions shrink slightly.
  * further add ¬º tsp turmeric and saute well.
  * now add in the prepared masala paste and cook well.
  * saute and cook well for at least 10-15 minutes or until ghee separates.
  * add in 2 tbsp curd and saute well until well combined.
  * furthermore, add ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp jaggery. mix well.
  * now add in roasted paneer and cook for a minute.
  * finally, garnish with few curry leaves and enjoy paneer ghee roast with roti or dosa.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make veg ghee roast with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, to prepare masala paste heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 5 dried red chill, 1 tbsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin, ¬º tsp methi, ¬Ω tsp fennel and ¬Ω tsp pepper. !
  2. roast on low flame until the spices turn aromatic. !
  3. further, add 4 clove garlic and saute slightly without burning. !
  4. transfer the spices into a blender and allow to cool completely. !
  5. also add 2 tbsp tamarind extract and ¬º cup water. !
  6. blend to smooth paste. masala paste is ready, keep aside. !
  7. in another pan heat 1 tsp ghee and roast 15 cubes paneer. !
  8. roast on low to medium flame or until it turns golden brown. keep aside. !
  9. in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee and add ¬Ω onion and few curry leaves. !
  10. saute until onions shrink slightly. !
  11. further add ¬º tsp turmeric and saute well. !
  12. now add in the prepared masala paste and cook well. !
  13. saute and cook well for at least 10-15 minutes or until ghee separates. !
  14. add in 2 tbsp curd and saute well until well combined. !
  15. furthermore, add ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp jaggery. mix well. !
  16. now add in roasted paneer and cook for a minute. !
  17. finally, garnish with few curry leaves and enjoy **paneer ghee roast** with roti or dosa. !

## notes:
  * firstly, adding jaggery will balance the sourness and spiciness.
  * also, you can prepare masala before in hand and saute with paneer just before serving.
  * additionally, remove the seeds to reduce the spiciness of ghee roast.
  * finally, fresh  tastes great while preparing **paneer ghee roast.**

## gadbad ice cream recipe | gudbud ice cream | gadi bidi ice cream
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy gadbad ice cream recipe | gudbud ice cream | gadi bidi ice cream
5 from 18 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 3 minutes mins
Total Time 3 minutes mins
Course Dessert
Cuisine mangalore, udupi
Servings 1 Serving

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 scoop 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp grapes, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp mango, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp apple, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 scoop strawberry ice cream
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp strawberry jelly
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp nuts, cashew, almonds, pistachios
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp tutti frutti
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 scoop mango ice cream
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cherry

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a tall glass take 1 scoop vanilla ice cream.
  * add 1 tbsp grapes, 1 tbsp mango and 1 tbsp apple.
  * top with 1 scoop strawberry ice cream.
  * further, add 1 tbsp strawberry jelly.
  * now add 2 tbsp nuts and 1 tbsp tutti frutti.
  * finally, add 1 scoop mango ice cream and garnish gadbad ice cream with a cherry.

## how to make gudbud ice cream with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a tall glass take 1 scoop vanilla ice cream. !
  2. add 1 tbsp grapes, 1 tbsp mango and 1 tbsp apple. feel free to add fruits of your choice. !
  3. top with 1 scoop strawberry ice cream. !
  4. further, add 1 tbsp strawberry jelly. !
  5. now add 2 tbsp nuts and 1 tbsp tutti frutti. !
  6. finally, add 1 scoop mango ice cream and garnish **gadbad ice cream** with a cherry. !

## notes:
  * firstly, use any 3 flavoured of ice cream of your choice. vanilla, pista and mango flavour goes well.
  * also, add fruits of your choice to make gadbad richer.
  * additionally, dry fruit gadbad can be prepared by adding just dry fruits and ice creams.
  * finally, **gadbad ice cream recipe** tastes great when served in a tall glass.

# Recipe 101
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/rice-halbai-sweet-recipe/

### halbai sweet video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for halbai sweet recipe:
!

## halbai recipe | halbai sweet recipe | how to make rice halbai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy halbai recipe | halbai sweet recipe | how to make rice halbai
5 from 29 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Soaking Time 2 hours hrs
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 21 pieces
Calories 86 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup coconut
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak 1 cup rice for 2 hours.
  * drain off the water and transfer to the blender.
  * add 1 cup coconut and ¬º cup water.
  * blend to smooth paste, keep aside.
  * in a large kadai take 1 cup jaggery and add 2¬æ cup water.
  * stir well until the jaggery dissolves completely.
  * add in prepared rice coconut paste, ¬º tsp salt and stir well.
  * stir until the mixture is well combined without forming lumps.
  * further, add 2 tbsp ghee and mix well.
  * the mixture will start to turn glossy and separates the pan after 15 minutes.
  * level up spreading uniformly. rest for 30 minutes or until it sets completely.
  * after 30 minutes, slowly unmould the halbai.
  * finally, garnish with cashew and enjoy halbai or rice halwa with ghee during nagarpanchami festival.

### Video

### Nutrition
Calories: 86kcalCarbohydrates: 17gProtein: 1gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 1gSodium: 31mgPotassium: 24mgFiber: 1gSugar: 10gVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 7mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make halbai recipe with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak 1 cup rice for 2 hours. !
  2. drain off the water and transfer to the blender. !
  3. add 1 cup coconut and ¬º cup water. !
  4. blend to smooth paste, keep aside. !
  5. in a large kadai take 1 cup jaggery and add 2¬æ cup water. !
  6. stir well until the jaggery dissolves completely. strain off the jaggery water if there is any impurities. !
  7. add in prepared rice coconut paste, ¬º tsp salt and stir well. !
  8. stir until the mixture is well combined without forming lumps. !
  9. continue to stir keeping the flame on medium. !
  10. the mixture starts to thicken after 10 minutes. !
  11. further, add 2 tbsp ghee and mix well. !
  12. the mixture will start to turn glossy and separates the pan after 15 minutes. !
  13. once it starts to hold the shape, turn off the flame. !
  14. add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and mix well. !
  15. transfer to a tray (width: 15 cm, height: 6 cm, length: 17 cm). make sure to grease the tray with ghee to avoid sticking and line butter paper at the bottom of the tray. !
  16. level up spreading uniformly. !
  17. rest for 30 minutes or until it sets completely. !
  18. after 30 minutes, slowly unmould the halbai. cut to the desired shape. make sure to grease the knife with ghee to prevent from sticking. !
  19. finally, garnish with cashew and enjoy**halbai** or **rice halwa** with  during nagarpanchami festival. !

## notes:
  * firstly, use 1:3 proportion of rice and water ratio to get a perfect consistency.
  * also, traditionally, the akki halbai recipe is set over banana leaf instead of a tray.
  * additionally, if you are looking to prepare raagi halbai to replace rice with raagi.
  * finally, **halbai recipe** stays good for 2 days when refrigerated.

# Recipe 102
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/potato-curry-recipe-masala-dosa-aloo-bhaji-masala-dosa/

### potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa recipe card:
!

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
5 from 187 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine Indian
Servings 4 servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 potatoes, boiled
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, thinly sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 green chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard seeds / rai
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric powder
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste

### Instructions 
  * boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.
  * finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.
  * in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter.
  * then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.
  * now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.
  * add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.
  * now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.
  * mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins
  * squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.
  * serve aloo bhaji hot with masala dosa's, rice or chapathis.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa photo recipe:
  1. boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.  !
  2. finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.  !
  3. in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter. !
  4. then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.  !
  5. now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.  !
  6. add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.  !
  7. now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.  !
  8. mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins  !
  9. squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.  !
  10. serve aloo bhaji hot with **** ‚Äòs, rice or chapathis.  !

## notes:
  * aloo bhaji taste great when prepared fresh.
  * you can use leftover all bhaji as a stuffing for sandwich. you can also prepare aloo bonda with this.
  * tempering is very important in aloo bhaji, be generous while tempering.

# Recipe 103
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/gulla-bajji-eggplant-brinjal-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## gulla bajji, mattu gulla bajji, eggplant ‚Äì brinjal side dish recipe card below :
!

## gulla bajji recipe | mattu gulla bajji recipe | eggplant - brinjal recipes
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy gulla bajji recipe | mattu gulla bajji recipe | eggplant - brinjal recipes
5 from 22 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course Side Dish
Cuisine south indian
Servings 3 servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 gulla / green brinjal / eggplant
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chillies, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp tamarind pulp
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tbsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 sandige menasu / majjige menasu
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing /asafoetida

### Instructions 
  * firstly, wash the green brinjal and separate the stalk. cut each into 4 pieces (if the brinjal is big, then cut them into 8-12 pieces)
  * further, cook the chopped brinjal in a open pot with sufficient water and salt.
  * as it cooks, the brinjal looses it bright green color and turns pale. when the brinjals pieces look soft, turn off the heat. this might take around 10- 15 minutes.
  * allow the brinjal pieces to come to room temperature. (leaving the water behind. don't discard it).
  * deseed the brinjal if there are too many seeds along with peeling the skin of gulla.
  * once done add tamarind pulp, jaggery and salt in the mixing bowl.
  * now add de-skinned brinjal and start mashing it using your hands.
  * once done add chopped chillies and mix well.
  * further in a small kadai heat ghee and add mustard seeds, urad dal, sandige menasu, curry leaves and hing. allow to splutter.
  * pour the tempering to gulla bajji and give a final mix, before serving. add little water (in which the brinjals were cooked) to get desired consistency.
  * finally, serve the gulla bajji with hot steamed rice.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## step by step gulla bajji, mattu gulla bajji, eggplant ‚Äì brinjal side dish photo recipe :
  1. firstly, wash the green brinjal and separate the stalk. cut each into 4 pieces (if the brinjal is big, then cut them into 8-12 pieces)  !
  2. further, cook the chopped brinjal in a open pot with sufficient water and salt.  !
  3. as it cooks, the brinjal looses it bright green color and turns pale. when the brinjals pieces look soft, turn off the heat. this might take around 10- 15 minutes.  !
  4. allow the brinjal pieces to come to room temperature. (leaving the water behind. don‚Äôt discard it).  !
  5. deseed the brinjal if there are too many seeds along with peeling the skin of gulla.  !
  6. once done add tamarind pulp, jaggery and salt in the mixing bowl.  !
  7. now add de-skinned brinjal and start mashing it using your hands.  !
  8. once done add chopped chillies and mix well.  !
  9. further in a small kadai heat  and add mustard seeds, urad dal, sandige menasu, curry leaves and hing. allow to splutter.  !
  10. pour the tempering to gulla bajji and give a final mix, before serving. add little water (in which the brinjals were cooked) to get desired consistency.  !
  11. finally, serve the **gulla bajji** with hot steamed rice. ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/gulla-bajji-eggplant-brinjal-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2016/01/gulla-bajji-17.jpg>)

## notes:
  * firstly, add 1 tbsp of coconut for thicker consistency.
  * also add chopped onions and coriander leaves at the end for more flavours.
  * additionally, tempering with coconut oil gives a nice aroma to the gojju.
  * finally, **gulla bajji** taste great when prepared with mattu gulla / green eggplant.

## chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
5 from 23 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course beverage
Cuisine indain
Servings 2 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp tea powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cardamoms
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 black pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 half cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ half cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp sugar

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min
  * furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  * also and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.
  * now add milk, sugar.
  * bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.
  * furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.
  * finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any breakfast recipes.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## chai recipe | masala tea recipe | indian masala chai step by step photo recipe:
  1. firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min  !
  2. furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  3. and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.  !
  4. now add milk, sugar.  !
  5. also bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.  !
  6. furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.  !
  7. finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any **.** !

## notes:
  * firstly, if you do not like spices, skip all of them. this will be a plain tea.
  * furthermore, adjust the consistency of your tea with the milk. if you do not like thick masala chai, reduce the quantity of milk and increase the water.
  * also, add milk and get to a boil just before serving.
  * finally, you can use masala tea powder if you do not have spices.

# Recipe 105
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/maddur-vada-recipe-maddur-vade/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Maddur Vada
It is a simple, crisp, and crunchy deep-fried snack recipe made with a combination of rice flour, maida, and rava/sooji. The **Maddur Vada** most commonly known as **Maddur Vade** hails from the small town of Maddur from Karnataka. It is most commonly known to serve as an evening snack with a cup of tea or coffee, but not limited to it. It can also be an ideal side dish for any type of meal, including rasam rice or dal rice combo meal.
There are many different types of **Maddur Vada** , but the most common is made with rice flour, maida, and rava. The taste of this snack is derived from the onions combined with the above dry ingredients. The juice from onions is infused into the dough and tastes great when deep fried in low flame. The same vada can also be made with wheat flour as an alternative to maida. This makes it healthy but may not be a tasty snack. In addition, adding rava helps to make it crisp and crunchy, but optional.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Maddur Vada
!

## Maddur Vada Recipe | Crispy Maddur Vade - Tea Time Snack
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Maddur Vada Recipe | Crispy Maddur Vade - Tea Time Snack
5 from 25 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 15 Servings
Calories 107 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rava, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 onion, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coriander.
  * Add 1 cup rice flour, 1 cup maida and ¬Ω cup rava.
  * Also add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, pinch hing and 1 tsp salt.
  * Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Further, add 2 tbsp hot oil and mix. This helps the vada to turn crunchy.
  * Add water slowly and knead the dough.
  * Do not add more water as the dough needs to be tight.
  * Pinch a ball-sized dough, press and flatten it slightly thick.
  * Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.
  * Do not touch for 2 minutes as there are chances for the vada to break.
  * Stir occasionally and fry both sides until the vada turns golden brown.
  * Drain off to remove excess oil.
  * Finally, enjoy Maddur Vada Recipe with coconut chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 107kcalCarbohydrates: 17gProtein: 4gFat: 3gSaturated Fat: 0.5gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 4mgSodium: 224mgPotassium: 76mgFiber: 1gSugar: 1gVitamin A: 73IUVitamin C: 11mgCalcium: 20mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Maddur Vada with step by step photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 onion, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coriander.  !
  2. Add 1 cup rice flour, 1 cup maida and ¬Ω cup rava.  !
  3. Also add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, pinch hing and 1 tsp salt.  !
  4. Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  5. Further, add 2 tbsp hot oil and mix. This helps the vada to turn crunchy.  !
  6. Add water slowly and knead the dough.  !
  7. Do not add more water as the dough needs to be tight.  !
  8. Pich a ball-sized dough, press and flatten it slightly thick.  !
  9. Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.  !
  10. Do not touch for 2 minutes as there are chances for the vada to break.  !
  11. Stir occasionally and fry both sides until the vada turns golden brown.  !
  12. Drain off to remove excess oil.  !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Maddur Vada Recipe** with coconut chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, the key tip to make crunchy maddur vada is to use as little water as possible.
  * Also, the onions release water, so make sure to add water as required.
  * Additionally, you can add almonds and cashews along with peanuts to get crunchy bites.
  * Finally, **Maddur Vada Recipe** stays crunchy for 3 to 4 days when stored in air tight container.

# Recipe 106
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mysore-rasam-recipe-south-indian-rasam/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Mysore Rasam
It is basically an extension of the traditional South Indian rasam recipe with an additional flavoring spice mixed with coconut. In other words, **Mysore Rasam** is a rasam recipe with slightly thicker in its consistency and also with a blend of spice mix flavors. It is typically served with rice or any flavored rice, but with the spice mix and consistency, it can also be served with dosa and idli recipes too.
Generally, Mysore Rasam was a popular choice, particularly for marriage or any celebrations feast. It was always considered a premium rasam or purpose-based soup. Therefore, the recipe instructions or particularly the Mysore Rasam powder were secretly held by a few chefs. However, this has been now a popular choice for every day to day meals, and hence the recipe started to get distributed.

## Chef Pro Tips:
The recipe is no rocket science and hence less likely to get it wrong. Yet I would like to emphasize on few mandatory or critical tips ‚Äì
  1. **Homemade spice mix** ‚Äì You may easily get store-bought spice mix for this recipe. However, my personal recommendation is to use homemade mix for fresh ingredients.
  2. **Tomato & Tamarind Ratio ‚Äì** The sour taste is mandatory and hence tamarind is mandatory. However, due to the use of tomatoes and their own sourness, you may have to alter the quantity of tamarind.
  3. **Consistency ‚Äì** The consistency of this rasam is slightly thicker when compared to the traditional rasam. Do not make it thin like other rasam as it may lose its taste and flavor.
  4. **Tadka (> "tempering")) ‚Äì** This rasam requires the tadka as a mandatory. Also, give the tempering with ghee and avoid oil.
  5. **Over Boiling ‚Äì** Once the spice mix is added, give it 2 minutes to boil. Do not overboil as it may leave a bitter taste.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe card for Mysore Rasam:
!

## Mysore Rasam Recipe | South Indian Rasam Recipe with Coconut
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Mysore Rasam Recipe | South Indian Rasam Recipe with Coconut
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course rasam
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 5 Servings
Calories 256 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for Mysore rasam powder:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 dried red chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup desiccated coconut

#### for Mysore rasam:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup tamarind extract
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tbsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor dal, cooked
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω tbsp mysore rasam powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions

#### How to make homemade Mysore rasam powder:
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 1 tsp oil. add ¬º cup coriander seeds, ¬º cup chana dal, 1 tbsp cumin, 2 tbsp pepper, 10 dried red chilli powder and few curry leaves.
  * roast on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * add ¬Ω cup desiccated coconut and roast until the coconut turns golden brown.
  * cool completely, and grind to a fine powder. Mysore rasam powder is ready.

#### How to make Mysore rasam recipe:
  * In a large vessel, take 2 tomato, 1 cup tamarind extract, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 3 chilli, few curry leaves, 1 tsp jaggery and ¬æ tbsp salt.
  * Boil for 10 minutes or until the tomatoes turn mushy.
  * Mash the tomato slightly.
  * Now add 4 cup water and 1 cup toor dal. Adjust the consistency as required.
  * Further, add 1¬Ω tbsp Mysore rasam powder and mix well. Adjust the spiciness according to your preferences.
  * Get the rasam to a boil and simmer for 1 minute for the flavour to absorb.
  * Now prepare the tempering, by heating 2 tsp ghee. Add 1 tsp mustard, pinch hing, 2 dried red chilli, few curry leaves.
  * Splutter the tempering and pour over the rasam.
  * Further add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Mysore Rasam Recipe with hot steamed rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 256kcalCarbohydrates: 35gProtein: 11gFat: 10gSaturated Fat: 6gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gTrans Fat: 0.004gCholesterol: 5mgSodium: 1105mgPotassium: 397mgFiber: 12gSugar: 5gVitamin A: 755IUVitamin C: 51mgCalcium: 111mgIron: 4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make South Indian Mysore Rasam:
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 1 tsp oil. add ¬º cup coriander seeds, ¬º cup chana dal, 1 tbsp cumin, 2 tbsp pepper, 10 dried red chili powder, and a few curry leaves.  !
  2. roast on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  3. add ¬Ω cup desiccated coconut and roast until the coconut turns golden brown.  !
  4. cool completely, and grind to a fine powder. Mysore rasam powder is ready.  !

### How to make Mysore rasam recipe:
  1. In a large vessel, take 2 tomato, 1 cup tamarind extract, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 3 chilli, few curry leaves, 1 tsp jaggery and ¬æ tbsp salt.  !
  2. Boil for 10 minutes or until the tomatoes turn mushy.  !
  3. Mash the tomato slightly.  !
  4. Now add 4 cup water and 1 cup toor dal. Adjust the consistency as required.  !
  5. Further, add 1¬Ω tbsp Mysore rasam powder and mix well. Adjust the spiciness according to your preferences.  !
  6. Get the rasam to a boil and simmer for 1 minute for the flavour to absorb.  !
  7. Now prepare the tempering, by heating 2 tsp ghee. Add 1 tsp mustard, pinch hing, 2 dried red chilli, few curry leaves.  !
  8. Splutter the tempering and pour over the rasam.  !
  9. Further add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.  !
  10. Finally, enjoy **Mysore Rasam Recipe** with hot steamed rice.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, if you are preparing the rasam powder in small quantities, then use fresh coconut. else use desiccated coconut.
  * Also, after adding rasam powder, do not over-boil, as it will lose its aroma.
  * Additionally, make sure to boil the tomato and tamarind extract really well.
  * Finally, **Mysore Rasam Recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly spicy.

# Recipe 107
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/thatte-idli-recipe-tatte-idli-plate-idli/

### thatte idli video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## Recipe card for thatte idli recipe:
!

## thatte idli recipe | tatte idli or plate idli | how to make thatte idli
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy thatte idli recipe | tatte idli or plate idli | how to make thatte idli
5 from 210 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south india
Servings 9 Servings

### Ingredients 
cupsgrams
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup idli rice / dosa rice / sona masuri rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup thin poha / avalakki / aval
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for greasing

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large mixing bowl soak 2 cup idli rice for 5 hours. alternatively, use dosa rice / sona masuri rice.
  * in another bowl soak 1 cup urad dal for 3 hours.
  * drain off the water from urad dal and blend to smooth paste adding water as required.
  * transfer the smooth and fluffy batter of urad dal into a large bowl.
  * in the blender take soaked rice and add ¬æ cup of washed thin poha.
  * bend to slightly coarse paste adding water as required.
  * transfer the rice batter to the bowl of urad dal batter.
  * mix well making sure everything is combined well.
  * now cover and rest in warm place for 8-10 hours or till the batter ferments and doubles.
  * after 8 hours, batter doubles indicating well fermented with air pockets present.
  * add 1¬Ω tsp salt to the batter and mix well.
  * mix gently without disturbing the air pockets.
  * now grease the thatte idli plate with oil.
  * scoop the batter into idli plate greased with oil.
  * arrange the idli plate into the stand.
  * steam for 20 minutes on medium flame or till a tooth pick inserted comes out clean.
  * finally, thatte idlis are ready to serve along with chutney and sambar.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make thatte idli with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large mixing bowl soak 2 cup idli rice for 5 hours. alternatively, use dosa rice / sona masuri rice. !
  2. in another bowl soak 1 cup urad dal for 3 hours. !
  3. drain off the water from urad dal and blend to smooth paste adding water as required. !
  4. transfer the smooth and fluffy batter of urad dal into a large bowl. !
  5. in the blender take soaked rice and add ¬æ cup of washed thin poha. !
  6. bend to slightly coarse paste adding water as required. !
  7. transfer the rice batter to the bowl of urad dal batter. !
  8. mix well making sure everything is combined well. !
  9. now cover and rest in warm place for 8-10 hours or till the batter ferments and doubles. !
  10. after 8 hours, batter doubles indicating well fermented with air pockets present. !
  11. add 1¬Ω tsp salt to the batter and mix well. !
  12. mix gently without disturbing the air pockets. !
  13. now grease the thatte idli plate with oil. !
  14. scoop the batter into idli plate greased with oil. !
  15. arrange the idli plate into the stand. !
  16. steam for 20 minutes on medium flame or till a tooth pick inserted comes out clean. !
  17. finally,**thatte** **idlis** are ready to serve along with  and . !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to blend the urad dal paste into a very smooth and fluffy batter.
  * also, grind the rice batter into a slightly coarse consistency.
  * additionally, using idli rice helps to get smooth and fluffy idli.
  * finally, the same **thatte idli** batter can be poured into idli plate to make soft mallige idli.

# Recipe 108
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mysore-bonda-recipe-mysore-bajji/

### mysore bonda video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for mysore bonda recipe:
!

## mysore bonda recipe | mysore bajji recipe | instant bonda recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy mysore bonda recipe | mysore bajji recipe | instant bonda recipe
4.84 from 25 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Resting Time 4 hours hrs
Total Time 4 hours hrs 30 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 20 pieces
Calories 61 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp baking soda
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup maida / plain flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coconut, shredded
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 1 cup curd, ¬æ tsp salt and 1 tsp baking soda.
  * mix well until the curd turns frothy.
  * now add 2 cup maida and start to mix gently.
  * adding more curd if required, start to beat in 1 direction.
  * the batter will turn elastic texture.
  * now add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coconut, 2 tbsp coriander and 1 tsp cumin.
  * mix well combining everything well.
  * now, cover and rest for 4 hours.
  * after 4 hours, the batter will turn more soft and fluffy.
  * beat it further for a minute.
  * dip your hand in the water and pinch a ball sized batter.
  * drop in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.
  * stir and fry until the bonda turns golden brown and crisp.
  * finally, drain off the mysore bajji and enjoy with chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 61kcalCarbohydrates: 11gProtein: 3gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 1gSodium: 144mgPotassium: 42mgFiber: 1gSugar: 1gVitamin A: 56IUVitamin C: 8mgCalcium: 22mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make mysore bajji with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 1 cup curd, ¬æ tsp salt and 1 tsp baking soda. !
  2. mix well until the curd turns frothy. !
  3. now add 2 cup maida and start to mix gently. !
  4. adding more curd if required, start to beat in 1 direction. !
  5. the batter will turn elastic texture. !
  6. now add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coconut, 2 tbsp coriander and 1 tsp cumin. !
  7. mix well combining everything well. !
  8. now, cover and rest for 4 hours. !
  9. after 4 hours, the batter will turn more soft and fluffy. !
  10. beat it further for a minute. !
  11. dip your hand in the water and pinch a ball sized batter. !
  12. drop in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium. !
  13. stir and fry until the bonda turns golden brown and crisp. !
  14. finally, drain off the **mysore bajji** and enjoy with chutney. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to beat the batter really well. else the bajji will be dense.
  * also, if your bajji is hard then add a pinch of baking soda and mix the batter.
  * additionally, fry on medium flame else the bonda will not get cooked from inside.
  * finally, **mysore bonda** or**mysore bajji recipe** tastes great when served hot.

# Recipe 109
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/potato-curry-recipe-masala-dosa-aloo-bhaji-masala-dosa/

### potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa recipe card:
!

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
5 from 187 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine Indian
Servings 4 servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 potatoes, boiled
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, thinly sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 green chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard seeds / rai
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric powder
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste

### Instructions 
  * boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.
  * finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.
  * in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter.
  * then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.
  * now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.
  * add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.
  * now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.
  * mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins
  * squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.
  * serve aloo bhaji hot with masala dosa's, rice or chapathis.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa photo recipe:
  1. boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.  !
  2. finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.  !
  3. in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter. !
  4. then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.  !
  5. now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.  !
  6. add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.  !
  7. now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.  !
  8. mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins  !
  9. squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.  !
  10. serve aloo bhaji hot with **** ‚Äòs, rice or chapathis.  !

## notes:
  * aloo bhaji taste great when prepared fresh.
  * you can use leftover all bhaji as a stuffing for sandwich. you can also prepare aloo bonda with this.
  * tempering is very important in aloo bhaji, be generous while tempering.

# Recipe 110

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card of chai recipe | masala tea recipe| indian masala:
!

## chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
5 from 23 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course beverage
Cuisine indain
Servings 2 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp tea powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cardamoms
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 black pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 half cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ half cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp sugar

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min
  * furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  * also and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.
  * now add milk, sugar.
  * bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.
  * furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.
  * finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any breakfast recipes.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## chai recipe | masala tea recipe | indian masala chai step by step photo recipe:
  1. firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min  !
  2. furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  3. and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.  !
  4. now add milk, sugar.  !
  5. also bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.  !
  6. furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.  !
  7. finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any **.** !

## notes:
  * firstly, if you do not like spices, skip all of them. this will be a plain tea.
  * furthermore, adjust the consistency of your tea with the milk. if you do not like thick masala chai, reduce the quantity of milk and increase the water.
  * also, add milk and get to a boil just before serving.
  * finally, you can use masala tea powder if you do not have spices.

# Recipe 111

## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar recipe card:**
!

## mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
HEBBARS KITCHEN
mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course sambar
Cuisine south indian
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor daal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 to matoes
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chillies
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

#### seasoning ingredients
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω split urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.
  * once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.
  * meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.
  * bullet idli sambar
  * furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.
  * now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.
  * add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.
  * additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.
  * bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  * furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.
  * prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.
  * finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with bullet idli's dipped in this sambar.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar step by step photo recipe:**
  1. firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.  !
  2. once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.  !
  3. meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.  !
  4. furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.  !
  5. now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.  !
  6. also add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.  !
  7. additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.  !
  8. bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  9. furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.  !
  10. prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.  !
  11. finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with **** dipped in this sambar.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, idlis taste great when dipped in sambar for atleast 5 minutes.
  * furthermore, you can add **** if you wish to make it more spicy.
  * moreover, mash the dal properly so that the consistency is maintained.
  * finally, ad a tsp of ghee to make it more flavourful.
