# Recipe 112
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | easy paddu recipe card below:
!

## guliappa recipe / paddu recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
guliyappa recipe / paddu recipe
5 from 188 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 12 hours hrs
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 12 hours hrs 30 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 30 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal / split black lentils
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup sona masuri rice / chawal / dosa rice
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp menthe / fenugreek seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup paper avalakki / beaten rice / poha
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for greasing tawa

### Instructions 
  * soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl and soak for 5 hours.
  * first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter.
  * transfer to a large vessel.
  * now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter.
  * now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender.
  * transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well.
  * cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours.
  * the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented.
  * mix the batter slightly.
  * take required batter in a different bowl.
  * finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.
  * add fried onions and ginger, chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves and mix well.
  * also add in salt and mix the batter well.
  * now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.
  * reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.
  * once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.
  * your paddu recipe is ready


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## easy paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | paddu recipe with step by step photo recipe:
  1. soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl. add in enough water and soak for 5 hours. !
  2. first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter. add water if required to make a smooth paste. !
  3. transfer to a large vessel. and keep aside !
  4. now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter. !
  5. now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender. and grind to a smooth thick paste. !
  6. transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well. !
  7. cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours. !
  8. the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented. !
  9. mix the batter slightly. !
  10. take required batter in a different bowl.
  11. finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa.jpg>)
  12. fry the onions and ginger with a table spoon of oil till they turn translucent.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa-11.jpg>)
  13. now add fried onions and ginger along with finely chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves to the batter and mix well.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa31.jpg>)
  14. also add in salt and mix the batter well. ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa4.jpg>)
  15. heat the guliyappa pan and a drop of oil in all moulds.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa5.jpg>)
  16. now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa6.jpg>)
  17. reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa8.jpg>)
  18. once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa10.jpg>)
  19. remove the cooked guliyappas and serve hot with**** or chutney powder.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa12.jpg>)

## notes:
  * first of all, if your guliyappa is not getting golden brown, add some sugar.
  * in addition, adjust the consistency of the batter by adding required water.
  * furthermore, to make it little spicy, add some chopped chilli.
  * finally, skip the masala step and pour the batter directly to moulds, but these onion masala enhances the taste of guliyappa.

# Recipe 113
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mini-idli-recipe-bullet-idli-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for mini idli recipe | idli batter recipe | button idli recipe:
!

## mini idli recipe| bullet idli recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
mini idli recipe| bullet idli recipe
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 12 hours hrs
Cook Time 8 minutes mins
Total Time 12 hours hrs 8 minutes mins
Course Main
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### ingredients for bullet idli batter
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup idli rava - cream of rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal/spilt & skinned black gram lentils
  * ‚ñ¢ salt as required
  * ‚ñ¢ water for soaking
  * ‚ñ¢ coconut oil to grease

### Instructions

#### mini idli batter recipe:
  * firstly, soak the urad dal in enough water for 4-5 hours.
  * furthermore, drain the water from the urad dal and keep it aside.
  * take the urad dal in the wet grinder / mixer. add some of the urad dal strained water and grind.
  * however, if the batter appears too thick, add some water. grind to a smooth batter.
  * after that pour in a non reactive deep pan or pot.
  * furthermore, rinse the idli rava till the water runs clear of the starch.
  * drain the water well from idli rava by squeezing excess water from idli rava.
  * mix the squeezed idli rava to the batter well.
  * make sure there are enough space for batter to raise when fermented.
  * cover and ferment in warm place for atleast 6 - 8 hours.
  * you can see the batter has raised slightly indicating its well fermented.
  * mix the batter slightly and add salt to taste.

#### steaming mini idli recipe:
  * brush idli moulds with oil.
  * pour the batter in the idli moulds.
  * additionally, place the idli stand in the steamer containing with some boiling water.
  * furthermore, cover with a lid and steam the idlis for 10 minutes.
  * finally, arrange the mini idlis then add more sambar on top.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## mini idli recipe | idli batter recipe | bullet idli step by step photo recipe:

### mini idli batter recipe:
  1. firstly, soak the urad dal in enough water for 4-5 hours. !
  2. furthermore, drain the water from the urad dal and keep it aside. we will use some of this water for grinding the idlis.
  3. take the urad dal in the wet grinder / mixer. add some of the urad dal strained water and grind.  !
  4. however, if the batter appears too thick, add some water. grind to a smooth batter.  !
  5. after that pour in a non reactive deep pan or pot.  !
  6. furthermore, rinse the idli rava till the water runs clear of the starch.  !
  7. drain the water well from idli rava by squeezing excess water from idli rava.  !
  8. mix the squeezed idli rava to the batter well. always mix the batter with your hand to make sure there are no lumps in the batter  !
  9. make sure there are enough space for batter to raise when fermented. !
  10. cover and ferment in warm place for atleast 6 ‚Äì 8 hours. see notes section for tips n fermentation.
  11. you can see the batter has raised slightly indicating its well fermented. !
  12. mix the batter slightly and add salt to taste. !

### steaming mini idli recipe:
  1. brush idli moulds with oil.
  2. pour the batter in the idli moulds. !
  3. additionally, place the idli stand in the steamer containing with some boiling water. !
  4. furthermore, cover with a lid and steam the idlis for 10 minutes. !
  5. finally, arrange the mini idlis then add more **** on top. drizzle ghee. serve hot with  and .  !

## notes:
  * firstly, you can use pressure cooker to steam idlis. but don‚Äôt put the vent weight / whistle.
  * furthermore, do not add salt for the entire batter, if you want to store batter for long time.
  * moreover, always store the batter in airtight container in refrigerator.
  * most noteworthy, do not add too much water while grinding the batter. add only required amount.
  * most of all, if you live in cold countries then cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours.
  * if you live in a warmer place**,** then ferment for 8 hour max.
  * finally, i usually keep my batter in pre heated oven (switch off the oven though) to ferment idli batter well. if possible try to preheat oven ever 3-4 hours.

# Recipe 114
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/honey-chilli-potato-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## About Honey Chilli Potato
This is an easy fusion recipe, prepared with crispy potato fries and lip-smacking Indo-Chinese sauces and condiments. **Honey Chilli Potatoes** are typically served as a starter or as an appetiser just before any meal for lunch and dinner. They are the most common street snack and are served as a side with other Indo-Chinese meals like fried rice or noodles, but they are not limited to these. They can also be served as a main meal or as a stuffing between rotis and wraps.
The recipe for **Honey Chilli Potato** is straightforward, yet there are many variations to this simple recipe. Typically, it is prepared with freshly sliced potatoes and deep-fried till crisp before making an Indo-Chinese snack. However, it can be made with leftover fries or wedges for the same taste and flavour. The same recipe can also be made with frozen fries or wedges. In addition, the same recipe can be made with other types of veggies like baby corn, mushrooms, and paneer.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Honey Chilli Potato
!

## Honey Chilli Potato Recipe - Street Style with Secret Tips
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Honey Chilli Potato Recipe | Crispy Honey Chilli Potato‚ÄîStreet Style**
5 from 197 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine indo chinese
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 223 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for boiling potato:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 potato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ water
  * ‚ñ¢ salt

#### for frying:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp corn flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper powder
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

#### for sauce:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves garlic, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 spring onion, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω capsicum, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp soy sauce
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp chilli sauce
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp corn flour slurry
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp honey

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, peel the skin of the potato and chop it into the size of french fries. Soak in water to remove starch.
  * Drain off the water and half boil in salt water for 3 minutes.
  * Drain off and cool completely.
  * In a large bowl, take half-boiled potato.
  * Add ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 tbsp corn flour, 2 tbsp maida, and ¬Ω tsp pepper powder.
  * Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.
  * Fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.
  * Stir occasionally, and fry till the potato is crunchy and golden brown.
  * Drain off and keep aside.
  * In a large wok, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 inch ginger, 4 cloves garlic, 2 chilies, 2 spring onions, and 1 tsp sesame. Stir fry until they turn aromatic.
  * Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω capsicum and stir fry on high flame.
  * Now add 2 tbsp tomato sauce, 2 tbsp soy sauce, 2 tbsp vinegar, 2 tsp chilli sauce, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, and ¬Ω tsp salt. Stir fry on high flame till the sauce turns aromatic.
  * Further, add 3 tbsp corn flour slurry and mix well making sure it turns glossy.
  * Add in fried potato, 2 tbsp honey, 1 tsp honey, and spring onion.
  * Mix well till the sauces are coated well. Do not cook more as it turns soggy.
  * Finally, enjoy Honey Chilli Potato Recipe topped with toasted sesame.

### Nutrition
Calories: 223kcalCarbohydrates: 31gProtein: 4gFat: 10gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 6gTrans Fat: 0.04gSodium: 1539mgPotassium: 298mgFiber: 2gSugar: 17gVitamin A: 1268IUVitamin C: 74mgCalcium: 38mgIron: 2mg

## How to Make Honey Chilli Potato with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, peel the skin of the potato and chop it into the size of french fries. Soak in water to remove starch. !
  2. Drain off the water and half boil in salt water for 3 minutes. Drain off and cool completely. In a large bowl, take half-boiled potato. !
  3. Add ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 tbsp corn flour, 2 tbsp maida, and ¬Ω tsp pepper powder. !
  4. Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined. !
  5. Fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium. !
  6. Stir occasionally, and fry till the potato is crunchy and golden brown. Drain off and keep aside. !
  7. In a large wok, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 inch ginger, 4 cloves garlic, 2 chilies, 2 spring onions, and 1 tsp sesame. Stir fry until they turn aromatic. !
  8. Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω capsicum and stir fry on high flame. !
  9. Now add 2 tbsp tomato sauce, 2 tbsp soy sauce, 2 tbsp vinegar, 2 tsp chilli sauce, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, and ¬Ω tsp salt. Stir fry on high flame till the sauce turns aromatic. !
  10. Further, add 3 tbsp corn flour slurry and mix well making sure it turns glossy. !
  11. Add in fried potato, 2 tbsp honey, 1 tsp honey, and spring onion. !
  12. Mix well till the sauces are coated well. Do not cook more as it turns soggy. !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Honey Chilli Potato Recipe** topped with toasted sesame. !

## Notes
  * Firstly, fry the potatoes till they turn crispy; otherwise, they won‚Äôt taste good.
  * Also, adjust the amount of honey depending on the sweetness you are looking for.
  * Additionally, do not cook once honey is added, as the flavor of honey will be lost.
  * Finally, **Honey Chilli Potato** **Recipe** tastes great when served hot and crispy.

# Recipe 115

####

## About Kalakand Sweet
Milk Kalakand, also known as **Kalakand Mithai Sweet** , is an extremely popular and premium sweet from North India or Eastern Part Indian cuisine. It is made with Milk and sugar. Milk Kalakand, also known as Kalakand Mithai Sweet, is an extension of the popular Bengali sweet rasgulla or Rasmali but with a different texture and shape. It is most commonly made during the festival season, like Diwali and Ganesh Chaturthi, but it is not limited to it. These barfi-shaped sweets can also be served to friends and family as gifts for any occasion.
There are many different ways to prepare a simple milk-based **Kalakand Sweet**. The most common way is to prepare fresh cow‚Äôs milk with added sugar. The same recipe can also be made with condensed milk and milk powder; this is the easiest way. Further, the recipe can also be made with grated paneer and sugar syrup. Generally, they are prepared with either paneer or chenna, but they can also be extended to other sweets. In addition, the variations include adding fruit puree, such as mango kalakand, apple, orange, and even any type of berries.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Kalakand Sweet
!

## Kalakand Sweet Recipe | Kalakand Milk Cake Barfi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy kalakand sweet recipe | kalakand mithai | kalakand milk cake barfi
3.50 from 2 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Resting Time 8 hours hrs
Total Time 8 hours hrs 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 15 pieces
Calories 47 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 litre milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp vinegar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp nuts, chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large vessel take 2-litre milk and get to a boil.
  * once the milk comes to a boil add 2 tbsp vinegar and mix well.
  * add vinegar until the milk curdles.
  * drain off the milk and rinse with water. rinsing with water helps to remove sourness.
  * now squeeze off the water and transfer to a large plate.
  * mash the paneer to smooth texture. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai, heat 1-litre milk.
  * stir and get to a boil.
  * continue to boil until the milk reduces to half.
  * add ¬æ cup sugar and mix until the sugar dissolves.
  * further, add prepared paneer and mix well.
  * continue to cook until the mixture starts to separate the pan.
  * further, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and mix well.
  * now transfer the mixture to the tray and level up.
  * top with chopped nuts and press gently.
  * rest for 8 hours or until it sets completely.
  * cut into pieces and is ready to serve.
  * finally, enjoy kalakand recipe with chopped nuts for a week when refrigerated.

### Nutrition
Calories: 47kcalCarbohydrates: 10gProtein: 1gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 1mgSodium: 1mgPotassium: 9mgFiber: 1gSugar: 10gVitamin A: 1IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 2mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Kalakand Sweet with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, take 2 litres of milk in a large vessel and get to a boil.  !
  2. Once the milk comes to a boil, add 2 tbsp of vinegar and mix well.  !
  3. Add vinegar until the milk curdles.  !
  4. Drain off the milk and rinse with water. Rinsing with water helps to remove sourness.  !
  5. Now squeeze off the water and transfer to a large plate.  !
  6. Mash the paneer to smooth the texture. Keep aside.  !
  7. In a large Kadai, heat 1 litre of milk.  !
  8. Stir and get to a boil.  !
  9. Continue to boil until the milk is reduced to half.  !
  10. Add ¬æ cup sugar and mix until the sugar dissolves.  !
  11. Furthermore, add prepared paneer and mix well.  !
  12. Continue to cook until the mixture starts to separate from the pan.  !
  13. Furthermore, add ¬º tsp cardamom powder and mix well.  !
  14. Now, transfer the mixture to the tray and level up.  !
  15. Top with chopped nuts and press gently.  !
  16. Rest for 8 hours or until it sets ultimately.  !
  17. Cut into pieces and ready to serve.  !
  18. Finally, enjoy the **kalakand recipe** with chopped nuts for a week when refrigerated.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, use whole cream milk as it yields more paneer.
  * Also, adjust the amount of sugar to your taste.
  * Additionally, adding nuts is optional. However, crunchy bites will make it flavourful.
  * Finally, the **Kalakand recipe** tastes great when prepared and served fresh.

# Recipe 116
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/methi-malai-paneer-recipe-paneer-methi/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

## About Methi Malai Paneer
An easy yet flavoured and creamy dhaba-style paneer gravy curry recipe made with fenugreek leaves and cooking cream. **Methi Malai paneer** is a popular curry in restaurants or dhabas, it can also be an ideal choice for lunch and dinner. It is a unique North Indian curry that offers creamy and mild sweetness with a hint of bitter taste. Thus making it a perfect choice for both rice and any type of bread and rotis.
There are many different methods to make this creamy **Methi Malai Paneer** Recipe. The most common way is to make it with paneer cubes, fresh fenugreek leaves and onion tomato base. However, the same curry can also be made with paneer grate like Bhurji gravy. In addition, the gravy base can be extended further by adding vegetables like mushrooms, sweet corn, peas and even soya nuggets.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Methi Malai Paneer
!

## Methi Malai Paneer Curry Recipe - Dhaba Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Methi Malai Paneer Recipe | Methi Paneer Recipe | Paneer Methi Malai**
5 from 202 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 15 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 45 minutes mins
Course curries
Cuisine north indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 156 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bunch methi / fenugreek leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 black cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup tomato puree
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ 20 cubes  
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cream
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, take 1 bunch methi leaves in a large bowl.
  * Add 1 tsp salt and soak for 15 minutes.
  * Squeeze off the water, this helps to remove bitterness from methi.
  * Chop them finely making sure the methi is clean. Keep aside.
  * In a kaai, heat 2 tbsp ghee and saute chopped methi.
  * Once the methi turns aromatic, keep it aside.
  * Add 2 tbsp oil, pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 black cardamom and 4 cloves. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Now add 1 cup tomato puree, 1 tsp salt and cook well.
  * Cook until the oil separates from the sides.
  * Add 2 cup hot water and adjust the consistency.
  * Further add 20 cubes paneer, 2 tbsp cream and mix gently.
  * Cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed.
  * Now add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Methi Malai Paneer Recipe with roti and rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 156kcalCarbohydrates: 11gProtein: 3gFat: 12gSaturated Fat: 7gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 3gCholesterol: 31mgSodium: 646mgPotassium: 406mgFiber: 3gSugar: 5gVitamin A: 1048IUVitamin C: 9mgCalcium: 72mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Methi Malai Paneer with Step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, take 1 bunch methi leaves in a large bowl.  !
  2. Add 1 tsp salt and soak for 15 minutes.  !
  3. Squeeze off the water, this helps to remove bitterness from methi.  !
  4. Chop them finely making sure the methi is clean. Keep aside.  !
  5. In a kadai, heat 2 tbsp ghee and saute chopped methi.  !
  6. Once the methi turns aromatic, keep it aside.  !
  7. Add 2 tbsp oil, pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 black cardamom and 4 cloves. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  8. Add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.  !
  9. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  10. Now add 1 cup tomato puree, 1 tsp salt and cook well.  !
  11. Cook until the oil separates from the sides.  !
  12. Also, add saute methi and cook well.  !
  13. Add 2 cup hot water and adjust the consistency.  !
  14. Further add 20 cubes paneer, 2 tbsp cream and mix gently.  !
  15. Cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed.  !
  16. Now add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well.  !
  17. Finally, enjoy **Methi Malai Paneer Recipe** with roti and rice.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to pluck only the leaves, as the stems are hard and won‚Äôt taste good.
  * Also, add cream to make the gravy creamy. Do not compromise on it.
  * Additionally, you can cut the paneer into shape of your choice.
  * Finally, **Methi Malai Paneer Recipe** tastes great when made creamy and less spicy.

# Recipe 117
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/bengali-aloo-chop-recipe-alu-chop-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Aloo Chop
A classical Eastern Indian cuisine deep-fried snack recipe prepared with a combination of mashed potatoes, a blend of spice mix and besan batter. **Aloo Chop** , commonly known as **Bengali Potato Fritters** , is a popular West Bengal street food with spicy condiments like green chutney or tomato sauces. It is typically confused with spiced hashbrowns, but this is much more than that. It has a similar shape and texture to batata vada, but the blend of spices and potato mash makes it unique. Also, the shape is flat, like a disc, which is typical of this snack.
A simple **Aloo Chop** or **Alur Chop** snack is prepared in different ways. The most common way is to blend spice mix prepared in advance and mixed with boiled potatoes before deep frying. However, the variations can be quickly introduced based on how the spice mix is ready. Also, deep frying can be varied. You can use shallow, deep, and even air frying techniques. However, deep frying is the most tasty way. Also, the snack is open-ended and can take different types of condiments. It includes,
  * Green Chutney
  * Tamarind Sauce
  * Achar or Pickle
  * Mint Raita or Dip
  * Maggie Hot & Sweet Tomato Ketchup
  * Onion & Tomato mix

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Aloo Chop
!

## Aloo Chop Recipe | Alur Chop | Aloor Chop
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Aloo Chop Recipe | Alur Chop | Aloor Chop
4.79 from 19 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine bengali
Servings 11 Servings
Calories 96 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for masala:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 dried red chilli

#### for batter:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for making batter
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp baking soda

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 boiled potato, mashed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 boiled potato, mashed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kala namak

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, to prepare the masala for chop, dry roast 1 tsp cumin, 1 tbsp coriander seeds and 3 dried red chilli.
  * Roast on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Cool completely, and grind to a fine powder. Keep aside.
  * In a bowl take 1¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Add water as required and prepare a smooth batter. Keep aside.
  * To prepare the stuffing, mash 3 boiled potato and keep aside.
  * In a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp cumin and pinch hing.
  * Also add 2 chilli, ¬Ω onion,1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute well.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 2 boiled potato, ¬Ω tsp salt and mix well.
  * Add prepared masala powder, 2 tbsp coriander, ¬Ω tsp kala namak and mix well.
  * The stuffing is ready. Allow to cool completely.
  * Once the stuffing is cooled, prepare small patties-shaped mixture. Keep aside.
  * To the besan batter add ¬º tsp baking soda and mix well just before frying.
  * Dip the aloo mixture in besan batter coating the batter uniformly.
  * Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.
  * Stir occasionally, and fry on both sides.
  * Fry until the vada turns crispy brown and golden. Drain off.
  * Finally, enjoy Aloo Chop Recipe with chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 96kcalCarbohydrates: 11gProtein: 4gFat: 4gSaturated Fat: 0.3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gTrans Fat: 0.01gSodium: 251mgPotassium: 205mgFiber: 2gSugar: 2gVitamin A: 144IUVitamin C: 14mgCalcium: 21mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Alur Chop with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, to prepare the masala for chop, dry roast 1 tsp cumin, 1 tbsp coriander seeds, and 3 dried red chilli.  !
  2. Roast on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  3. Cool completely, and grind to a fine powder. Keep aside.  !
  4. In a bowl take 1¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  5. Add water as required and prepare a smooth batter. Keep aside.  !
  6. To prepare the stuffing, mash 3 boiled potato and keep aside.  !
  7. In a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp cumin and pinch hing.  !
  8. Also add 2 chilli, ¬Ω onion,1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute well. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 2 boiled potato, ¬Ω tsp salt, and mix well.  !
  9. Add prepared masala powder, 2 tbsp coriander, ¬Ω tsp kala namak, and mix well. The stuffing is ready. Allow to cool completely.  !
  10. Once the stuffing is cooled, prepare small patties-shaped mixture. Keep aside.  !
  11. To the besan batter add ¬º tsp baking soda and mix well just before frying.  !
  12. Dip the aloo mixture in besan batter coating the batter uniformly.  !
  13. Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium. Stir occasionally, and fry on both sides. Fry until the vada turns crispy brown and golden. Drain off.  !
  14. Finally, enjoy **Aloo Chop Recipe** with chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to prepare the masala powder to enhance the flavour of vada.
  * Also, if you make a thick batter, then the coating will be very thick. If the batter is watery, then it will not stick to the mixture.
  * Additionally, fry on medium flame to cook uniformly and make vada crispy.
  * Finally, **Aloo Chop Recipe** tastes great when prepared spicy.

URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/chana-dal-paratha-recipe-dal-ka-paratha/

####

#### 

00:02:12

## About Dal Paratha
It is a popular and healthy lentil-stuffed Indian flatbread recipe from the rich and premium Rajasthani cuisine. **Dal Ka Paratha** , most commonly known as **Moong Dal Paratha** , is known for its texture and the layers it has to offer in each bite. In addition, due to the filling and protein-rich stuffing, it makes it one of the best paratha for lunch boxes and kids tiffin boxes. The bread is typically served with a combination of yoghurt dip/raita and spicy pickle. But it goes very well with different types of North Indian curries, including veg and non-veg.
There are many different ways to make this simple **Dal Paratha** or **lentil paratha recipe**. Mixing the lentil stuffing directly with the wheat or paratha dough is the most common way. This removes the complication of stuffing, rolling and pinning. The other common way is to stuff the lentils into the wheat dough pockets. This may need some hand-eye coordination and may not be easy for beginners. Lastly, the same recipe can be made with other types of lentils or a combination of lentils.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Moong Dal Paratha
!

## dal paratha recipe | dal ka paratha | lentil stuffed paratha recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy dal paratha recipe | dal ka paratha | lentil stuffed paratha recipe
5 from 214 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 3 hours hrs
Cook Time 1 hour hr
Total Time 4 hours hrs
Course paratha
Cuisine north indian
Servings 10 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup chana dal, soaked 3 hours
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric / haldi
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kashmiri red chilli powder / lal mirch powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur / dry mango powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder / jeera powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp ajwain / carom seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 ball sized wheat dough
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for roasting

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in large vessel take 1 cup chana dal, soaked for 3 hours.
  * boil for 15 minutes or till chana dal turns soft yet retain their shape.
  * drain off the water and keep aside for 30 minutes or till water is drained off completely.
  * transfer the cooked chana dal into a blender and grind to a fine powder.
  * add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt and 2 tbsp coriander leaves.
  * mix well making sure all the spices are combined well.
  * pinch a ball sized wheat dough and dust with some wheat flour. check pizza paratha recipe to check how to prepare the wheat dough.
  * further, roll it in a circle of about 5 to 5.5 inches in diameter.
  * place a ball sized chana dal stuffing in the centre.
  * take the edge and start pleating bringing to centre.
  * sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.
  * on a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook both sides brushing oil.
  * finally, serve hot chana dal paratha with sauce, raita or pickle.

## How to Make Dal Paratha with Step-by-step photos
  1. firstly, in large vessel take 1 cup chana dal, soaked for 3 hours. !
  2. boil for 15 minutes or till chana dal turns soft yet retain their shape. you can alternatively pressure cook for 2 whistles adding 2 cups water. !
  3. Drain off the water and keep aside for 30 minutes or till water is drained off completely. !
  4. transfer the cooked chana dal into a blender and grind to a fine powder without adding any water. !
  5. now transfer the cooked chana dal powder into large mixing bowl. !
  6. add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, ¬Ω tsp **, **¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt and 2 tbsp coriander leaves. !
  7. mix well making sure all the spices are combined well. !
  8. pinch a ball sized wheat dough and dust with some wheat flour. check  to check how to prepare the wheat dough. !
  9. further, roll it in a circle of about 5 to 5.5 inches in diameter. !
  10. place a ball sized chana dal stuffing in the centre. !
  11. take the edge and start pleating bringing to centre. !
  12. also join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough. !
  13. sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick. !
  14. on a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute. !
  15. furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute). !
  16. also brush oil /  and press slightly. flip again once or twice till both the sides are cooked properly. !
  17. finally, serve hot**chana dal paratha** with , **** or . !

## Notes
  * First, soak the chana dal well to reduce the cooking time.
  * also, make sure to drain off the water completely once cooked, or else it won‚Äôt be easy to blend and the stuffing will turn to water.
  * Additionally, add finely chopped onions to the stuffing to enhance the flavour.
  * Finally, the **chana dal paratha recipe** tastes great when roasted with .

# Recipe 119

## About Kaju Masala Curry
An authentic North Indian Cuisine curry recipe prepared with a combination of crunchy roasted cashews in a tomato and onion curry sauce. **Kaju Masala** , popularly known as Kaju Paneer Masala, is an ideal gravy sabzi recipe for different types of Indian flatbread like naan and roti. The best part of this recipe is the balanced taste it has to offer. It is neither spicy nor sweet, thus making a perfect medium spiced curry similar to paneer butter masala.
There are many different ways to make this simple and tasty **Kaju Paneer Masala Curry** Recipe. The most common way is to make it with roasted cashews cooked in a creamy tomato and onion sauce gravy. However, it can also be made as a semi-dry thick gravy with cashews and diced onions. In addition, the curry can also be made with other hero ingredients like potatoes, carrots, mushrooms and soya nuggets.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Kaju Masala
!

## Kaju Masala Recipe | Kaju Curry - Hotel Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Kaju Masala Recipe | Kaju Curry Recipe | Cashew Nut Masala**
4.98 from 200 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 15 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 45 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine north indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 338 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for puree:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cashew, soaked

#### for curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup cashew
  * ‚ñ¢ 20 cubes paneer, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp curd
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cream
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp kasuri methi, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp

### Instructions 
  * In a mixer jar take 2 tomato, 2 tbsp cashew and grind them to a smooth paste. Keep asdie.
  * In a large kadai, heat 2 tbsp ghee. Fry ¬Ω cup cashews till they turn golden brown. Keep aside.
  * Also, fry 20 cubes of paneer till they turn golden brown. Keep aside.
  * Add in 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 5 cloves, 4 pepper, and saute till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add in 2 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute till the onions turn golden brown.
  * Keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, 1 tbsp chilli powder.
  * Saute on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add in prepared tomato puree and cook well.
  * Add 2 tbsp curd and 1 tsp salt and cook until the mixture releases oil.
  * Add in hot water and mix well adjusting the consistency as required. Cook well.
  * Further, add 2 tbsp cream, fried cashew and paneer. Mix and cook till the flavors are well absorbed.
  * Now add 2 tbsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander, 2 chilli, and ¬Ω tsp garam masala. Mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Kaju Masala Recipe with roti.

## How to Make Kaju Masala with Step-by-step Photos
  1. In a mixer jar take 2 tomato, 2 tbsp cashew and grind them to a smooth paste. Keep aside.  !
  2. In a large kadai, heat 2 tbsp ghee. Fry ¬Ω cup cashews till they turn golden brown. Keep aside.  !
  3. Also, fry 20 cubes of paneer till they turn golden brown. Keep aside.  !
  4. Add in 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 5 cloves, 4 pepper, and saute till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  5. Add in 2 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute till the onions turn golden brown.  !
  6. Keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, 1 tbsp chilli powder.  !
  7. Saute on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  8. Add in prepared tomato puree and cook well.  !
  9. Add 2 tbsp curd and 1 tsp salt and cook until the mixture releases oil.  !
  10. Add in hot water and mix well adjusting the consistency as required. Cook well.  !
  11. Further, add 2 tbsp cream, fried cashew and paneer. Mix and cook till the flavors are well absorbed.  !
  12. Now add 2 tbsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander, 2 chilli, and ¬Ω tsp garam masala. Mix well.  !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Kaju Masala Recipe** with roti.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, soak the cashew well to get a silky smooth gravy.
  * Additionally, frying the cashew and paneer in ghee will enhance the flavor of gravy.
  * Also, you can add sugar if the tomatoes are too sour.
  * Finally,**Kaju Masala Recipe** tastes great when prepared creamy.

# Recipe 120

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## About Badam Burfi
An excellent and tasty Indian sweet recipe made with a combination of powdered almond and desiccated coconut in a one-string sugar syrup. **Badam Burfi,** known as Badam Katli, is an ideal festival recipe for offering Prasadam to beloved gods. It can also be a perfect sweet snack and be served and exchanged with friends and family. In addition, it is also considered a healthy alternative compared to other dry fruits and sweets, significant because of Almonds.
There are many different ways to make this classical **Badam Burfi Recipe**. The variations mainly differ from the supporting ingredients added to this classical dessert. The typical combination is coconut, but it is not limited. It can take other dry fruit powders like cashews, pasta, and dates. Adding these makes it richer and premium, with just badam powder. In addition, adding rava, besan, and even wheat powder can give it a crunchy texture.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Badam Burfi
!

## Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi with Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi Recipe | Badam Katli Recipe**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 1 hour hr
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 15 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 20 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup badam / almonds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp saffron milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cardamom / elachi, powdered
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak almonds in hot water for 1 hour.
  * now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.
  * also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.
  * transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.
  * meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.
  * keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.
  * boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.
  * now add the prepared almond powder, saffron milk and cardamom powder.
  * mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.
  * continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan.
  * transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.
  * and allow to cool for 5 minutes.
  * grease your hand with little ghee and knead for a minute.
  * once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin,.
  * furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.
  * you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  * finally, serve badam burfi / badam katli on diwali or any festival.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Badam Burfi with Step-by-step Photos

### badam powder or almond meal recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak ¬æ cup of almonds in 1 cup of hot water for 1 hour.  !
  2. now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.  !
  3. also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.  !
  4. transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.  !

### badam buri | almond barfi recipe:
  1. meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  2. keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.  !
  3. boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.  !
  4. now add the prepared almond powder.  !
  5. also add saffron milk. to prepare saffron milk, soak few strands of saffron in warm milk for 10 minutes.  !
  6. additionally add cardamom powder for more flavours.  !
  7. mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.  !
  8. once the mixture begins to boil, add a tbsp of . however, it is optional, but do add more flavour to burfi.  !
  9. continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan. if you prefer slightly hard burfi then continue to stir for longer time.  !
  10. transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.  !
  11. add a tsp of **** to make smooth dough.  !
  12. and allow to cool for 5 minutes. do not rest more, as they will turn hard and wont be able to give shape.  !
  13. grease your hand with little  and knead for a minute. be careful as the dough will be very hot. try to knead when its hot, else it will be difficult. and do not over knead as badam will start releasing oil.  !
  14. once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin, adjusting the thickness according to your choice.  !
  15. furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.  !
  16. you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  17. finally, serve **badam burfi / badam katli** on diwali or any festival. !

## Notes
  * firstly, soak the badam well or blanch it for easy removal of skin.
  * also, make sure to get just 1 string consistency of sugar syrup. else it turns burfi hard and brittle.
  * most noteworthy, use nonstick pan for easy and efficient badam katlis.
  * and entire badam burfi has to be prepared on low flame.
  * finally, instead of butter paper, you can also use a plastic sheet or greased plate to prepare **badam burfi.**

# Recipe 121

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

## About Atta Besan Ladoo
It is a simple combination of 2 recipes, i.e. wheat and besan ladoo, combined to make a classic Indian dessert recipe. Traditionally, besan ladoo is prepared during festivals and religious ceremonies. However, it can have health concerns, as chickpea flour can upset your stomach. Hence, to mitigate this problem, a new Laddu recipe is prepared. One is the Atta Ladoo, commonly called the **Atta Besan Ladoo recipe**. It has the same taste and crunchiness as besan but carries the health benefits of wheat flour.
There are many ways to make a simple and healthy **Atta Besan Ladoo recipe**. The most common way is to prepare it with a combination of wheat and chickpea flour with a 1:1 ratio. This gets the best of both. However, the ratio can be altered to make a unique sweet recipe. In addition, adding roasted rava or semolina makes it crisp and crunchy. Further, adding assorted dry fruits with dry ingredients makes it a memorable and premium sweet dessert recipe.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Atta Ladoo
!

## Atta Ladoo Recipe | Atta Besan Ladoo - Wheat Laddu
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Atta Ladoo Recipe | Atta Besan Ladoo | Wheat Laddu Recipe**
5 from 376 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 15 ladoo
Calories 172 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp gond / edible gum
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp rava / suji, fine
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp melon seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ silver vark, for decoration

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, heat ¬Ω cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond on low flame.
  * Fry till the gond puffs up and turns crystal.
  * Drain off the gond and keep aside. Make sure to fry the gond on low flame, or else the gond will not get cooked from inside and will remain sticky while eating.
  * Add 1 cup wheat flour, 1 cup besan, and 2 tbsp rava in the same ghee.
  * Keep roasting on low flame till the flour is well combined.
  * Now add 1 tbsp ghee, 2 tbsp melon seeds and roast well.
  * Roast until the flour turns golden brown and aromatic.
  * Also, thee has been released from the flour, indicating the flour has roasted well.
  * Transfer to the large plate and cool slightly.
  * Add fried gond and crush slightly.
  * Also, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well. Mix making sure all the ingredients are well combined.
  * In a mixer jar take 1 cup sugar and grind to a fine powder.
  * Once the besan atta mixture has cooled add in powdered sugar and mix well. Make sure to add the sugar powder when the mixture is warm, or the sugar will melt.
  * Mix well till the mixture is well combined.
  * Prepare the ladoo by shaping them gently.
  * Finally, decorate the Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe with vark and chopped cashews.

### Nutrition
Calories: 172kcalCarbohydrates: 26gProtein: 3gFat: 7gSaturated Fat: 4gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gCholesterol: 15mgSodium: 6mgPotassium: 81mgFiber: 1gSugar: 14gVitamin A: 3IUVitamin C: 0.01mgCalcium: 6mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Atta Ladoo with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, heat ¬Ω cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond on low flame.  !
  2. Fry till the gond puffs up and turns crystal.  !
  3. Drain off the gond and keep aside. Make sure to fry the gond on low flame, or else the gond will not get cooked from inside and will remain sticky while eating.  !
  4. Add 1 cup wheat flour, 1 cup besan, and 2 tbsp rava in the same ghee.  !
  5. Keep roasting on low flame till the flour is well combined.  !
  6. Now add 1 tbsp ghee, 2 tbsp melon seeds and roast well.  !
  7. Roast until the flour turns golden brown and aromatic.  !
  8. Also, the has been released from the flour, indicating the flour has roasted well.  !
  9. Transfer to the large plate and cool slightly.  !
  10. Add fried gond and crush slightly.  !
  11. Also, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well. Mix making sure all the ingredients are well combined.  !
  12. In a mixer jar take 1 cup sugar and grind to a fine powder.  !
  13. Once the besan atta mixture has cooled add in powdered sugar and mix well. Make sure to add the sugar powder when the mixture is warm, or the sugar will melt.  !
  14. Mix well till the mixture is well combined. Prepare the ladoo by shaping them gently.  !
  15. Finally, decorate the **Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe** with vark and chopped cashews.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to roast the besan and atta well, else the flour will remain raw.
  * Also, adding rava will give crunchy texture to the ladoo.
  * Additonally, you can add nuts of your choice to make the ladoo healthy.
  * Finally, **Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe** tastes great when prepared with fresh homemade ghee.

# Recipe 122

## About Onion Paratha
An easy and simple stuffed flatbread recipe made with wheat flour and a combination of onions and besan spiced masala. **Onion Paratha** , most commonly known as **Pyaz Ka Paratha** , is a common alternative to cooked vegetable paratha like aloo or gobi paratha. Generally, it is prepared by stuffing the besan and onion-based masala inside the wheat dough bread. But it can also be done by mixing the spiced onion directly with the dough to make it Onion Roti.
There are many use cases for this paratha; the most common purpose is to pack it up in lunch or tiffin boxes. Compared to other parathas, which typically need more effort to cook vegetables. However, **Onion Paratha** does not include such complicated steps and procedures. It only takes 5-7 minutes to prepare the stuffing and hence can be prepared in a jiffy. Moreover, the spice stuffing is balanced and requires no additional sides or condiments.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Onion Paratha
!

## Onion Paratha Recipe - Dhaba Style | Pyaz Ka Paratha
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Onion Paratha recipe | Pyaz Ka Paratha | Pyaaz Paratha
5 from 193 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 20 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 50 minutes mins
Course paratha
Cuisine Indian
Servings 7 Servings
Calories 183 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### !for onion stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp kasuri methi, crushed

#### !for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading

#### !other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ wheat flour, for dusting
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, and saute till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add 2 onion, 2 chilli, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste, and saute till the onion softens.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp aamchur, and 1 tsp salt.
  * Saute till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Also, add ¬º cup besan and saute till the besan turns aromatic.
  * Further add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tbsp kasuri methi and mix well. Onion stuffing is ready, keep it aside.
  * Add 2 cup wheat flour and ¬Ω tsp salt to prepare the dough.
  * Add water as required and knead to a smooth dough.
  * Now pinch a ball-sized dough and make a cup by pressing from the sides.
  * Place a ball-sized prepared onion stuffing in the center. Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre.
  * Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough.
  * Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.
  * On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.
  * Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).
  * Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.
  * Finally, serve hot Onion Paratha with sauce, raita, or pickle.

### Nutrition
Calories: 183kcalCarbohydrates: 35gProtein: 6gFat: 2gSaturated Fat: 0.2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gTrans Fat: 0.004gSodium: 509mgPotassium: 203mgFiber: 2gSugar: 3gVitamin A: 206IUVitamin C: 24mgCalcium: 29mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Onion Paratha with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing, and saute till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  2. Add 2 onion, 2 chilli, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste, and saute till the onion softens.  !
  3. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp aamchur, and 1 tsp salt.  !
  4. Saute till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  5. Also, add ¬º cup besan and saute till the besan turns aromatic.  !
  6. Further add 2 tbsp coriander, 2 tbsp kasuri methi and mix well. Onion stuffing is ready, keep it aside.  !
  7. Add 2 cup wheat flour and ¬Ω tsp salt to prepare the dough.  !
  8. Add water as required and knead to a smooth dough.  !
  9. Now pinch a ball-sized dough and make a cup by pressing from the sides.  !
  10. Place a ball-sized prepared onion stuffing in the center. Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre.  !
  11. Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough.  !
  12. Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.  !
  13. On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.  !
  14. Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).  !
  15. Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.  !
  16. Finally, serve hot **Onion Paratha** with sauce, raita, or pickle.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, adding besan helps absorb the moisture from the stuffing.
  * Also, make sure to prepare the stuffing just before making paratha. Else the onion will release moisture and will be difficult to roll.
  * Additionally, the paratha must be roasted well so the onion will get cooked well.
  * Finally, roasting the paratha with ghee gives it a nice flavor to **Pyaz Paratha Recipe**.

# Recipe 123
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/maddur-vada-recipe-maddur-vade/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Maddur Vada
It is a simple, crisp, and crunchy deep-fried snack recipe made with a combination of rice flour, maida, and rava/sooji. The **Maddur Vada** most commonly known as **Maddur Vade** hails from the small town of Maddur from Karnataka. It is most commonly known to serve as an evening snack with a cup of tea or coffee, but not limited to it. It can also be an ideal side dish for any type of meal, including rasam rice or dal rice combo meal.
There are many different types of **Maddur Vada** , but the most common is made with rice flour, maida, and rava. The taste of this snack is derived from the onions combined with the above dry ingredients. The juice from onions is infused into the dough and tastes great when deep fried in low flame. The same vada can also be made with wheat flour as an alternative to maida. This makes it healthy but may not be a tasty snack. In addition, adding rava helps to make it crisp and crunchy, but optional.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Maddur Vada
!

## Maddur Vada Recipe | Crispy Maddur Vade - Tea Time Snack
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Maddur Vada Recipe | Crispy Maddur Vade - Tea Time Snack
5 from 25 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 15 Servings
Calories 107 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rava, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 onion, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coriander.
  * Add 1 cup rice flour, 1 cup maida and ¬Ω cup rava.
  * Also add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, pinch hing and 1 tsp salt.
  * Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Further, add 2 tbsp hot oil and mix. This helps the vada to turn crunchy.
  * Add water slowly and knead the dough.
  * Do not add more water as the dough needs to be tight.
  * Pinch a ball-sized dough, press and flatten it slightly thick.
  * Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.
  * Do not touch for 2 minutes as there are chances for the vada to break.
  * Stir occasionally and fry both sides until the vada turns golden brown.
  * Drain off to remove excess oil.
  * Finally, enjoy Maddur Vada Recipe with coconut chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 107kcalCarbohydrates: 17gProtein: 4gFat: 3gSaturated Fat: 0.5gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 4mgSodium: 224mgPotassium: 76mgFiber: 1gSugar: 1gVitamin A: 73IUVitamin C: 11mgCalcium: 20mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Maddur Vada with step by step photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 onion, 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and 2 tbsp coriander.  !
  2. Add 1 cup rice flour, 1 cup maida and ¬Ω cup rava.  !
  3. Also add 2 tbsp sesame, 2 tbsp roasted peanuts, pinch hing and 1 tsp salt.  !
  4. Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  5. Further, add 2 tbsp hot oil and mix. This helps the vada to turn crunchy.  !
  6. Add water slowly and knead the dough.  !
  7. Do not add more water as the dough needs to be tight.  !
  8. Pich a ball-sized dough, press and flatten it slightly thick.  !
  9. Deep fry in hot oil, keeping the flame on medium.  !
  10. Do not touch for 2 minutes as there are chances for the vada to break.  !
  11. Stir occasionally and fry both sides until the vada turns golden brown.  !
  12. Drain off to remove excess oil.  !
  13. Finally, enjoy **Maddur Vada Recipe** with coconut chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, the key tip to make crunchy maddur vada is to use as little water as possible.
  * Also, the onions release water, so make sure to add water as required.
  * Additionally, you can add almonds and cashews along with peanuts to get crunchy bites.
  * Finally, **Maddur Vada Recipe** stays crunchy for 3 to 4 days when stored in air tight container.

# Recipe 124
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/badanekayi-palya-recipe-karnataka-style/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Khanavali Badanekayi Palya:
It is basically a spicy baingan sabzi recipe with a blend of spices from North Karnataka cuisine. It is particularly famous with the North Karnataka Khanavali restaurants which serve this curry with flatbreads like jowar roti, ragi roti, or even akki rotti. There are different styles to make this curry which mainly differs from dry to gravy-based curries. But the most popular is the gravy based **badanekayi palya** which can also be served with rice or pulao too.
North Karnataka cuisine is known for its spiciness, especially with the range of curries it has to offer. The same set of spice mix is obvious in this recipe too. Particularly the use of Niger Seeds or locally known as gurellu elevates the flavor and aroma of any recipe. As a matter of fact, these seeds are added to almost all recipes, and the combination of roti, **badanekayi palya,** and gurellu chutney powder is the most popular one.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Badane Kayi Palya:
!

## Badanekayi Palya Recipe | Khanavali Brinjal Stir Fry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Badanekayi Palya Recipe | Karnataka Style Khanavali Badane Kayi Palya | Brinjal Stir Fry
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine north karnataka
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 474 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### masala powder:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp peanut
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp gurellu / niger seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp dry coconut
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 6 cloves garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup coriander

#### for curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 brinjal, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tomato, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp jaggery
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp

### Instructions 
  * firstly, to prepare khanavali style masala powder, dry roast 2 tbsp peanut until it turns crunchy.
  * add 2 tbsp gurellu, 2 tbsp dry coconut, 1 tsp cumin and 2 tsp coriander seeds.
  * roast on low flame until the spices turn aroamtic.
  * cool completely, and transfer to mixer jar.
  * add 6 cloves garlic, 5 chilli, 2 inch ginger and 1 cup coriander.
  * grind to coarse powder without adding water. keep aside.
  * to prepare the curry, heat ¬º cup oil in a large kadai.
  * add 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin and pinch hing. splutter the tempering.
  * add 1 onion, few curry leaves and saute until the onion softens.
  * further add 3 brinjal, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and ¬Ω tsp salt. saute for 2 minutes, until the spices are well coated.
  * cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the brinjal are half cooked.
  * now add 1 tomato, ¬Ω cup water and mix gently.
  * cover and continue to simmer for 5 minutes or until the brinjal and tomato softens.
  * further add prepared masala powder, 1 tsp jaggery and ¬Ω tsp salt. mix gently making sure everything is well combined.
  * add in 1 cup water and adjust the consistency.
  * cover and boil for 5 minutes or until all the flavours are well absorbed.
  * finally, add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well. enjoy khanavali style badanekayi palya with roti or chapathi.

### Nutrition
Calories: 474kcalCarbohydrates: 65gProtein: 20gFat: 22gSaturated Fat: 2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 6gMonounsaturated Fat: 12gTrans Fat: 0.1gSodium: 744mgPotassium: 3840mgFiber: 20gSugar: 23gVitamin A: 4345IUVitamin C: 432mgCalcium: 821mgIron: 28mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Badanekayi Palya with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, to prepare khanavali style masala powder, dry roast 2 tbsp peanut until it turns crunchy.  !
  2. add 2 tbsp gurellu, 2 tbsp dry coconut, 1 tsp cumin and 2 tsp coriander seeds.  !
  3. roast on low flame until the spices turn aroamtic.  !
  4. cool completely, and transfer to mixer jar.  !
  5. add 6 cloves garlic, 5 chilli, 2 inch ginger and 1 cup coriander.  !
  6. grind to coarse powder without adding water. keep aside.  !
  7. to prepare the curry, heat ¬º cup oil in a large kadai.  !
  8. add 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin and pinch hing. splutter the tempering.  !
  9. add 1 onion, few curry leaves and saute until the onion softens.  !
  10. further add 3 brinjal, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and ¬Ω tsp salt. saute for 2 minutes, until the spices are well coated.  !
  11. cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the brinjal are half cooked.  !
  12. now add 1 tomato, ¬Ω cup water and mix gently.  !
  13. cover and continue to simmer for 5 minutes or until the brinjal and tomato softens.  !
  14. further add prepared masala powder, 1 tsp jaggery and ¬Ω tsp salt. mix gently making sure everything is well combined.  !
  15. add in 1 cup water and adjust the consistency.  !
  16. cover and boil for 5 minutes or until all the flavours are well absorbed.  !
  17. finally, add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well. enjoy **Khanavali Style Badanekayi Palya** with roti or chapathi.  !

## Notes:
  * firstly, make sure to dry roast the gurellu else the curry will not be flavourful. also do not skip this ingredient,
  * additionally, increase the amount of chilli if you are looking for spicy curry.
  * also, prepare the curry slightly watery, as the curry thickens once cooled.
  * finally, **Khanavali Style Badanekayi Palya Recipe** tastes great when served hot and spicy.

# Recipe 125

## recipe card for shimla mirch besan sabji recipe:
!

## shimla mirch besan sabji recipe | capsicum besan bhaji | shimla mirch besan
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy shimla mirch besan sabji recipe | capsicum besan bhaji | shimla mirch besan
4.99 from 195 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course sabji
Cuisine south india
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp fennel / saunf
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 capsicum, cube
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kashmiri red chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt

### Instructions 
  * roast on low flame until the besan turns aromatic and golden brown. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp fennel, pinch hing.
  * add 1 chilli and saute on low flame.
  * further, add 2 capsicum and stir fry without overcooking.
  * keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬æ tsp coriander powder, 1 tsp aamchur and ¬æ tsp salt.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * now add in roasted besan and mix well.
  * mix until the besan is well coated to capsicum. you can sprinkle 2 tbsp of water if the mixture is too dry.
  * cover and simmer for 7 minutes until everything is well cooked.
  * finally, enjoy shimla mirch besan sabji recipe with phulka or roti.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make capsicum besan bhaji with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a pan take ¬º cup besan and roast on low flame. !
  2. roast on low flame until the besan turns aromatic and golden brown. keep aside. !
  3. in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp fennel, pinch hing. !
  4. add 1 chilli and saute on low flame. !
  5. further, add 2 capsicum and stir fry without overcooking. !
  6. keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬æ tsp coriander powder, 1 tsp aamchur and ¬æ tsp salt. !
  7. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic. !
  8. now add in roasted besan and mix well. !
  9. mix until the besan is well coated to capsicum. you can sprinkle 2 tbsp of water if the mixture is too dry. !
  10. cover and simmer for 7 minutes until everything is well cooked. !
  11. finally, enjoy **shimla mirch besan sabji recipe** with phulka or roti. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to roast the besan on low flame to prevent from burning.
  * also, add besan as required to make the curry slightly dry or sticky.
  * additionally, capsicum needs to be crunchy and not soggy in this sabzi.
  * finally, **shimla mirch besan sabji recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly spicy.

# Recipe 126
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/susla-recipe-puffed-rice-upma-mandakki/

### susla video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

## recipe card for puffed rice upma recipe:
!

## susla recipe | puffed rice upma | mandakki or churumuri susla | uggani
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy susla recipe | puffed rice upma | mandakki or churumuri susla | uggani
4.89 from 26 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 8 minutes mins
Course breakfast / snacks
Cuisine andhra, north karnataka
Servings 2 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup puffed rice / churumuri / murmura
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp peanuts
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup putani powder / roasted gram dal powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cup puffed rice / churumuri / murmura.
  * pour 3 cup water and rinse the churumuri well. do not allow to soak churumuri as they turn mushy.
  * squeeze off the water gently and keep aside the churumuri.
  * in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil and roast 2 tbsp peanuts on low flame until it turns crunchy.
  * now add ¬æ tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing and few curry leaves. splutter the tempering.
  * further add 1 onion, 2 chilli and saute well.
  * add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp sugar, ¬æ tsp salt and saute on low flame.
  * add in squeezed churumuri along with ¬º cup putani powder.
  * mix gently until the spices are coated well.
  * cover and simmer for 3 minutes or until flavours are absorbed.
  * now add 1 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well.
  * finally, enjoy churumuri susla / puffed rice upma for your breakfast or snacks.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make susla with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cup puffed rice / churumuri / murmura. !
  2. pour 3 cup water and rinse the churumuri well. do not allow to soak churumuri as they turn mushy. !
  3. squeeze off the water gently and keep aside the churumuri. !
  4. in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp oil and roast 2 tbsp peanuts on low flame until it turns crunchy. !
  5. now add ¬æ tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, pinch hing and few curry leaves. splutter the tempering. !
  6. further add 1 onion, 2 chilli and saute well. !
  7. add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp sugar, ¬æ tsp salt and saute on low flame. !
  8. add in squeezed churumuri along with ¬º cup putani powder. !
  9. mix gently until the spices are coated well. putani powder enhances the flavour and also absorb excess moisture. !
  10. cover and simmer for 3 minutes or until flavours are absorbed. !
  11. now add 1 tbsp lemon juice and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well. !
  12. finally, enjoy **churumuri susla / puffed rice upma** for your breakfast or snacks. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to not over soak or over squeeze churumuri.
  * also, susla can be topped with sev while serving.
  * additionally, add tomato along with onions and skip lemon juice for variation.
  * finally, **churumuri susla / puffed rice upma recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly spicy.

# Recipe 127
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/potato-curry-recipe-masala-dosa-aloo-bhaji-masala-dosa/

### potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa recipe card:
!

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
potato curry for masala dosa | aloo baji for masala dosa
5 from 187 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine Indian
Servings 4 servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 potatoes, boiled
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, thinly sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 green chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard seeds / rai
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric powder
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 stem coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste

### Instructions 
  * boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.
  * finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.
  * in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter.
  * then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.
  * now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.
  * add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.
  * now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.
  * mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins
  * squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.
  * serve aloo bhaji hot with masala dosa's, rice or chapathis.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## potato curry for masala dosa | aloo bhaji for masala dosa photo recipe:
  1. boil the potatoes well and peel off the skin.  !
  2. finely chop green chillies, ginger, coriander leaves. also thinly slice onion and keep ready.  !
  3. in a pan heat a tablespoon of oil and add cumin seeds, mustard seeds, urad dal, red chilli and channa dal. wait till mustard seeds splutter. !
  4. then add curry leaves and hing. fry for a minute.  !
  5. now add thinly sliced onion and fry till then turn translucent.  !
  6. add in finely chopped chilli and ginger. fry till the raw smell of ginger goes away.  !
  7. now add boiled potatoes and turmeric.  !
  8. mash the potatoes well and add in 3 tbsp of water to have a smooth gravy paste. cook 3 mins  !
  9. squeeze some lemon juice and add chopped coriander leaves. give a good mix.  !
  10. serve aloo bhaji hot with **** ‚Äòs, rice or chapathis.  !

## notes:
  * aloo bhaji taste great when prepared fresh.
  * you can use leftover all bhaji as a stuffing for sandwich. you can also prepare aloo bonda with this.
  * tempering is very important in aloo bhaji, be generous while tempering.

# Recipe 128
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/sabudana-vada-recipe-sago-vada/

### sabudana vada video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for sabudana vada recipe:
!

## sabudana vada recipe | how to make sabudana vada | sago vada | sabakki vada
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy sabudana vada recipe | how to make sabudana vada | sago vada | sabakki vada
5 from 198 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Soaking Time 3 hours hrs
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course Snack
Cuisine north indian
Servings 17 vada

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sabudana / sago / tapioca
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 potato / aloo, boiled & mashed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup peanuts, roasted & crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp lemon juice
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for frying

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 1 cup sabudana and soak with enough water for 3 hours.
  * drain off the water and rest for 30 minutes, allowing to drain off the water completely.
  * now take the soaked sabudana in a large bowl.
  * also, add 2 potato and ¬Ω cup peanuts.
  * additionally, add ¬Ω tsp ginger paste, 1 tsp cumin, 1 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * mix and mash well with your hand.
  * prepare vada by deep frying or fry in appe pan.
  * finally, serve sabudana vada hot along with masala tea.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make sabudana vada with step by step photo recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 1 cup sabudana and soak with enough water for 3 hours. soaking time varies, so make sure to soak only until sabudana turns soft. !
  2. drain off the water and rest for 30 minutes, allowing to drain off the water completely.
  3. now take the soaked sabudana in a large bowl. !
  4. also, add 2 potato and ¬Ω cup peanuts. !
  5. additionally, add ¬Ω tsp ginger paste, 1 tsp cumin, 1 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander, 1 tsp lemon juice and ¬Ω tsp salt. !
  6. mix and mash well with your hand. this is very important, as you will be squeezing off the water present in sabudana. else there are chances for the water present in sabudana to burst while you deep fry. !
  7. prepare a soft dough. if you are not able to form a dough then add another boiled potato and mash well. !

### sabudana vada in appe pan:
  1. firstly, heat appe pan and pour ¬º tsp of oil in each mould of appe pan. !
  2. prepare small balls from the prepared sabudana mixture. !
  3. place it over appe pan. !
  4. keeping the flame on low to medium cover and cook for 5 minutes. !
  5. flip over once the bottom turns golden brown. !
  6. again cover and cook for 5 minutes. !
  7. make sure to flip over in between until vada is cooked completely and turns golden brown. !
  8. cook for 20 minutes in total, or until sabbaki vada gets cooked completely. !
  9. finally, **sabudana vada in appe pan** is ready to be served. !

### deep frying sabudana vada:
  1. firstly, prepare small patties from sabudana mixture. !
  2. deep fry the patties in hot oil. or preheat and bake at 180 degree celcius for 30 minutes. !
  3. fry on medium flame until they turn golden brown flipping in between. !
  4. drain off over a kitchen towel to remove excess oil. !
  5. finally, serve **sabudana vada** hot along with . !

## notes:
  * firstly, soak the sabudana till they are soft. some sabudana just need 2 hours of soaking. so vary accordingly.
  * also, adding roasted and crushed peanuts give a crunchy bite to vada and also absorbs moisture.
  * furthermore, if the vada burst while deep frying, it means you haven‚Äôt soaked well or mashed or drained sabudana well.
  * additionally, if you are not able to form a dough then add another boiled potato and mash well.
  * finally, **sabudana vada recipe** tastes great when served hot and crispy.
