# Recipe 129
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/chai-recipe-masala-tea-indian-masala-chai-recipe/

### chai recipe | masala tea recipe| indian masala chai video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card of chai recipe | masala tea recipe| indian masala:
!

## chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy chai | masala tea | indian masala chai
5 from 23 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 20 minutes mins
Course beverage
Cuisine indain
Servings 2 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp tea powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cardamoms
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 black pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 half cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ half cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp sugar

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min
  * furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  * also and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.
  * now add milk, sugar.
  * bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.
  * furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.
  * finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any breakfast recipes.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## chai recipe | masala tea recipe | indian masala chai step by step photo recipe:
  1. firstly, in a small pan, take half cup of water and add cardamom, cloves, ginger, black pepper and boil for 2-3 min  !
  2. furthermore, bring it to boil and lower the flame. simmer it for 1-2 minutes until you get the nice aroma.
  3. and tea leaves or tea powder and simmer for 3-4 minutes.  !
  4. now add milk, sugar.  !
  5. also bring it to boil and brew for 2 minutes.  !
  6. furthermore, switch of the flame and filter out the tea powder and spices with a fine mesh sieve.  !
  7. finally, serve the masala chai with biscuits or with any **.** !

## notes:
  * firstly, if you do not like spices, skip all of them. this will be a plain tea.
  * furthermore, adjust the consistency of your tea with the milk. if you do not like thick masala chai, reduce the quantity of milk and increase the water.
  * also, add milk and get to a boil just before serving.
  * finally, you can use masala tea powder if you do not have spices.

# Recipe 130
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mini-idli-sambar-tiffin-idli-sambar-bullet-idli-sambar/

## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar recipe card:**
!

## mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
HEBBARS KITCHEN
mini idli sambar | tiffin idli sambar | bullet idli sambar
5 from 16 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course sambar
Cuisine south indian
Servings 3 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor daal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 to matoes
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 green chillies
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω lemon

#### seasoning ingredients
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω split urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.
  * once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.
  * meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.
  * bullet idli sambar
  * furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.
  * now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.
  * add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.
  * additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.
  * bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  * furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.
  * prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.
  * finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with bullet idli's dipped in this sambar.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## **mini idli sambar recipe | tiffin idli sambar recipe | bullet idli sambar step by step photo recipe:**
  1. firstly, wash and rinse the dal and put into a pressure cooker. in the same cooker add tomatoes and turmeric powder. pressure cook for 4 whistles.  !
  2. once the pressure releases from the cooker, whisk the dal and tomatoes well.  !
  3. meanwhile, chop onions, coriander leaves, ginger and chilli and keep them aside.  !
  4. furthermore, in a pan, add 1 tsp of oil. to the same pan add onions and fry them till golden brown.  !
  5. now add curry leaves, ginger and chilli. fry for a minute.  !
  6. also add smashed daal to the kadai and bring to a boil.  !
  7. additionally, season with salt and chilli powder.  !
  8. bring it to boil. add water to maintain the consistency of sambar. boil it for 5 mins.
  9. furthermore, garnish with coriander leaves and lemon juice, add a tsp of ghee and switch off.  !
  10. prepare the tempering and add it over sambar.  !
  11. finally, your tiffin sambar is ready. serve it with **** dipped in this sambar.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, idlis taste great when dipped in sambar for atleast 5 minutes.
  * furthermore, you can add **** if you wish to make it more spicy.
  * moreover, mash the dal properly so that the consistency is maintained.
  * finally, ad a tsp of ghee to make it more flavourful.

# Recipe 131
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | easy paddu recipe card below:
!

## guliappa recipe / paddu recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
guliyappa recipe / paddu recipe
5 from 188 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 12 hours hrs
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 12 hours hrs 30 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 30 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal / split black lentils
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup sona masuri rice / chawal / dosa rice
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp menthe / fenugreek seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup paper avalakki / beaten rice / poha
  * ‚ñ¢ few coriander leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ oil for greasing tawa

### Instructions 
  * soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl and soak for 5 hours.
  * first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter.
  * transfer to a large vessel.
  * now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter.
  * now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender.
  * transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well.
  * cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours.
  * the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented.
  * mix the batter slightly.
  * take required batter in a different bowl.
  * finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.
  * add fried onions and ginger, chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves and mix well.
  * also add in salt and mix the batter well.
  * now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.
  * reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.
  * once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.
  * your paddu recipe is ready


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## easy paddu recipe | guliyappa recipe | paddu recipe with step by step photo recipe:
  1. soak urad dal and rice, methi in a separate bowl. add in enough water and soak for 5 hours. !
  2. first drain the water from rice and blend to smooth batter. add water if required to make a smooth paste. !
  3. transfer to a large vessel. and keep aside !
  4. now blend urad dal to smooth fluffy batter. !
  5. now add a cup of paper avalakki to the blender. and grind to a smooth thick paste. !
  6. transfer the batter into the same bowl and mix well. !
  7. cover and ferment in a warm place for 12 hours. !
  8. the next day you can see the batter has raised well indicating its well fermented. !
  9. mix the batter slightly. !
  10. take required batter in a different bowl.
  11. finely chop onion, ginger, coriander leaves and curry leaves.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa.jpg>)
  12. fry the onions and ginger with a table spoon of oil till they turn translucent.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa-11.jpg>)
  13. now add fried onions and ginger along with finely chopped coriander leaves, curry leaves to the batter and mix well.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa31.jpg>)
  14. also add in salt and mix the batter well. ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa4.jpg>)
  15. heat the guliyappa pan and a drop of oil in all moulds.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa5.jpg>)
  16. now slowly pour the batter into each of the moulds with the help of large spoon.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa6.jpg>)
  17. reduce the heat to medium and cook for 3 min with a closed lid.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa8.jpg>)
  18. once the batter gets cooked from bottom, slowly with the help of spoon flip it over and cook other side.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa10.jpg>)
  19. remove the cooked guliyappas and serve hot with**** or chutney powder.  ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/guliyappa-recipe-paddu-recipe/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2015/12/guliyappa12.jpg>)

## notes:
  * first of all, if your guliyappa is not getting golden brown, add some sugar.
  * in addition, adjust the consistency of the batter by adding required water.
  * furthermore, to make it little spicy, add some chopped chilli.
  * finally, skip the masala step and pour the batter directly to moulds, but these onion masala enhances the taste of guliyappa.

# Recipe 132
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/methi-malai-paneer-recipe-paneer-methi/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Methi Malai Paneer
An easy yet flavoured and creamy dhaba-style paneer gravy curry recipe made with fenugreek leaves and cooking cream. **Methi Malai paneer** is a popular curry in restaurants or dhabas, it can also be an ideal choice for lunch and dinner. It is a unique North Indian curry that offers creamy and mild sweetness with a hint of bitter taste. Thus making it a perfect choice for both rice and any type of bread and rotis.
There are many different methods to make this creamy **Methi Malai Paneer** Recipe. The most common way is to make it with paneer cubes, fresh fenugreek leaves and onion tomato base. However, the same curry can also be made with paneer grate like Bhurji gravy. In addition, the gravy base can be extended further by adding vegetables like mushrooms, sweet corn, peas and even soya nuggets.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Methi Malai Paneer
!

## Methi Malai Paneer Curry Recipe - Dhaba Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Methi Malai Paneer Recipe | Methi Paneer Recipe | Paneer Methi Malai**
5 from 202 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 15 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 45 minutes mins
Course curries
Cuisine north indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 156 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bunch methi / fenugreek leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 black cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup tomato puree
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ 20 cubes  
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cream
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, take 1 bunch methi leaves in a large bowl.
  * Add 1 tsp salt and soak for 15 minutes.
  * Squeeze off the water, this helps to remove bitterness from methi.
  * Chop them finely making sure the methi is clean. Keep aside.
  * In a kaai, heat 2 tbsp ghee and saute chopped methi.
  * Once the methi turns aromatic, keep it aside.
  * Add 2 tbsp oil, pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 black cardamom and 4 cloves. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Now add 1 cup tomato puree, 1 tsp salt and cook well.
  * Cook until the oil separates from the sides.
  * Add 2 cup hot water and adjust the consistency.
  * Further add 20 cubes paneer, 2 tbsp cream and mix gently.
  * Cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed.
  * Now add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Methi Malai Paneer Recipe with roti and rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 156kcalCarbohydrates: 11gProtein: 3gFat: 12gSaturated Fat: 7gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 3gCholesterol: 31mgSodium: 646mgPotassium: 406mgFiber: 3gSugar: 5gVitamin A: 1048IUVitamin C: 9mgCalcium: 72mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Methi Malai Paneer with Step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, take 1 bunch methi leaves in a large bowl.  !
  2. Add 1 tsp salt and soak for 15 minutes.  !
  3. Squeeze off the water, this helps to remove bitterness from methi.  !
  4. Chop them finely making sure the methi is clean. Keep aside.  !
  5. In a kadai, heat 2 tbsp ghee and saute chopped methi.  !
  6. Once the methi turns aromatic, keep it aside.  !
  7. Add 2 tbsp oil, pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 black cardamom and 4 cloves. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  8. Add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.  !
  9. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tbsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  10. Now add 1 cup tomato puree, 1 tsp salt and cook well.  !
  11. Cook until the oil separates from the sides.  !
  12. Also, add saute methi and cook well.  !
  13. Add 2 cup hot water and adjust the consistency.  !
  14. Further add 20 cubes paneer, 2 tbsp cream and mix gently.  !
  15. Cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed.  !
  16. Now add ¬Ω tsp garam masala and mix well.  !
  17. Finally, enjoy **Methi Malai Paneer Recipe** with roti and rice.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to pluck only the leaves, as the stems are hard and won‚Äôt taste good.
  * Also, add cream to make the gravy creamy. Do not compromise on it.
  * Additionally, you can cut the paneer into shape of your choice.
  * Finally, **Methi Malai Paneer Recipe** tastes great when made creamy and less spicy.

# Recipe 133
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/shahi-paneer-recipe-shahi-paneer-masala/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Shahi Paneer Masala
It is a classical North Indian rich and creamy curry recipe prepared with a combination of dry fruits with onion sauce and paneer cubes. In **Shahi Paneer** , the word ‚ÄòShahi‚Äô literally means royal in Hindi, and the reference is attached mainly because of its rich and luxurious profile. It is also believed that the recipe and the gravy sauce were first introduced during the Mughal empires and served to the royal family. Hence, it carries the name and serves it on auspicious and religious occasions.
A simple and creamy **Shahi Paneer Masala Recipe** is prepared in many ways. The most common way is to make it with a combination of nuts like almonds, cashews, and walnuts and diced onions. The tomato is skipped as it does not yield a rich colour, however in some variation, even tomatoes are added. Adding tomatoes will change their colour and texture, and it is typically added in dhaba-style recipes. Further, the curry can also be used as a multi-purpose sauce and other vegetables and meat tenders can be added to the same sauce.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Shahi Paneer Masala
!

## Shahi Paneer Recipe | Shahi Paneer Masala | Shahi Paneer Ki Sabji
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy **Shahi Paneer Recipe | Shahi Paneer Masala | Shahi Paneer Ki Sabji**
5 from 665 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine north indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 308 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for tomato puree:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp pepper
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnanmon
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginnger
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp badam, blanched
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup curd

#### for gravy:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp butter
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup cream
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 20 cubes paneer
  * ‚ñ¢ few kesar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp kasuri methi, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Take spices and saute on low flame.
  * Add 1 inch ginger, 4 cloves garlic and 2 onion. Saute until the onions turn golden brown.
  * Also add 2 tomato, 2 tbsp badam and cook till the tomatoes soften.
  * Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.
  * Add ¬º cup curd, and grind to smooth paste.
  * Now sieve the puree to get a silky smooth texture. Keep aside.
  * In a Kadai, take 2 tbsp butter and 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder and ¬Ω tsp cumin powder.
  * Saute on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add in prepared puree and cook well.
  * Also add ¬º cup cream, 1 tsp salt and cook till the oil separates.
  * Now add 20 cubes paneer, few kesar, 1 tsp sugar and mix well.
  * Simmer for 5 minutes, or until the flavours are well absorbed.
  * Add 2 tbsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Shahi Paneer Recipe with roti and naan.

### Nutrition
Calories: 308kcalCarbohydrates: 13gProtein: 5gFat: 28gSaturated Fat: 9gPolyunsaturated Fat: 5gMonounsaturated Fat: 12gTrans Fat: 0.3gCholesterol: 35mgSodium: 650mgPotassium: 351mgFiber: 3gSugar: 6gVitamin A: 1128IUVitamin C: 20mgCalcium: 111mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Shahi Paneer with Step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Take spices and saute on low flame.  !
  2. Add 1 inch ginger, 4 cloves garlic and 2 onion. Saute until the onions turn golden brown.  !
  3. Also add 2 tomato, 2 tbsp badam and cook till the tomatoes soften.  !
  4. Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.  !
  5. Add ¬º cup curd, and grind to smooth paste.  !
  6. Now sieve the puree to get a silky smooth texture. Keep aside.  !
  7. In a Kadai, take 2 tbsp butter and 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder and ¬Ω tsp cumin powder.  !
  8. Saute on low flame till the spices turn aromatic.  !
  9. Add in prepared puree and cook well.  !
  10. Also add ¬º cup cream, 1 tsp salt and cook till the oil separates.  !
  11. Now add 20 cubes paneer, few kesar, 1 tsp sugar and mix well.  !
  12. Simmer for 5 minutes, or until the flavours are well absorbed.  !
  13. Add 2 tbsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.  !
  14. Finally, enjoy Shahi **Paneer Recipe** with roti and naan.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to use generous amount of butter and cream to make the gravy tasty.
  * Also, adding badam or cashew gives texture to the curry.
  * Additionally, you can use honey in place of sugar to balance the sourness.
  * Finally, Shahi Paneer Recipe tastes great when prepared rich and creamy.

# Recipe 134
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/lachha-paratha-lachha-parantha-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Lachha Paratha
It is perhaps one of the easy and simple paratha prepared without any stuffing and the selling point is its flakiness. **Lachha Paratha** most commonly known as **Lachha Parantha** is a popular North Indian or Punjabi cuisine paratha recipe. The additional layered flakiness gives it an edge compared to other stuffed parathas, thus making it more attractive and appetizing.
There are many different types of **Lachha Paratha** recipes across India. The different types of paratha are mainly derived from the combination of flour used to make it. The main hero combination is wheat and plain flour, but most commonly just wheat flour is used. The same layered paratha can also be made with just plain flour. This is very similar to Kerala paratha and known for its taste and softness.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe card for Flaky Lachha Paratha
!

## Lachha Paratha Recipe | Crisp, Flaky Layered Lachha Parantha
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Lachha Paratha Recipe | Crisp, Flaky Layered Lachha Parantha
5 from 257 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course roti
Cuisine Indian
Servings 10 roti
Calories 116 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ ghee, for layers
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, on a large plate (paraat) take 2 cups of wheat flour.
  * Add ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt and 2 tbsp oil.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Add water and start to knead the dough.
  * Knead to smooth and soft dough adding water as required.
  * Spread some oil, cover it, and rest for 20 minutes.
  * After resting the dough, knead the dough slightly and pinch a ball-sized.
  * Dust with wheat flour and roll as thin as possible.
  * Spread ghee generously and fold zig zag.
  * Roll it spiral and tuck it from inside.
  * Dust with wheat flour, and roll slightly thick.
  * Cook the roti on hot tawa, and flip over.
  * Roast the roti spreading oil on both sides.
  * Cook until the paratha turns golden and crisp.
  * Finally, crush the Lachha Paratha Recipe and enjoy it with curry.

### Nutrition
Calories: 116kcalCarbohydrates: 19gProtein: 3gFat: 3gSaturated Fat: 0.2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gTrans Fat: 0.01gSodium: 117mgPotassium: 27mgFiber: 1gSugar: 0.1gCalcium: 4mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Lachha Paratha with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, on a large plate (paraat) take 2 cups of wheat flour. !
  2. Add ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt and 2 tbsp oil.  !
  3. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  4. Add water and start to knead the dough.  !
  5. Knead to smooth and soft dough adding water as required.  !
  6. Spread some oil, cover it, and rest for 20 minutes.  !
  7. After resting the dough, knead the dough slightly and pinch a ball-sized.  !
  8. Dust with wheat flour and roll as thin as possible.  !
  9. Spread ghee generously and fold zig zag.  !
  10. Roll it spiral and tuck it from inside. Dust with wheat flour, and roll slightly thick.  !
  11. Cook the roti on hot tawa, and flip over.  !
  12. Roast the roti spreading oil on both sides.  !
  13. Cook until the paratha turns golden and crisp.  !
  14. Finally, crush the **Lachha Paratha Recipe** and enjoy it with curry.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, knead the dough super soft, or the paratha will not be soft from the inside.
  * Also, spreading ghee gives a nice flavour to the paratha.
  * Additionally, adding ajwain is optional. Ajwain helps in digestion.
  * Finally, **Lachha Paratha Recipe** tastes great when served hot.

# Recipe 135
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/gobi-paratha-recipe-gobhi-paratha-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Gobi Paratha
An easy and simple stuffed paratha recipe prepared with wheat flour dough, stuffed with raw cauliflower grate, and mixed herbs and spices. **Cauliflower paratha** most commonly known as **Gobi Paratha** is a staple food from North India and is often served as an alternative to Aloo Paratha. It is typically loaded with spice and savory stuffing and hence does not require any additional sides and condiments. However, it tastes even better when served with mint or yogurt raita or with any desired curries and sabzi.
There are many different ways to make this simple and healthy **Gobi Paratha**. The most common and popular way is to make the stuffing with raw gobi grate and mix it with spices and herbs. However, there is another popular way to cook the cauliflower first and then mash it and prepare the stuffing. In addition, the cooked cauliflower can also be mixed directly into the wheat dough. This is much easier and simpler to cook. Lastly, in the place of wheat flour, plain or maida flour can also be used to make it more tasty.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Gobi Paratha
!

## Gobi Paratha Recipe | Cauliflower Paratha - Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Gobi Paratha Recipe | Cauliflower Paratha - Tips & Tricks
5 from 239 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 20 minutes mins
Cook Time 25 minutes mins
Total Time 45 minutes mins
Course paratha
Cuisine north indian
Servings 6 Servings
Calories 165 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω gobi / cauliflower / gobi, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ !for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, grate ¬Ω gobi coarsely.
  * In a bowl take 2 cup grated gobi.
  * Add ¬Ω tsp garam masala, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Also add 1 inch ginger, grated, 2 chilli and 2 tbsp coriander.
  * Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.
  * Further to prepare the dough, in a large bowl take 2 cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp ajwain and mix well.
  * Add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.
  * Now pinch a ball-sized dough and roll about 4 inches in diameter.
  * Place a ball-sized prepared gobi stuffing in the centre.
  * Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre.
  * Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough.
  * Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.
  * On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.
  * Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).
  * Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.
  * Finally, serve hot **Gobi Paratha** with sauce, raita or pickle.

### Nutrition
Calories: 165kcalCarbohydrates: 34gProtein: 5gFat: 1gSaturated Fat: 0.1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.2gMonounsaturated Fat: 0.1gSodium: 392mgPotassium: 133mgFiber: 2gSugar: 1gVitamin A: 184IUVitamin C: 25mgCalcium: 20mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Gobi Paratha with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, grate ¬Ω gobi coarsely.  !
  2. In a bowl take 2 cup grated gobi.  !
  3. Add ¬Ω tsp garam masala, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp aamchur and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  4. Also add 1 inch ginger, grated, 2 chilli and 2 tbsp coriander. Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.  !
  5. Further to prepare the dough, in a large bowl take 2 cup wheat flour, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp ajwain and mix well.  !
  6. Add water as required and knead to smooth and soft dough.  !
  7. Now pinch a ball-sized dough and roll about 4 inches in diameter.  !
  8. Place a ball-sized prepared gobi stuffing in the centre.  !
  9. Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre. Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough.  !
  10. Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.  !
  11. On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.  !
  12. Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).  !
  13. Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.  !
  14. Finally, serve hot**Gobi Paratha** with sauce, raita or pickle.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to prepare the stuffing just before making paratha. Else the gobi will release moisture and will be difficult to roll.
  * Also, the paratha must be roasted well so the gobi will get cooked well.
  * Additionally, roasting the paratha with ghee gives it a nice flavour.
  * Additionally, you can add ¬º cup maida to the dough, to make paratha super soft.
  * Finally, **Gobi Paratha Recipe** tastes great when stuffing is made masaledar.

## Recipe Card for Mix Veg Curry
!

## mix veg recipe | mix vegetable | mixed vegetable curry | mix veg curry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy mix veg recipe | mix vegetable | mixed vegetable curry | mix veg curry
4.96 from 303 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 40 minutes mins
Total Time 50 minutes mins
Course Main Course
Cuisine north india
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for roasting vegetables:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 12 , cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp almonds / badam, blanched
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 potato / aloo, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω carrot, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup cauliflower / gobi, florets
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 beans, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup peas / matar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º capsicum, chopped

#### for tomato puree:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 clove
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 12  almonds / badam, blanched

#### for curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf / tej patta
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp kasuri methi
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 green chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kashmiri red chilli powder / lal mirch powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup , whisk
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cream / malai
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly heat 4 tsp oil and saute spices.
  * saute 1 onion and 1 tsp ginger garlic paste.
  * further add spices and 1 tsp salt. saute well.
  * add tomato puree and cook well.
  * add ¬Ω cup whisked curd. stir continuously.
  * now add roasted mix vegetables and mix well.
  * add ¬Ω cup water and cook for another 10 minutes.
  * turn off the flame and add 2 tbsp cream, 1 tsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well.
  * finally, serve mix vegetable curry / mix veg recipe with hot roti.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Mix Veg with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, saute 12 cubes  in 3 tsp of oil, and keep aside. !
  2. in the same oil saute 2 tbsp blanched almonds till they turn golden brown. !
  3. further, add 1 chopped potato, ¬Ω carrot and saute for 3 minutes. !
  4. also add ¬Ω cup cauliflower, 4 beans and ¬º cup peas. saute for another 3 minutes. !
  5. now add ¬º capsicum and continue to saute for another minute. !
  6. keep all the vegetables aside. !
  7. now prepare the curry by heating 4 tsp oil and saute 1 bay leaf, 1 tsp cumin, 2 tsp kasuri methi and 1 green chilli. !
  8. saute 1 onion and 1 tsp ginger garlic paste till they turn slightly golden brown. !
  9. further add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp red chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬º tsp and 1 tsp salt. !
  10. saute for a minute or till spices get cooked completely. !
  11. now prepare tomato paste by taking 2 chopped tomato in a blender. !
  12. also add 1 inch cinnamon, 5 clove, 2 pods cardamom and 12 blanched almonds. !
  13. blend to smooth paste without adding any extra water. !
  14. transfer the prepared tomato puree to kadai and mix well. !
  15. cover and cook for 5 minutes or till oil is released from masala paste. !
  16. lower the flame and add ¬Ω cup whisked curd. stir continuously, without allowing curd to curdle. !
  17. now add in roasted mix vegetables and mix well. !
  18. add ¬Ω cup water or as required and mix well adjusting consistency. !
  19. cover and continue to cook for another 10 minutes, or till vegetables are cooked completely. !
  20. turn off the flame and add 2 tbsp cream, 1 tsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well. !
  21. finally, serve **mix vegetable curry** /**mix veg recipe** with hot roti. !

## Notes
  * firstly, add vegetables of your choice like broccoli, mushrooms, or beetroot.
  * also, roasting vegetables will enhance the flavour, however to reduce the oil, steam / boil the vegetables.
  * furthermore, replace almonds with cashews for creamy texture.
  * additionally, add whisked curd to prevent curd from curdling.
  * finally, **mix vegetable curry** /**mix veg recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly creamy.

# Recipe 137
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/paneer-ki-sabji-quick-paneer-curry/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Paneer Ki Sabji
An easy and simple, yet premium curry recipe prepared with diced paneer cubes in a spicy and tangy onion tomato gravy. **Paneer Ki Sabji** or **Quick Paneer Curry** can be an ideal gravy curry that can be served with multiple types of Indian flat breads like roti and chapati but not limited to. It can also be a fancy side dish for flavored rice recipes like jeera rice, pulao, and fried rice.
There are different types of **paneer ki sabzi** across India, but the most popular way is dhaba-style curry. It is mainly prepared with simple onion and tomato gravy with additional thick yogurt or curd. Adding yogurt makes it thick and creamy and also helps to get that thick gravy consistency. In addition, adding cashew paste, and cooking cream makes it more fancy and more flavored.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card For Quick Paneer Ki Sabji
!

## Paneer Ki Sabji | Dhaba Style Paneer Curry | Paneer Sabzi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy paneer ki sabji | quick paneer curry recipe | paneer sabzi recipe
4.96 from 248 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine punjabi
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 310 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for paneer marination:
  * ‚ñ¢ 15 cube 
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tsp oil, for roasting

#### for curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 pod black cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pod cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup tomato puree
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 15 cubes paneer, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp ginger garlic paste and ¬º tsp salt.
  * mix well combining all the spices well.
  * cover and rest for 30 minutes or more for marination.
  * now heat 3 tsp oil and saute marinated paneer.
  * do not overcook the paneer as it turns rubbery. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 1 tbsp ghee and 2 tbsp oil.
  * add 1 tsp cumin, 1 bay leaf, 1 pod black cardamom, 1 inch cinnamon, 2 pods cardamom and 4 cloves.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * now add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.
  * further keeping the flame on low, add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * add 2 cup tomato puree and mix well.
  * cover and cook for 10 minutes or until the oil separates.
  * keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω cup curd and stir continuously.
  * keep cooking until the curd is well combined.
  * now add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency as required.
  * further, add cooked paneer and mix well.
  * cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed.
  * add 1 tsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * finally, enjoy paneer ki sabji with roti or rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 310kcalCarbohydrates: 24gProtein: 9gFat: 22gSaturated Fat: 5gCholesterol: 13mgSodium: 1089mgPotassium: 904mgFiber: 6gSugar: 10gVitamin A: 1480IUVitamin C: 28mgCalcium: 141mgIron: 6mg

## How to Make Paneer ki Sabji with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 15 cubes of paneer, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp ginger garlic paste, and ¬º tsp salt. !
  2. mix well combining all the spices well. cover and rest for 30 minutes or more for marination. !
  3. now heat 3 tsp oil and saute marinated paneer. !
  4. do not overcook the paneer as it turns rubbery. keep aside. !
  5. in a large kadai heat 1 tbsp ghee and 2 tbsp oil. !
  6. add 1 tsp cumin, 1 bay leaf, 1 pod black cardamom, 1 inch cinnamon, 2 pods cardamom and 4 cloves. !
  7. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic. !
  8. now add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown. !
  9. further keeping the flame on low, add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tsp salt. !
  10. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic. !
  11. add 2 cup tomato puree and mix well. !
  12. cover and cook for 10 minutes or until the oil separates. !
  13. keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω cup curd and stir continuously. !
  14. keep cooking until the curd is well combined. !
  15. now add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency as required. !
  16. further, add cooked paneer and mix well. !
  17. cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed. !
  18. add 1 tsp kasuri methi, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well. !
  19. finally, enjoy **paneer ki sabji** with roti or rice. !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to marinate the paneer for a rich juicy paneer.
  * Also, whisk the curd well, else there are chances for the curd to curdle.
  * Additionally, you can add cream or cashew paste to get a thicker consistency,
  * Finally, the **paneer ki sabji recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly oil and spicy.

# Recipe 138

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

## About Mixed Veg Handi
It is a classical North Indian cuisine mixed vegetable curry prepared using a traditional clay pot known as handi. **Mixed Veg Handi** gets its name from the traditional clay pot used to prepare curry. As such there are no additional ingredients or cooking techniques, but the use of a clay pot makes it special and gives a unique taste to it. It can be best served with a range of Indian flatbreads, but the best choice is garlic naan, tandoori roti, and jeer rice.
Traditionally, **Mixed Veg Handi** or **Veg Diwani Handi** is prepared and served in North Indian or Punjabi dhabas. The roadside dhabas typically use basic and less fancy crockeries to cook most of the curries and recipes. Hence most of the curries started getting the name with the technique or utensils associated with it. Handi curry is one such recipe where the name is mainly associated with the way it is prepared.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Mixed Veg Handi
!

## Veg Handi Recipe | Mixed Vegetable Handi - Dhaba Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Veg Handi Recipe | Mixed Vegetable Handi - Dhaba Style
5 from 196 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 15 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 35 minutes mins
Course Side Dish
Cuisine punjabi
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for onion-tomato paste:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 medium sized onion, roughly chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 garlic cloves, roughly chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 large tomato, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 7 cashews, whole

#### vegetables:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 carrot, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup gobi / cauliflower, florets
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω capsicum, thinly sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 potato, cubed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup peas / matar
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 beans, chopped

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf / tej patta
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon stick / dalchini
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves / lavang
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric powder / haldi
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kashmiri red chili powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder / dhaniya powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp cumin powder / jeera powder
  * ‚ñ¢ salt to taste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cups water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi / dry fenugreek leaves, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp cream / malai
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander leaves, finely chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, heat oil and saute onions till they change colour.
  * also saute ginger and garlic.
  * further add roughly chopped tomatoes, cashews and saute well.
  * cool down the mixture completely and blend smooth.
  * in the same kadai, heat oil and saute bay leaf, cinnamon stick and cloves.
  * now add chili powder and turmeric and saute.
  * pour the prepared onion-tomato paste and cook.
  * furthermore, add coriander powder, cumin powder and salt.
  * add curd keeping and stir continuously.
  * now add mixed vegetables and water.
  * cover and cook the vegetables for 15 minutes.
  * add crushed kasuri methi, cream, garam masala and coriander leaves. mix well.
  * finally, serve veg handi or veg diwani handi with tandoori roti, naan or rice.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How To Make Veg Handi with Step-by-step Photos

### onion tomato paste recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large kadai or handi heat oil and saute onions till they change colour.  !
  2. also saute ginger and garlic till the raw smell disappears.  !
  3. further add roughly chopped tomatoes and saute well.  !
  4. add cashew to make gravy more rich and creamy.  !
  5. saute till the tomatoes turn soft and mushy.  !
  6. cool down the mixture completely and transfer to the blender.  !
  7. blend to smooth paste without adding any water. keep aside.  !

### mix veg handi recipe:
  1. in the same kadai, heat oil and add bay leaf, cinnamon stick and cloves. !
  2. saute them till they aromatic on low flame. !
  3. now add chili powder and turmeric. adding chili powder and turmeric to oil, gives bright colour to the gravy. !
  4. saute on low flame for 20 seconds without burning the spices. !
  5. pour the prepared onion-tomato paste. !
  6. and saute well for 10 minutes or till the paste turns thick. !
  7. furthermore, add coriander powder, cumin powder and salt. !
  8. saute on low flame for a minute to cook the spices. !
  9. add curd keeping the flame on low to avoid curd from curdling. !
  10. stir continuously till the curd mixes well with spices. !
  11. now add mixed vegetables of your choice. i have added almost 2 cups of vegetables. !
  12. add 2 cups of water or as required to cook the vegetables. !
  13. mix well and adjust the seasonings. !
  14. cover and cook the vegetables for 15 minutes or till they are cooked completely. !
  15. add crushed kasuri methi, cream,  and coriander leaves. mix well. !
  16. finally, serve **veg handi** or**veg diwani handi** with ,  or rice. !

## Notes
  * firstly, add vegetables of your choice, like broccoli,  and corn.
  * additionally, prepare veg handi in butter for more rich flavour.
  * instead of cooking vegetables in gravy, steam the vegetables and later add to gravy to hasten cooking time.
  * finally, **veg handi** or**veg diwani handi** taste more royal when prepared with cashew and almond paste.

# Recipe 139
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/amritsari-kulcha-recipe-aloo-kulcha/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Amritsari Aloo Kulcha
It is a simple and easy Indian flatbread recipe with spiced potato stuffing and baked in a traditional tandoor oven. **Aloo Kulcha** popularly known as **Amritsari Kulcha** is a popular alternative to the tandoori roti or garlic naan bread. Unlike other Indian breads, the kulcha is made with plain flour or maida, making it an attractive loaf of tasty bread. The bread is typically served with a range of yogurt dips and raita, but it can also be served with any Indian curries.
There are many different types of Kulcha recipes and the variation mainly depends upon the type of stuffing used. The most popular stuffing has to be the potato, but there is no limit to the different types of stuffing that can be made. The other most popular stuffing combination is Aloo Gobi stuffing with the same bread dough. In addition, traditionally the bread is baked in the tandoor oven, but it can also be baked using tawa on a gas cooktop.

## Chef Tips for Aloo Kulcha
The recipe does not have any complicated steps and ingredients, yet some critical tips for a soft Aloo Kucha are ‚Äì
  1. **Flour Type ‚Äì** Traditionally, the bread kulcha is made with plain flour or maida flour. This flour makes it ideal for texture and taste. However, wheat flour or a combination of wheat and plain flour can also be used.
  2. **Stuffing ‚Äì** The stuffing has to be thick and silky without any lumps in between. This helps to stuff easily and also roll the bread without any difficulty.
  3. **Cooking Technique ‚Äì** Traditional ovens can be difficult to source to bake this kulcha at home. This recipe post shows a practical solution for using a tawa and gas cooktop mimicking the tandoor oven cooking.
  4. **Accompaniment ‚Äì** Generally, any sour and creamy yogurt dip or raita makes it a perfect accompaniment. Yet any dry or gravy-based curry can be a perfect choice too.
  5. **Variations ‚Äì** The stuffing can take any type of cooked vegetable mash and it is open-ended. In addition, the dough can also be prepared with a 1:1 ratio of wheat and plain flour.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Amritsari Aloo Kulcha
!

## Kulcha Recipe | Amritsari Aloo Kulcha - Street Style on Tawa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Kulcha Recipe | Amritsari Aloo Kulcha - Street Style on Tawa
5 from 211 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 2 hours hrs
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 2 hours hrs 30 minutes mins
Course roti
Cuisine Indian
Servings 10 Servings
Calories 191 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp baking powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp baking soda
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee

#### for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 potato, boiled & grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kala namak
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

#### for rolling:
  * ‚ñ¢ kalonji
  * ‚ñ¢ sesame
  * ‚ñ¢ coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ chilli powder

### Instructions

#### Dough kneading for kulcha:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cup maida, ¬Ω tsp baking powder, ¬º tsp baking soda, 1 tbsp sugar and ¬Ω tsp salt. Mix well.
  * Add ¬Ω cup curd, and water. Start to knead the dough adding water as required.
  * At first, the dough will be sticky. Keep kneading to make the dough soft and smooth.
  * Also, add 2 tbsp ghee and continue to knead the dough.
  * Knead to smooth and soft dough, tuck the dough and rest for 30 minutes.

#### Aloo stuffing for kulcha:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 3 potato. Make sure to grate the boiled potato, so it will be easy while rolling the kulcha.
  * Add 1 onion, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp aamchur, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp kala namak and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste.
  * Also, add 2 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * Aloo stuffing is ready for preparing kulcha. Keep aside.

#### Rolling and roasting kulcha on tawa:
  * Firstly, take the dough and dust with madia.
  * Stuff a ball sized stuffing into the dough and seal.
  * Now roll gently keeping it uniform thickness.
  * Spread some water on top, sprinkle kalonji, sesame, coriander and chilli powder.
  * Flip over and spread water over kulcha. This helps kulcha to stick on the tawa.
  * Furthermore, slowly flip the kulcha and put it on hot tawa. Sprinkle salt water, as it helps to stick the kulcha well.
  * After a minute, flip the tawa upside down and cook the kulcha directly on flame till they turn golden brown and puff up.
  * Gently scrape the kulcha from bottom and remove.
  * Also brush some butter.
  * Finally, serve Aloo Kulcha Recipe hot with your favourite curry like chana masala.

### Nutrition
Calories: 191kcalCarbohydrates: 33gProtein: 5gFat: 4gSaturated Fat: 2gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 1gCholesterol: 8mgSodium: 287mgPotassium: 108mgFiber: 2gSugar: 2gVitamin A: 140IUVitamin C: 16mgCalcium: 44mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Aloo Kulcha with step-by-step photos

### Dough kneading for kulcha:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 3 cup maida, ¬Ω tsp baking powder, ¬º tsp baking soda, 1 tbsp sugar and ¬Ω tsp salt. Mix well.  !
  2. Add ¬Ω cup curd, and water. Start to knead the dough adding water as required.  !
  3. At first, the dough will be sticky. Keep kneading to make the dough soft and smooth.  !
  4. Also, add 2 tbsp ghee and continue to knead the dough.  !
  5. Knead to smooth and soft dough, tuck the dough and rest for 30 minutes.  !

### Aloo stuffing for kulcha:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 3 potato. Make sure to grate the boiled potato, so it will be easy while rolling the kulcha.  !
  2. Add 1 onion, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp aamchur, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt, ¬Ω tsp kala namak and ¬Ω tsp ginger paste.  !
  3. Also, add 2 chilli, 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.  !
  4. Aloo stuffing is ready for preparing kulcha. Keep aside.  !

### Rolling and roasting kulcha on tawa:
  1. Firstly, take the dough and dust with madia.  !
  2. Stuff a ball sized stuffing into the dough and seal.  !
  3. Now roll gently keeping it uniform thickness.  !
  4. Spread some water on top, sprinkle kalonji, sesame, coriander and chilli powder. Flip over and spread water over kulcha. This helps kulcha to stick on the tawa.  !
  5. Furthermore, slowly flip the kulcha and put it on hot tawa. Sprinkle salt water, as it helps to stick the kulcha well.  !
  6. After a minute, flip the tawa upside down and cook the kulcha directly on flame till they turn golden brown and puff up.Gently scrape the kulcha from bottom and remove.  !
  7. Also brush some butter.  !
  8. Finally, serve **Aloo Kulcha Recipe** hot with your favourite curry like chana masala.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, you can use wheat flour instead of maida for a healthy alternative.
  * Also, keep the aloo stuffing masaledar else the kulcha will not taste great.
  * Furthermore, knead to smooth a soft dough else kulcha will be chewy.
  * In addition, you can also use oven or tandoor for baking the kulcha instead of tawa. But never use nonstick tawa as it slips while reversing.
  * Finally, applying water is mandatory to **Aloo Kulcha Recipe**. This helps naan or kulcha to stick to tawa and can reverse the tawa and cook directly on flame.

# Recipe 140
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/paneer-paratha-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Paneer Paratha
It is a simple and healthy popular cottage cheese stuffed flatbread recipe made and served for morning breakfast, lunch, and dinner. The **Paneer Paratha** is loaded with a filling stuffing that can be easily the best choice for lunch boxes or tiffin boxes. There are many ways it is served, but the most common way is to serve with a flavored yogurt or curd raita. However, not limited and can also be served with a range of curries.
There are many ways to make this simple and flavored **Paneer Paratha recipe**. But the most common and popular way is to make it with basic paneer crumble and a range of basic spices added to it. This not only keeps it simple to prepare but also makes it to the point. The other most common way is to make it with other cooked and mashed vegetables. The popular choice is the mashed and boiled potatoes or cauliflower. However, the experiment is open-ended and can be tweaked as per preference.

## Chef Tips for Paneer Paratha
The recipe for any paratha is extremely simple without any complications or complicated ingredients used in it. It goes the same for this recipe too, yet some simple and mandatory tips are ‚Äì
  1. **Paneer ‚Äì** Use fresh moist and preferably homemade paneer for this paratha. Store-bought paneer comes adulterated and can be hard to crumble and eventually for stuffing.
  2. **Spice Mixture ‚Äì** The basic spice mixture used for this recipe is chilli powder, garam masala, and amchur powder. However, the spice mixture can further be increased, and depending upon taste buds, you can add kasuri methi, chaat masala, etc.
  3. **Moist Dough ‚Äì** The dough has to be soft and moist so that it can be easily shaped and pleated. There are many different pleating and stuffing techniques, but having moist and soft dough helps to pleat in any shape.
  4. **Cooking Method ‚Äì** Use a preheated griddle or tawa to roast the rolled and stuffed paratha. If the tawa is not heated properly, it may stick to the tawa and cannot be easily flipped.
  5. **Accompaniments ‚Äì** The paratha does not require any mandatory side dish, yet can be served with basic to fancy accompaniments. The most common is flavored yogurt or raita, but it can also be served with a range of pickles or any type of curries.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Paneer Paratha
!

## Paneer Paratha Recipe | How to Make Paneer Parata
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Paneer Paratha Recipe | How to Make Paneer Parata
4.99 from 247 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 30 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Resting Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 5 minutes mins
Course paratha
Cuisine Indian
Servings 6 Servings
Calories 383 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for Paneer Stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup paneer, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt

#### for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp ajwain / carom seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading

### Instructions

#### How to make paneer stuffing for paratha:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup paneer, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp aamchur, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, 1 inch ginger, grated, 2 chilli, finely chopped, 2 tbsp coriander, and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined. Paneer stuffing is ready, keep it aside.

#### How to make dough for paratha:
  * Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup of wheat flour ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp ajwain. Mix well.
  * Add water as required and start to knead.
  * Knead to a smooth and soft dough adding water as required.
  * Grease oil and rest for 20 minutes.

#### How to make Paneer Paratha:
  * After the dough has rested for 20 minutes, knead slightly.
  * Now pinch a ball-sized dough and roll about 4 inches in diameter.
  * Place a ball-sized prepared paneer stuffing in the centre.
  * Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre.
  * Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough.
  * Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.
  * On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.
  * Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).
  * Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.
  * Finally, serve hot Paneer paratha with sauce, raita or pickle.

## How to Make Paneer Paratha with step-by-step photos

#### How to make paneer stuffing for paratha:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup paneer, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp aamchur, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, 1 inch ginger, grated, 2 chilli, finely chopped, 2 tbsp coriander, and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  2. Mix well making sure everything is well combined. Paneer stuffing is ready, keep it aside.  !

#### How to make dough for paratha:
  1. Firstly, in a large bowl take 2 cup of wheat flour ¬Ω tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp ajwain. Mix well.  !
  2. Add water as required and start to knead.  !
  3. Knead to a smooth and soft dough adding water as required.  !
  4. Grease oil and rest for 20 minutes.  !

#### How to make Paneer Paratha:
  1. After the dough has rested for 20 minutes, knead slightly.  !
  2. Now pinch a ball-sized dough and roll about 4 inches in diameter.  !
  3. Place a ball-sized prepared paneer stuffing in the centre. Take the edge and start pleating bringing it to the centre.  !
  4. Also, join the pleats together and secure tight pinching off excess dough. !
  5. Sprinkle some wheat flour and roll slightly thick.  !
  6. On a hot tawa place the rolled paratha and cook for a minute.  !
  7. Furthermore, flip the paratha when the base is partly cooked (after a minute).  !
  8. Also, brush oil/ghee and press slightly. Flip again once or twice till both sides are cooked properly.  !
  9. Finally, serve hot**Paneer paratha** with sauce, raita or pickle.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, you can also add onions to the paneer stuffing for variation.
  * Also, roasting the paratha with ghee gives a nice flavour to the paratha.
  * Additionally, you can add ¬º cup maida to the dough, to make paratha super soft.
  * Finally, **Paneer Paratha Recipe** tastes great when stuffing is made masaledar.

# Recipe 141
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/matar-kachori-recipe-peas-kachori-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Matar Kachori
An extremely simple and popular deep-fried snack recipe prepared with plain flour with spiced and tasty peas masala stuffing. **Peas Kachori** most commonly known as **Matar kachori** is an ideal tea-time snack, but not limited to it. It can also be an ideal morning breakfast and even a lunch meal with a spicy side dish or curry. It is also a most common street food snack served with a choice of condiments across India.
There are many different types and variations of this simple Kachori recipe. The most common types and variations are mainly with the stuffing used in each of these Kachori. The most common or easy stuffing is Peas or Matar hence the **Matar Kachori recipe**. The stuffing can also be done with other vegetables like potatoes, onions, mixed vegetables and even paneer.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Matar Ki Kachori
!

## Matar Kachori Recipe | Matar Ki Kachori | Peas Kachori
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Matar Kachori Recipe | Matar Ki Kachori | Peas Kachori**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 25 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine Indian
Servings 6 Servings
Calories 365 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### !for dough:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup maida
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup oil
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for kneading

#### !for stuffing:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup peas / matar, frozen / fresh
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp fennel
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp dry mango powder
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, on a large plate take 2 cup maida, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt, and ¬º cup oil.
  * Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Add water as required and knead to a smooth dough.
  * Grease the dough with oil, cover, and rest for 30 minutes.
  * Meanwhile, prepare the stuffing by sauting 3 cup peas.
  * Saute until the peas turn aromatic and soften.
  * Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.
  * Add 1 inch ginger, 4 chilli, and grind to a coarse paste. Keep aside.
  * In a pan heat 2 tbsp oil, add pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, and ¬Ω tsp fennel. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Further, add 2 tbsp besan and saute till the besan turns aromatic.
  * Now add prepared peas paste and cook for a minute.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp kasuri methi, ¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tsp sugar, and 1 tsp dry mango powder.
  * Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.
  * Matar stuffing is ready. Allow to cool completely.
  * Knead the dough again, pinch a small ball-sized dough, and tuck well.
  * With your fingers, press the sides gently and make a cup shape.
  * Place a small ball-sized prepared matar stuffing.
  * Start to pleat and seal tight. Pinch off excess dough.
  * Now flatten gently, having a uniform thickness.
  * in hot oil, keeping the flame on low.
  * Do not touch until the kachori starts to float by itself. Takes approximately 3 minutes.
  * Carefully flip over and fry both sides on low flame.
  * Fry until the kachori turns golden brown and crisp.
  * Drain off the kachori over kitchen paper making sure to remove excess oil.
  * Finally, enjoy Matar Kachori Recipe with imli chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 365kcalCarbohydrates: 48gProtein: 10gFat: 15gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 4gMonounsaturated Fat: 9gTrans Fat: 0.1gSodium: 398mgPotassium: 363mgFiber: 6gSugar: 7gVitamin A: 848IUVitamin C: 72mgCalcium: 38mgIron: 4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Matar Kachori with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, on a large plate take 2 cup maida, ¬º tsp ajwain, ¬Ω tsp salt, and ¬º cup oil.  !
  2. Crumble and mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  3. Add water as required and knead to a smooth dough.  !
  4. Grease the dough with oil, cover, and rest for 30 minutes.  !
  5. Meanwhile, prepare the stuffing by sauting 3 cup peas.  !
  6. Saute until the peas turn aromatic and soften.  !
  7. Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.  !
  8. Add 1 inch ginger, 4 chilli, and grind to a coarse paste. Keep aside.  !
  9. In a pan heat 2 tbsp oil, add pinch hing, 1 tsp cumin, and ¬Ω tsp fennel. Saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  10. Further, add 2 tbsp besan and saute till the besan turns aromatic.  !
  11. Now add prepared peas paste and cook for a minute.  !
  12. Keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 1 tsp kasuri methi, ¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tsp sugar, and 1 tsp dry mango powder.  !
  13. Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.  !
  14. Matar stuffing is ready. Allow to cool completely.  !
  15. Knead the dough again, pinch a small ball-sized dough, and tuck well.  !
  16. With your fingers, press the sides gently and make a cup shape.  !
  17. Place a small ball-sized prepared matar stuffing.  !
  18. Start to pleat and seal tight. Pinch off excess dough.  !
  19. Now flatten gently, having a uniform thickness.  !
  20. Drop in hot oil, keeping the flame on low.  !
  21. Do not touch until the kachori starts to float by itself. Takes approximately 3 minutes.  !
  22. Carefully flip over and fry both sides on low flame.  !
  23. Fry until the kachori turns golden brown and crisp.  !
  24. Drain off the kachori over kitchen paper making sure to remove excess oil.  !
  25. Finally, enjoy **Matar Kachori Recipe** with imli chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to roast the besan well, or else the flavor of besan will not taste good.
  * Also, you can adjust the amount of spices to your choice.
  * Additionally, make sure to fry on a low flame to cook uniformly.
  * Finally, **Matar Kachori Recipe** stays good for a week when stored in an airtight container.

## Recipe Card for Malai Pyaaz Ki Sabzi

## Malai Pyaaz Ki Sabzi Recipe | Cream And Onion Curry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Malai Pyaaz Ki Sabzi Recipe | Cream And Onion Curry
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 5 minutes mins
Total Time 10 minutes mins
Course sabzi
Cuisine rajasthani
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 287 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp kalonji
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch cinnamon
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves garlic, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup cream / malai
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mango powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp kasuri methi, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, ¬Ω tsp kalonji, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 bay leaf, 1 inch ginger, 5 cloves garlic and 2 chilli.
  * Splutter the tempering on medium flame.
  * Add 2 onions and saute for 3 minutes until the onion softens slightly.
  * Keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add in ¬Ω cup cream and cook till the oil separates.
  * Further, add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency.
  * Boil for 3 minutes or until the curry turns creamy.
  * Now add ¬Ω tsp mango powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 2 tbsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. Mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Malai Pyaz Recipe with roti.

### Nutrition
Calories: 287kcalCarbohydrates: 16gProtein: 4gFat: 25gSaturated Fat: 10gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 10gTrans Fat: 0.04gCholesterol: 45mgSodium: 425mgPotassium: 380mgFiber: 3gSugar: 6gVitamin A: 1.162IUVitamin C: 58mgCalcium: 96mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Malai Pyaaz Ki Sabzi with Step-by-step photos
  1. Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, ¬Ω tsp kalonji, 1 inch cinnamon, 1 bay leaf, 1 inch ginger, 5 cloves garlic and 2 chilli.  !
  2. Splutter the tempering on medium flame.  !
  3. Add 2 onions and saute for 3 minutes until the onion softens slightly.  !
  4. Keeping the flame on low add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  5. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  6. Add in ¬Ω cup cream and cook till the oil separates.  !
  7. Further, add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency.  !
  8. Boil for 3 minutes or until the curry turns creamy.  !
  9. Now add ¬Ω tsp mango powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, 2 tbsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. Mix well.  !
  10. Finally, enjoy **Malai Pyaz Recipe** with roti.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, adding mango powder gives sourness to the curry. So make sure not to skip it.
  * Also, keep the onion sabji slightly spicy, as the cream will reduce the spice level.
  * Additionally, onion slices are chopped somewhat thick so that the crunchiness of onion remains when cooked.
  * Finally, **Malai Pyaz Recipe** can be prepared in less than 10 minutes.

# Recipe 143
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/chana-dal-recipe-chana-dal-fry-recipe/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Chana Dal Fry
It is a simple and comfortable food made with split Bengal Gram with a tomato onion gravy base. In other words, Chana Dal Masala Fry is a staple food and is often served with a range of flavored rice recipes and may also be served with a range of Indian Flat breads. Typically, it carries a thick texture compared to the other types of lentil curry, mainly because of the nature of the lentils. It is for this reason, that it is often considered a multipurpose curry and hence served with both rice and rotis.
There are many ways this simple Chana Dal Fry recipe can be prepared. The most common and basic way is to prepare with a combination of Bengal Gram and Moong Dal. Adding moong dal helps to get a rich and creamy texture. Additionally, it can also be made with a combination of other lentils like toor, masoor, and urad dal. Further, the way the dal is cooked can vary. Typically, the lentil is pressure-cooked and then tossed with tomato and onions. However, to hasten the cooking process, the onions and tomatoes can also be pressure-cooked.

## Chef Tips for Channa Dal Fry
The recipe is extremely simple to cook and prepare. It requires some of the basic ingredients to prepare with a minimum amount of time. Yet some critical and mandatory tips are ‚Äì
  1.     1. **Lentil Quality ‚Äì** The quality of channa dal has to be best and fresh. It should not powder when pressed and is also soggy in nature. You may perhaps, fry it with less oil to make it crisp before pressure cooking it.
    2. **Pressure Cooking ‚Äì** Typically, the combination of lentils is just pressure-cooked and then tossed with tomato and onion gravy base. This helps to maximize the flavors and also evenly cook the lentils as compared to pressure cooking tomatoes & onions with lentils.
    3. **Garnish ‚Äì** Typically, the cooked dal is garnished with Ghee tempering and fresh coriander leaves. However, it can also be garnished with finely chopped onions and carrot grates to make it a perfect multipurpose curry.
    4. **Lentil Combination ‚Äì** The ideal combination of this recipe is Moong Dal with Chana Dal. Yet you can experiment with other types of dal like Toor, Masoor, and Urad dal for the same purpose.
    5. **Texture ‚Äì** The recipe has to be thick and dense in nature with Bengal Gram almost cooked. It should hold its shape yet easily digestible and dissolve when pressed. Adding Moong Dal or Toor helps get a rich and creamy texture.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Chana Dal Fry:
!

## Chana Dal Recipe | Dhaba Style Chana Dal Fry Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Chana Dal Recipe | Dhaba Style Chana Dal Fry Tips & Tricks
5 from 194 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Soaking Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr
Course dal
Cuisine north indian
Servings 4 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for pressure cooking:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp masoor dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water

#### for dal:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 pod black cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves garlic, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi, crushed

#### for tadka:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch chilli powder

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, soak 1 cup chana dal and 2 tbsp masoor dal for 30 minutes. You can also use moong dal in place of masoor dal.
  * Transfer the soaked dal to the pressure cooker.
  * Add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tbsp ghee and 3 cup water.
  * Cover and pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked well.
  * Once the pressure is released, check whether the dal is well-cooked or not. Keep aside.
  * In a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 bay leaf, 2 pods cardamom, 1 pod black cardamom, 1 tsp cumin and pinch hing. saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Add 5 cloves garlic and saute slightly.
  * Further add 1 onion, 1 tbsp ginger paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.
  * Further keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬æ tsp salt
  * Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * Also, add 2 tomato and saute until the oil releases.
  * Now add in cooked dal and mix gently. adjust the consistency as required.
  * Cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the dal absorbs the flavour.
  * Furthermore, in a pan heat 2 tbsp ghee, 1 tsp cumin, 2 dried red chilli and pinch chilli powder.
  * Pour the tempering over the dal.
  * Also add 2 tbsp coriander, 1 tsp kasuri methi and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Chana Dal Tadka Recipe with jeera rice.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Chana Dal with step-by-step photos:
  1. Firstly, soak 1 cup chana dal and 2 tbsp masoor dal for 30 minutes. You can also use moong dal in place of masoor dal.  !
  2. Transfer the soaked dal to the pressure cooker.  !
  3. Add ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt, 1 tbsp ghee and 3 cup water.  !
  4. Cover and pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked well.  !
  5. Once the pressure is released, check whether the dal is well-cooked or not. Keep aside.  !
  6. In a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 bay leaf, 2 pods cardamom, 1 pod black cardamom, 1 tsp cumin and pinch hing. saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  7. Add 5 cloves garlic and saute slightly.  !
  8. Further add 1 onion, 1 tbsp ginger paste and saute until the onions turn golden brown.  !
  9. Further keeping the flame on low, add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬æ tsp salt.  !
  10. Saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  11. Also, add 2 tomato and saute until the oil releases.  !
  12. Now add in cooked dal and mix gently. adjust the consistency as required.  !
  13. Cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the dal absorbs the flavour.  !
  14. Furthermore, in a pan heat 2 tbsp ghee, 1 tsp cumin, 2 dried red chilli and pinch chilli powder.  !
  15. Pour the tempering over the dal.  !
  16. Also add 2 tbsp coriander, 1 tsp kasuri methi and mix well.  !
  17. Finally, enjoy **Chana Dal Tadka Recipe** with jeera rice.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, adding masoor dal or moong dal to chana dal gives a nice creaminess to the dal.
  * Also, you can add green chili if you prefer spicy dal.
  * Additionally, over-cooking the chana dal, makes the chana dal turn mushy.
  * Finally, **Chana dal Tadka Recipe** thickens once cooled, so adjust consistency before serving.

# Recipe 144
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/bharwa-mirchi-recipe-stuffed-chilies/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Bharwa Mirchi:
It is basically a simple and easy side dish recipe from the flavoured Rajasthani cuisine made with large green chilies. **Bharwa Mirchi** is typically made with long thick green chilies with besan or chickpea flour-based stuffing. The ingredients used for this recipe are basic and can be easily available in any dry-season state. Rajasthan is a dry and hot climate state, and the recipe suits its demographic. Moreover, the heat from the chiles provides the necessary, and hence it is prominent in Rajasthani cuisine.
In addition, the use of **Bharwa Mirchi** or **Stuffed Chilies** is multiple. Typically, it is made and served as a side dish snack, but it can also be made as gravy-based curries for roti and rice. The curry or gravy taste depends upon the use or types of chilies. Typically mild to medium taste chilies are most recommended, but not limited to it.

### Video Recipe:

## Recipe Card for Bharwa Mirchi:
!

## Bharwa Mirchi Recipe | Bharli Mirchi | Stuffed Chilies | Stuffed Mirchi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Bharwa Mirchi Recipe | Bharli Mirchi | Stuffed Chilies | Stuffed Mirchi
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course Side Dish
Cuisine rajasthani
Servings 5 Servings
Calories 183 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for besan masala:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp aamchur

#### for bharwa mirchi:
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cloves garlic, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add ¬Ω cup besan and roast on low flame.
  * roast until the besan turns golden brown and aromatic.
  * transfer to the bowl and cool completely.
  * add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, pinch hing, ¬Ω tsp salt, and 1 tsp aamchur.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * take chilli and slit in the centre.
  * stuff the masala generously. if the chillis are spicy, you can remove the seeds of chilli.
  * now heat 2 tbsp oil. splutter 1 tsp cumin, 5 cloves garlic and ¬Ω onion.
  * add in stuffed chilli and fry for 2 minutes.
  * cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the chilli softens. fry in between to prevent the chilli from burning.
  * add in leftover masala and mix well.
  * simmer for 3 minutes or until everything is well combined.
  * now add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * finally, enjoy Bharwa Mirchi Recipe with roti or rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 183kcalCarbohydrates: 15gProtein: 4gFat: 13gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 4gMonounsaturated Fat: 7gTrans Fat: 0.04gSodium: 255mgPotassium: 336mgFiber: 3gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 607IUVitamin C: 71mgCalcium: 38mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make Bharli Mirchi with step-by-step photos:
  1. firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil. add ¬Ω cup besan and roast on low flame.  !
  2. roast until the besan turns golden brown and aromatic.  !
  3. transfer to the bowl and cool completely.  !
  4. add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, ¬Ω tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, pinch hing, ¬Ω tsp salt, and 1 tsp aamchur.  !
  5. mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  6. take chilli and slit in the centre.  !
  7. stuff the masala generously. if the chillis are spicy, you can remove the seeds of chilli.  !
  8. now heat 2 tbsp oil. splutter 1 tsp cumin, 5 cloves garlic and ¬Ω onion.  !
  9. add in stuffed chilli and fry for 2 minutes.  !
  10. cover and simmer for 5 minutes or until the chilli softens. fry in between to prevent the chilli from burning.  !
  11. add in leftover masala and mix well.  !
  12. simmer for 3 minutes or until everything is well combined.  !
  13. now add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.  !
  14. finally, enjoy **Bharwa Mirchi Recipe** with roti or rice.  !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, make sure to roast the besan on low flame, else the besan will taste raw.
  * Also, make the masala spicy, or else the stuffing will taste bland.
  * Additionally, you can also add garlic and ginger paste to the stuffing for variation.
  * Finally, **Bharwa Mirchi Recipe** tastes great when the chilli is slightly crisp in a bite.

# Recipe 145

### Pitod Ki Sabji video recipe:

####

####
