## Recipe Card for Rajasthani patod curry:
!

## Pitod Ki Sabji Recipe | Rajasthani Patod Curry | No Vegetable Curry
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy Pitod Ki Sabji Recipe | Rajasthani Patod Curry | No Vegetable Curry
No ratings yet
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine rajasthani
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 337 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for besan katli:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp ajwain
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup water

#### for curry:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger paste
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp roasted besan
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

### Instructions

#### how to make besan katli:
  * firstly, in bowl take ¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, pinch hing, ¬º tsp ajwain and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * add 2 cup water in batches and whisk well.
  * prepare a watery consistency batter.
  * pour the besan batter into the pan and stir.
  * cook on low to medium flame stirring continuously.
  * cook until the mixture thickens and starts to separate the pan.
  * transfer the mixture over the plate and spread uniformly.
  * allow it to cool completely.
  * now cut into pieces of the shape of your choice. keep aside.

#### how to make pitod curry:
  * firstly, in a bowl take 2 cup curd, ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tsp ginger paste.
  * mix well making sure everything is well combined. keep aside.
  * in a kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee, add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp kasuri methi, pinch hing and 2 chilli. saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * add in the prepared curd mixture and cook on low flame.
  * keep stirring until the oil separates from the pan.
  * further add 1 tsp roasted besan, ¬Ω tsp salt and cook for 3 minutes.
  * cook until the gravy thickens slightly.
  * now add prepared besan katli and mix gently.
  * cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the flavours are well absorbed.
  * finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy Pitod Ki Sabji Recipe with roti or rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 337kcalCarbohydrates: 21gProtein: 21gFat: 20gSaturated Fat: 7gPolyunsaturated Fat: 6gMonounsaturated Fat: 5gCholesterol: 26mgSodium: 827mgPotassium: 380mgFiber: 5gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 681IUVitamin C: 51mgCalcium: 260mgIron: 5mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make pitod ki sabji with step by step photo:

### how to make besan katli:
  1. firstly, in bowl take ¬Ω cup besan, ¬º tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala, pinch hing, ¬º tsp ajwain and ¬Ω tsp salt.  !
  2. add 2 cup water in batches and whisk well.  !
  3. prepare a watery consistency batter.  !
  4. pour the besan batter into the pan and stir.  !
  5. cook on low to medium flame stirring continuously.  !
  6. cook until the mixture thickens and starts to separate the pan.  !
  7. transfer the mixture over the plate and spread uniformly.  !
  8. allow it to cool completely.  !
  9. now cut into pieces of the shape of your choice. keep aside.  !

### how to make pitod curry:
  1. firstly, in a bowl take 2 cup curd, ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp garam masala and 1 tsp ginger paste.  !
  2. mix well making sure everything is well combined. keep aside.  !
  3. in a kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee, add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp kasuri methi, pinch hing and 2 chilli. saute until the spices turn aromatic.  !
  4. add in the prepared curd mixture and cook on low flame.  !
  5. keep stirring until the oil separates from the pan.  !
  6. further add 1 tsp roasted besan, ¬Ω tsp salt and cook for 3 minutes.  !
  7. cook until the gravy thickens slightly.  !
  8. now add prepared besan katli and mix gently.  !
  9. cover and simmer for 5 minutes, or until the flavours are well absorbed.  !
  10. finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy**Pitod Ki Sabji Recipe** with roti or rice.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, over cooking the besan makes besan katli hard.
  * also, adjust spices to your preferences. however, the gravy tastes great when prepared spicy.
  * additionally, keep stirring the curd mixture to prevent curd curdling.
  * finally,**Pitod Ki Sabji Recipe** thickens once cooled, so adjust the consistency accordingly.

# Recipe 146
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/rajasthani-kadhi-recipe-thin-marwadi/

### Rajasthani Kadhi video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## Recipe Card for thin marwadi kadhi:
!

## Rajasthani Kadhi Recipe | Thin & Spicy No Pakoda Marwadi Kadhi
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy Rajasthani Kadhi Recipe | Thin & Spicy No Pakoda Marwadi Kadhi
3.80 from 5 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course curry
Cuisine rajasthani
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 227 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for marwadi kadhi:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω cup curd
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup besan / gram flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp fennel
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp methi
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 pods cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, finely chopped

#### for tempering
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, chopped

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl take 1¬Ω cup curd, ¬º cup besan, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt.
  * whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.
  * now add 4 cup water and mix well. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, ¬Ω tsp fennel, ¬º tsp methi, 1 bay leaf, 4 cloves, 2 pods cardamom, few curry leaves and pinch hing.
  * also add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and saute well.
  * now pour in the prepared besan curd mixture and mix well.
  * keep stirring until the mixture comes to a boil. the kadhi starts to thicken.
  * boil for 30 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed.
  * to prepare the tempering heat 1 tbsp ghee. add ¬Ω tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 2 dried red chilli, ¬º tsp chilli powder and mix well without burning.
  * pour the tempering over the kadhi. also, add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.
  * finally, enjoy Rajasthani Kadhi with jeera rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 227kcalCarbohydrates: 11gProtein: 11gFat: 16gSaturated Fat: 8gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 5gCholesterol: 29mgSodium: 636mgPotassium: 229mgFiber: 3gSugar: 3gVitamin A: 415IUVitamin C: 38mgCalcium: 157mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to make rajasthani kadhi with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl take 1¬Ω cup curd, ¬º cup besan, ¬Ω tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt.  !
  2. whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.  !
  3. now add 4 cup water and mix well. keep aside.  !
  4. in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, ¬Ω tsp fennel, ¬º tsp methi, 1 bay leaf, 4 cloves, 2 pods cardamom, few curry leaves and pinch hing.  !
  5. also add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger and saute well.  !
  6. now pour in the prepared besan curd mixture and mix well.  !
  7. keep stirring until the mixture comes to a boil. the kadhi starts to thicken.  !
  8. boil for 30 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed.  !
  9. to prepare the tempering heat 1 tbsp ghee. add ¬Ω tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp cumin, 2 dried red chilli, ¬º tsp chilli powder and mix well without burning.  !
  10. pour the tempering over the kadhi. also, add 2 tbsp coriander and mix well.  !
  11. finally, enjoy **Rajasthani Kadhi** with jeera rice.  !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to whisk and mix well, as if there are lumps then kadhi will not come out good.
  * also, adjust the amount of spices based on your spice level.
  * additionally, the kadhi thickens once cooled. so adjust the consistency accordingly.
  * finally, **Rajasthani Kadhi** recipe tastes great when prepared with homemade ghee.

# Recipe 147
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/panchmel-dal-recipe-pancharatna-dal/

### panchmel dal video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for pancharatna dal recipe:
!

## panchmel dal recipe | pancharatna dal | rajasthani dal panchratan
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy panchmel dal recipe | pancharatna dal | rajasthani dal panchratan
4.84 from 31 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Soaking Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 10 minutes mins
Course dal
Cuisine rajasthan
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 276 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for pressure cooking:
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup toor dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup moong dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup masoor dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water

#### for dal:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 bay leaf
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cloves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 black cardamom
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ginger garlic paste
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp coriander powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tomato, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp kasuri methi, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a bowl take ¬º cup toor dal, ¬º cup urad dal, ¬º cup moong dal, ¬º cup masoor dal and ¬º cup chana dal.
  * rinse well and soak for 30 minutes.
  * transfer the soaked dal into the pressure cooker.
  * add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 bay leaf, 1 tsp ghee and 3 cups water.
  * pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked completely.
  * once the pressure releases, open the cooker and check if the dal is cooked well. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 bay leaf, 4 cloves, 1 black cardamom, 1 tsp cumin and 1 dried red chilli.
  * saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic.
  * now add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until onions turn golden brown.
  * further add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬Ω tsp salt.
  * saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * add 2 tomato and saute until the tomatoes turn soft and mushy.
  * now add cooked dal and mix well adjusting consistency as required.
  * cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed.
  * further add ¬º tsp garam masala, 1 tsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well.
  * to prepare the tempering, heat 1 tsp ghee. add 1 tsp cumin, ¬º tsp chilli powder and 1 dried red chilli.
  * immediately pour the tempering over dal. make sure the tadka doesn't get burnt.
  * finally, enjoy panchmel dal or pancharatna dal with roti or jeera rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 276kcalCarbohydrates: 34gProtein: 12gFat: 11gSaturated Fat: 6gCholesterol: 26mgSodium: 623mgPotassium: 290mgFiber: 10gSugar: 4gVitamin A: 818IUVitamin C: 17mgCalcium: 90mgIron: 4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make panchmel dal with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, in a bowl take ¬º cup toor dal, ¬º cup urad dal, ¬º cup moong dal, ¬º cup masoor dal and ¬º cup chana dal. !
  2. rinse well and soak for 30 minutes. !
  3. transfer the soaked dal into the pressure cooker. !
  4. add ¬Ω tsp turmeric, ¬Ω tsp salt, 2 bay leaf, 1 tsp ghee and 3 cups water. !
  5. pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked completely. !
  6. once the pressure releases, open the cooker and check if the dal is cooked well. keep aside. !
  7. in a large kadai heat 2 tbsp ghee. add 1 bay leaf, 4 cloves, 1 black cardamom, 1 tsp cumin and 1 dried red chilli. !
  8. saute on low flame until the spices turn aromatic. !
  9. now add 1 onion, 1 tsp ginger garlic paste and saute until onions turn golden brown. !
  10. further add ¬º tsp turmeric, 1 tsp chilli powder, 1 tsp coriander powder, ¬Ω tsp cumin powder and ¬Ω tsp salt. !
  11. saute until the spices turn aromatic. !
  12. add 2 tomato and saute until the tomatoes turn soft and mushy. !
  13. now add cooked dal and mix well adjusting consistency as required. !
  14. cover and simmer for 10 minutes or until the flavours are well absorbed. !
  15. further add ¬º tsp garam masala, 1 tsp kasuri methi and 2 tbsp coriander. mix well. !
  16. to prepare the tempering, heat 1 tsp ghee. add 1 tsp cumin, ¬º tsp chilli powder and 1 dried red chilli. !
  17. immediately pour the tempering over dal. make sure the tadka doesn‚Äôt get burnt. !
  18. finally, enjoy **panchmel dal** or**pancharatna dal** with roti or jeera rice. !

## notes:
  * firstly, i have taken an equal proportion of 5 different dal. however, you can adjust the quantity to your choice.
  * also, make sure to soak the dal for at least 30 minutes, else the dal will not cook uniformly.
  * additionally, simmering on low flame helps to absorb flavour.
  * finally,**panchmel dal or pancharatna dal recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly thick.

# Recipe 148
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/moong-dal-halwa-moong-dal-sheera/

### moong dal halwa video recipe:

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## recipe card for moong ki daal ka halwa recipe:
!

## moong dal halwa | moong ki daal ka halwa | moong dal sheera
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy moong dal halwa | moong ki daal ka halwa | moong dal sheera
4.98 from 191 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 1 hour hr
Soaking Time 2 hours hrs
Total Time 3 hours hrs 10 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine north indian
Servings 6 Servings
Calories 455 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup moong dal
  * ‚ñ¢ water, for soaking
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup 
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp rava / semolina / suji
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 cashew, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 5 almond, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder

### Instructions 
  * firstly, rinse the moong dal and soak for 2 hours.
  * drain off the water and transfer to a blender.
  * blend to a slightly coarse paste adding water if required. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat ¬Ω cup ghee and add 1 tbsp rava.
  * roast on low flame until the rava turns aromatic. adding rava helps to give good texture to halwa.
  * now add in prepared moong dal paste and mix well.
  * keeping the flame on medium, mix until the moong dal absorbs the ghee.
  * continue to cook breaking the lumps.
  * cook until the mixture turns crumble and grainy texture.
  * after 20 minutes, the mixture turns crisp.
  * now add 2 cup milk, few saffron. you can alternatively use water or milk and water combination.
  * stir continuously, until the mixture absorbs all the milk.
  * the mixture will start to hold shape leaving the kadai.
  * now add 1 cup sugar and mix well.
  * the sugar starts to melt and turns the mixture watery.
  * continue to cook on low flame breaking lumps in between.
  * cook until the mixture starts to separate the ghee and turns golden brown. take approximately 60 minutes.
  * now add 5 cashew, 5 almond and ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder. mix well.
  * finally, enjoy moong dal halwa garnished with more nuts.

### Nutrition
Calories: 455kcalCarbohydrates: 60gProtein: 12gFat: 19gSaturated Fat: 11gCholesterol: 49mgSodium: 181mgPotassium: 121mgFiber: 4gSugar: 38gVitamin A: 671IUCalcium: 112mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make moong dal halwa with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, rinse the moong dal and soak for 2 hours. !
  2. drain off the water and transfer to a blender. !
  3. blend to a slightly coarse paste adding water if required. keep aside. !
  4. in a large kadai heat ¬Ω cup ghee and add 1 tbsp rava. !
  5. roast on low flame until the rava turns aromatic. adding rava helps to give good texture to halwa. !
  6. now add in prepared moong dal paste and mix well. !
  7. keeping the flame on medium, mix until the moong dal absorbs the ghee. !
  8. continue to cook breaking the lumps. !
  9. cook until the mixture turns crumble and grainy texture. after 20 minutes, the mixture turns crisp. !
  10. now add 2 cup milk, few saffron. you can alternatively use water or milk and water combination. !
  11. stir continuously, until the mixture absorbs all the milk. !
  12. the mixture will start to hold shape leaving the kadai. !
  13. now add 1 cup sugar and mix well. !
  14. the sugar starts to melt and turns the mixture watery. !
  15. continue to cook on low flame breaking lumps in between. !
  16. cook until the mixture starts to separate the ghee and turns golden brown. take approximately 60 minutes. !
  17. now add 5 cashew, 5 almond and ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder. mix well. !
  18. finally, enjoy **moong dal halwa** garnished with more nuts. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to cook the halwa on low to medium flame else the dal will change colour without getting cooked well.
  * also, you can add a pinch of food colour to prepare halwai style halwa.
  * additionally, adding milk helps to enhance the flavour of sheera. you can also add khowa to make it richer.
  * finally, **moong dal halwa recipe** tastes great when prepared with homemade ghee.

# Recipe 149

### dahi ki chatni video recipe:

## recipe card for dahi ki chatni recipe:
!

## dahi ki chatni recipe | dahi chutney recipe | dahi lahsun ki chutney
HEBBARS KITCHEN
easy dahi ki chatni recipe | dahi chutney recipe | dahi lahsun ki chutney
5 from 191 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Soaking Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 55 minutes mins
Course chutney
Cuisine rajasthan
Servings 1 box
Calories 883 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ hot water, for soaking
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 inch ginger, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper

#### !for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing / asafoetida
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 clove garlic, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup curd, whisked
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt

### Instructions 
  * firstly, soak 10 dried red chilli in hot water for 30 minutes. keep aside.
  * in a pan, heat 1 tbsp oil and ¬Ω cup garlic.
  * saute on medium flame until the garlic turns golden brown.
  * now add 2 inch ginger and saute well.
  * also add in soaked dried red chilli and cook for a minute.
  * further add 2 tbsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin and ¬Ω tsp pepper.
  * saute until the spices turn aromatic.
  * cool completely and transfer to the blender.
  * blend to smooth paste adding water as required. keep aside.
  * in a large kadai heat 3 tbsp oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, pinch thing, few curry leaves.
  * add 3 clove garlic and saute until the garlic changes colour.
  * further add in garlic chilli paste and cook well.
  * now add 1 cup curd and stir continuously.
  * keep stir until the curd is well combined with the chilli garlic paste.
  * once the curd is well combined add 1 tsp salt and mix well.
  * cover and cook for 10 minutes or until oil separates.
  * finally, dahi garlic chutney is ready to enjoy with roti or rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 883kcalCarbohydrates: 42gProtein: 30gFat: 70gSaturated Fat: 6gSodium: 2434mgPotassium: 567mgFiber: 8gSugar: 2gVitamin A: 297IUVitamin C: 26mgCalcium: 558mgIron: 8mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## how to make dahi chutney with step by step photo:
  1. firstly, soak 10 dried red chilli in hot water for 30 minutes. keep aside. !
  2. in a pan, heat 1 tbsp oil and ¬Ω cup garlic. !
  3. saute on medium flame until the garlic turns golden brown. !
  4. now add 2 inch ginger and saute well. !
  5. also, add in soaked dried red chilli and cook for a minute. !
  6. further add 2 tbsp coriander seeds, 1 tsp cumin and ¬Ω tsp pepper. !
  7. saute until the spices turn aromatic. !
  8. cool completely and transfer to the blender. !
  9. blend to smooth paste adding water as required. keep aside. !
  10. in a large kadai heat 3 tbsp oil and splutter 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp cumin, pinch thing, few curry leaves. !
  11. add 3 clove garlic and saute until the garlic changes colour. !
  12. further, add in garlic chilli paste and cook well. !
  13. now add 1 cup curd and stir continuously. !
  14. keep stir until the curd is well combined with the chilli garlic paste. !
  15. once the curd is well combined add 1 tsp salt and mix well. !
  16. cover and cook for 10 minutes or until oil separates. !
  17. finally, **dahi garlic chutney** is ready to enjoy with roti or rice. !

## notes:
  * firstly, make sure to whisk the curd really well before adding, else there are chances for the curd to curdle.
  * also, adjust the amount of red chilli based on the spice level you are looking for.
  * additionally, a generous amount of oil acts as a preservative. so do not compromise in oil usage.
  * finally, **dahi garlic chutney recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly spicy.

# Recipe 150

## About Shavige Uppittu
This is a straightforward South Indian breakfast recipe prepared with vermicelli noodles, coconut, and special masala. **Shavige Uppittu** , known as Shavige Bath in Karnataka, is a popular morning breakfast or snack recipe. It is typically served with a combination of idli and dosa with spiced coconut chutney or sev mixture. The spicy coconut chutney and these non-sticky spiced noodles make it unique and special with a lip-smacking taste.
There are many types of **Shavige Bath** or **Shavige Uppittu** across South India. The typical way to make this recipe is with thin vermicelli noodles and freshly ground coconut masala. Other spices and herbs are also used, making it a simple and easy morning breakfast. Adding coconut is optional, and it can be made without it. Different types of vermicelli noodles are available in the market. These can be used, and their size and thickness typically vary.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Shavige Uppittu
!

## Shavige Uppittu Recipe | Shavige Bath - Shavige Upma
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Shavige Uppittu Recipe | Shavige Bath Recipe | Shavige Upma Recipe**
4.99 from 190 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 15 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine karnataka
Servings 3 Servings
Calories 205 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 cup rice semiya
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp peanut
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 carrot, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp peas
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 capsicum, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 beans, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp coconut, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tsp lemon juice

### Instructions 
  * Heat water in a large vessel. Add 1 tsp salt and 2 tsp oil. Bring to a boil.
  * Add 2 cup rice semiya and boil for 3 minutes. Check the package instructions for boiling time.
  * Once the semiya is cooked, drain off the water and rinse with cold water. Keep aside.
  * In a large kadai, heat 2 tablespoons oil and fry 2 tablespoons of peanuts until they turn crunchy. Keep aside.
  * Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp urad dal, ¬Ω tsp chana dal, ¬Ω tsp cumin, pinch hing and a few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.
  * Also add 1 chilli, 1 inch ginger, 1 onion and saute well.
  * Further add 1 carrot, 3 tbsp peas, 1 capsicum, 1 beans, 1 tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp turmeric.
  * Stir fry till the vegetables turn crunchy.
  * Now add in cooked semiya and mix gently.
  * Also add fried peanuts, 3 tbsp coconut, 2 tbsp coriander, and 2 tsp lemon juice.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Finally, enjoy Shavige Bhat Recipe with chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 205kcalCarbohydrates: 16gProtein: 5gFat: 15gSaturated Fat: 3gPolyunsaturated Fat: 4gMonounsaturated Fat: 8gTrans Fat: 0.04gSodium: 819mgPotassium: 445mgFiber: 5gSugar: 6gVitamin A: 4981IUVitamin C: 92mgCalcium: 56mgIron: 2mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Shavige Bath with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Heat water in a large vessel. Add 1 tsp salt and 2 tsp oil. Bring to a boil.  !
  2. Add 2 cup rice semiya and boil for 3 minutes. Check the package instructions for boiling time.  !
  3. Once the semiya is cooked, drain off the water and rinse with cold water. Keep aside.  !
  4. In a large kadai, heat 2 tablespoons oil and fry 2 tablespoons of peanuts until they turn crunchy. Keep aside.  !
  5. Add 1 tsp mustard, ¬Ω tsp urad dal, ¬Ω tsp chana dal, ¬Ω tsp cumin, pinch hing and a few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.  !
  6. Also add 1 chilli, 1 inch ginger, 1 onion and saute well.  !
  7. Further add 1 carrot, 3 tbsp peas, 1 capsicum, 1 beans, 1 tsp salt and ¬Ω tsp turmeric.  !
  8. Stir fry till the vegetables turn crunchy.  !
  9. Now add in cooked semiya and mix gently.  !
  10. Also add fried peanuts, 3 tbsp coconut, 2 tbsp coriander, and 2 tsp lemon juice.  !
  11. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  12. Finally, enjoy **Shavige Bhat Recipe** with chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure not to overcook shavige as it turns sticky.
  * Also, you can add vegetables of your choice making upma healthy.
  * Additionally, add vermicelli only after the water comes to a boil else the semiya will turn sticky.
  * Finally, **Shavige Uppittu Recipe** or **Shavige Bhat Recipe** tastes great when prepared slightly spicy and tangy.

# Recipe 151
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/medu-vada-recipe-medhu-vadai/

####

####

00:02:12

## About Medu Vada
The **Medu vada recipe** is mainly prepared by soaking the urad dal for 3 hours, which is ground to a smooth paste later. It is later flavoured with ginger, green chillies, dried coconut, coriander and curry leaves. Further, it is shaped into doughnuts and deep-fried in hot oil until golden brown and crisp. These crisp and crunchy vadas are an ideal breakfast snack, typically served with steamed idli or dosa. It can be dipped in a spicy sambar or served with coconut or red chutney.
There are many different ways to make a **Medu Vada Recipe** , and the variation mainly depends on the type of toppings or flour used. The authentic recipe is made with ground urad dal with basic spices and herbs toppings. However, it can also be made with rava, other lentils, bread, Poha and maida flour. In addition, all these different types of vadas can be topped with a wide range of herbs. You can add spinach, dill leaves, pudina and coriander leaves to make it flavour.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Medu Vada
!

## Medu Vada Recipe in Mixer Grinder | Medhu Vadai
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy **Medu Vada Recipe in Mixer Grinder | Uddina Vada | Medhu Vadai | Ulundu Vadai**
4.99 from 200 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 15 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Soaking Time 8 hours hrs
Total Time 8 hours hrs 35 minutes mins
Course Breakfast, snacks
Cuisine south indian
Servings 20 Servings
Calories 39 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp rice
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for frying

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup urad dal, 2 tbsp rice and rinse well.
  * Soak for 6 to 8 hours making sure the dal is soaked well.
  * Drain off the water and transfer to the mixer jar. You can also grind in grinder for better texture.
  * Grind to smooth paste adding water as required. Make sure to add very little water as it helps to make the batter thick.
  * Transfer the fluffy batter to a large plate.
  * Add a pinch hing ¬æ tsp salt and whisk well.
  * This helps to incorporate air in the batter and make the batter fluffy.
  * Also add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger, 2 tbsp coriander, few curry leaves, and 1 tsp cumin.
  * Mix well making sure everything is well combined.
  * Now you can shape the vada using a tea strainer. Make sure to wet your hands and tea strainer. Place a ball-sized batter and make a hole in center.
  * Drop down gently in medium hot oil.
  * Flip over and fry on low to medium flame.
  * Fry till the vada turns golden brown and crispy. Drain off.
  * Finally, enjoy Medu Vada Recipe with chutney and sambar.

### Nutrition
Calories: 39kcalCarbohydrates: 7gProtein: 3gFat: 0.1gSaturated Fat: 0.01gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.02gMonounsaturated Fat: 0.02gSodium: 89mgPotassium: 28mgFiber: 2gSugar: 0.3gVitamin A: 56IUVitamin C: 8mgCalcium: 11mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Medu Vada with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup urad dal, 2 tbsp rice and rinse well.  !
  2. Soak for 6 to 8 hours making sure the dal is soaked well.  !
  3. Drain off the water and transfer to the mixer jar. You can also grind in grinder for better texture.  !
  4. Grind to smooth paste adding water as required. Make sure to add very little water as it helps to make the batter thick.  !
  5. Transfer the fluffy batter to a large plate.  !
  6. Add a pinch hing ¬æ tsp salt and whisk well.  !
  7. This helps to incorporate air in the batter and make the batter fluffy.  !
  8. Also add 2 chilli, 1 inch ginger, 2 tbsp coriander, few curry leaves, and 1 tsp cumin.  !
  9. Mix well making sure everything is well combined.  !
  10. Now you can shape the vada using a tea strainer. Make sure to wet your hands and tea strainer. Place a ball-sized batter and make a hole in center.  !
  11. Drop down gently in medium hot oil.  !
  12. Flip over and fry on low to medium flame.  !
  13. Fry till the vada turns golden brown and crispy. Drain off.  !
  14. Finally, enjoy **Medu Vada Recipe** with chutney and sambar.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, grind to a smooth and thick batter, as it helps shape the vada easily.
  * Also, you can add rice flour if the batter is watery. This helps to make vada crispy too.
  * Additionally, you can also add onions to get a crunchy bite.
  * Finally, **Medu Vada Recipe** can be reheated in air fryer or double-fried to make it crispier.

# Recipe 152

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

## About Insatnt Rava Dosa:
It is a popular South Indian breakfast instant dosa recipe with essential ingredients like semolina, rice flour, and plain flour. **Rava Dosa** is a favourite dosa, particularly in metro cities like Bangalore and Chennai, and is served with spicy red and white coconut chutney. Unlike the traditional dosa recipe made with soaking and grounding, this dosa batter is made instantly by mixing water with all dry ingredients.
It is a popular choice, particularly in metro cities, for its unique characteristics. Firstly, it is super crisp, has a thin, flaky texture, and provides an enjoyable experience when served with spicy chutney or flavoured kurma recipes. There are many variations to this simple,e instant dosa recipe, but the texture and taste almost remain the same. Even though this recipe is straightforward, it needs some simple mandatory tips for the best results.

## Why does this Recipe Work?
Several key factors are highlights of this recipe, but the most important factors are
  1. **Super Crispy Texture** ‚Äì The traditional dosa varies with texture, but the suji ka dosa has a crisp, flaky texture, which makes it unique and special compared to all other dosa.
  2. **Instant Preparation** ‚Äì This rava dose requires no planning, soaking, or grounding. The dosa batter is prepared instantly by mixing water directly with dry flour and ingredients.
  3. **Versatility** ‚Äì The batter can easily experiment with various toppings, finely chopped vegetables, and herbs. Each additional ingredient adds a new flavour and a unique taste to it.
  4. **Suitable for Dietary requirements** ‚Äì The ingredients used in this **instant Rava Dosa** are essential and can easily match any dietary requirements. There are no dairy products, and hence, vegan safe and also for vegetarians.
  5. **Instant Rava Dosa Mix** ‚Äì The recipe can also be extended and prepared as an instant mix for future use. Avoid adding vegetables and herbs to the instant mix, as it may not be suitable for a longer shelf life.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Instant Rava Dosa
!

## Rava Dosa Recipe | Instant Crispy Suji Ka Dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy rava dosa recipe | instant rava dosa | suji ka dosa | crispy rava dosa
4.95 from 340 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Resting Time 25 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 10 dosa

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rava / semolina / suji, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rice flour, fine
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup maida / all purpose flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp , optional
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω water
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large mixing bowl take ¬Ω cup rava, ¬Ω cup rice flour and ¬º cup maida.
  * also add 1 tbsp curd, 1 tsp salt and 2¬Ω cup water.
  * whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.
  * further add 1 chilli, 1 inch ginger, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 tsp cumin, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander and 1 onion.
  * add 1¬Ω cup water and prepare a watery consistency batter.
  * rest the batter for 20 minutes making sure the rava has absorbed water.
  * mix well making sure the batter is thin watery consistency.
  * now carefully pour the dosa batter over very hot tawa.
  * lower the flame and cook until the dosa turns golden and crisp.
  * finally, fold the dosa and serve rava dosa immediately with tomato chutney or coconut chutney.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Rava Dosa with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, take ¬Ω cup rava, ¬Ω cup rice flour, and ¬º cup maida in a large mixing bowl. !
  2. Also add 1 tbsp curd, 1 tsp salt and 2¬Ω cup water. !
  3. Whisk and mix well, making sure there are no lumps. !
  4. Further add one chilli, 1-inch ginger, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 tsp cumin, a few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander, and one onion. !
  5. Add 1¬Ω cup water and prepare a watery consistency batter. !
  6. Rest the batter for 20 minutes, making sure the rava has absorbed water. !
  7. Mix well, making sure the batter is thin and watery consistent. !
  8. Now carefully pour the dosa batter over very hot tawa. Do not fill the holes, as the texture of the dosa will spoil. !
  9. Also, spread a tsp of oil uniformly. !
  10. Lower the flame and cook until the dosa turns golden and crisp. !
  11. Finally, fold the dosa and serve**it** immediately with  or . !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, prepare a flowing consistency batter, or the dosa will not be crisp.
  * Also, if you are vegan, then skip adding curd. However, adding curd gives a nice flavour.
  * Additionally, you can add dry coconut pieces and cashew pieces into the batter.
  * Finally, the **rava dosa recipe** tastes excellent when served hot and crispy.

## Faqs

### What is rava dosa? What goes well with rava dosa?
Rava dosa is a popular crepe south Indian recipe made of semolina, rice flour, and maida. they do not require any grinding or fermentation, making an instant dosa. The rava dosa batter is thin compared to regular urad dal dosa batter, which yields crispy and flaky dosa. it is served for morning breakfast or evening snacks with coconut chutney, spicy chutney, veg kurma, sagu, or sambar.

### How to get a crispy rava dosa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-12.jpeg> "crispy rava dosa")

### What are the ingredients of rava dosa and how to prepare rava dosa?
rava dosa is usually prepared with semolina, rice flour, maida, spices, and fresh herbs. First, take a bowl and add rava, rice flour, and maida to it. rava and rice flour should be in the same proportions, and maida should be half of the rava and rice flour. add salt, 1 tbsp of curd, and water to it. also, add chopped chilli, curry leaves, ginger, pepper, cumin seeds, and coriander leaves. add more water to prepare a flowing consistency batter. rest the batter for 20 minutes. sp that the rava absorbs water. pour the batter into the hot tawa and roast in low flame until the dosa leaves the tawa or turns golden brown and crisp.

### What are the other variants to prepare tasty rava dosa?
Adding chopped onions to the rava dosa batter makes onion rava dosa and adding aloo bhaji while roasting the dosa yields rava masala dosa just like traditional masala dosa. adding dry fruits to the dosa makes it a dry fruit rava dosa. the addition of finely chopped or grated veggies makes vegetable rava dosa. also, chopped cashew nuts and coconut pieces can be added to the batter, making the dosa more tasty and crunchy in every bite. adding curd to the dosa gives the golden colour and a good flavour to the dosa.

### Why does rava dosa stick to the tawa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-10.jpeg> "instant rava dosa")
Always use a heavy bottom pan or well-seasoned cast-iron tawa to make rava dosa. An iron skillet pan is the best for preparing dosas. Seasoned tawa is the one that is used earlier to prepare dosa. grease the pan well and rub it with a slice of onion before pouring each dosa. Also, do not use the same tawa when preparing roti or chapati. maintain the tawa separately for both. If the dosa sticks to the non-stick tawa, pour some batter into it and prepare a small dosa. After 2-3 dosas, the dosas won‚Äôt stick to the pan as the tawa would be hot.

### Why is my rava dosa soft and not crispy?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-9.jpeg> "instant rava dosa")
You need to use Bombay rava or fine rava. The batter should be thin and watery in consistency, not thick or medium. Medium-consistency batter also yields soft dosa. add water to the dosa batter to adjust the consistency. Adding more curd to the batter may yield soft dosas. The tawa should be very hot, and the flame should be low soon after pouring the batter into the tawa. Mix well every time you pour the batter on the tawa, and the rava and other flours settle down. Use a heavy bottom pan or cast iron tawa to prepare dosa so that it does not stick to the tawa and helps to get crispy dosa. also, serve dosa hot. else when they cool down, they turn soft.

### Should we flip over the dosa and roast on both sides in rava dosa?
Flipping of dosa is not required while roasting the rava dosa. When the dosa is cooked well, fold and remove it from the tawa. All the dosa needn‚Äôt be cooked on both sides. If the dosas are getting brown at the bottom and still moist on the top side, you may need to flip over the dosa and roast it on the other side until it turns crisp. So, as soon as the dosa is poured into the tawa, adjust the flame to low. cover and roast until the edges leave the tawa. Do not forcibly remove the dosa from the pan. A cooked dosa leaves the tawa, which indicates the cooking is done.

### How to pour the rava dosa batter into the tawa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-7.jpeg> "rava dosa recipe")
The batter should be mainly thin or watery like flowing consistency. Only then is it possible to pour the batter. unlike traditional dosa, the batter is poured on the tawa, and the batter is not spread. pour it all over the tawa, beginning from the edges and towards the centre, and do not pour the batter in one place. fill the gaps by pouring the batter into them. cover and roast in low flame until it leaves the pan.

### What does my rava dosa break?
When you pour the batter into the tawa, make sure the batter is thin and flowing consistency. if it‚Äôs too skinny, the dosa might break. so add rice flour, maida, and rava according to their proportion and adjust the consistency, pour the batter into the pan.

### how to season the dosa tawa?
dosa tawa can be seasoned in the following ways: rub the tawa with gingelly oil and soak it in washed rice water for a week. rub the tawa with half the onion before spreading the dosas. heat the tawa, sprinkle salt, switch off the flame, wipe with a cloth and grease oil after it cools. clean the tawa with hot water and rub it with oil. Please keep it in the oven for one-hour upside down. Also, please do not wash the tawa when it is too hot, and do not put cold liquids on the cast iron tawa. avoid hard soaps, detergents, and steel scrubbers.

# Recipe 153

## About Murmura Snack Chiwda
A classical Indian snack recipe prepared with essential ingredients like puffed rice, fried snacks and fried peanuts. **Murmura Chivda** , commonly known as **Chiwda Murmura** , is a vital tea-time evening snack. It is widely appreciated by all age groups, particularly kids, and goes very well with any hot beverage. Recipes made from puffed rice are typically considered gluten-free, low-calorie, low-fat ingredients and ideal snack recipes.
There are many ways a simple **Murmura Chivda snack** can be prepared. The most common way is to dry roast the puffed rice with spice powders in a small quantity of oil. It is then tossed with fried ingredients like peanuts, dry coconut, sev mixture, lentils and red chillies. Additionally, adding finely chopped onions and tomatoes can give extra flavour and taste to the snack. However, adding any wet ingredients reduces its shelf life. Further, fried thick poha can add flavour and taste to Murmura Snack.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Murmura Snack Chivda
!

## Murmura Snack Recipe | Spicy Murmura Chivda - Bakery Style
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Murmura Recipe | Spicy Puffed Rice | Spicy Murmura Chivda**
5 from 198 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 5 minutes mins
Total Time 10 minutes mins
Course snacks
Cuisine south indian
Servings 1 Box
Calories 1310 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup peanuts
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp cashew
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp almonds
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp dry coconut, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 big bowl  murmura / puffed rice
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chilli powder
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp black salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp powdered sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp aamchur
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a large kadai heat 3 tbsp oil and fry ¬æ cup peanuts on low flame.
  * Once the peanuts turn crunchy, keep them aside.
  * In the same oil, fry 2 tbsp cashew, 2 tbsp almonds, 2 tbsp dry coconut, few curry leaves, and 2 dried red chilli in batches.
  * Keep aside once they turn crunchy.
  * Keeping the flame on low, add 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt. Saute till the turmeric turns aromatic.
  * Now add 1 big bowl murmura and mix gently.
  * Fry for 3 minutes or until the murmura turns crunchy.
  * Transfer to the the large bowl, add 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp black salt, 1 tbsp powdered sugar, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, and pinch hing.
  * Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.
  * Add in fried nuts and mix well.
  * Finally, enjoy Murmura Chivda Recipe topped with chopped onions.

### Nutrition
Calories: 1310kcalCarbohydrates: 42gProtein: 37gFat: 119gSaturated Fat: 17gPolyunsaturated Fat: 35gMonounsaturated Fat: 62gTrans Fat: 0.2gSodium: 3554mgPotassium: 1223mgFiber: 16gSugar: 11gVitamin A: 653IUVitamin C: 1mgCalcium: 192mgIron: 8mg

## How to Make Murmura Snack with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a large kadai heat 3 tbsp oil and fry ¬æ cup peanuts on low flame.  !
  2. Once the peanuts turn crunchy, keep them aside.  !
  3. In the same oil, fry 2 tbsp cashew, 2 tbsp almonds, 2 tbsp dry coconut, few curry leaves, and 2 dried red chilli in batches.  !
  4. Keep aside once they turn crunchy.  !
  5. Keeping the flame on low, add 1 tsp turmeric and 1 tsp salt. Saute till the turmeric turns aromatic.  !
  6. Now add 1 big bowl murmura and mix gently.  !
  7. Fry for 3 minutes or until the murmura turns crunchy.  !
  8. Transfer to the the large bowl, add 1 tsp chilli powder, ¬Ω tsp black salt, 1 tbsp powdered sugar, ¬Ω tsp aamchur, and pinch hing.  !
  9. Mix well making sure all the spices are well combined.  !
  10. Add in fried nuts and mix well.  !
  11. Finally, enjoy **Murmura Chivda Recipe** topped with chopped onions.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, fry the nuts on low flame until they turn crunchy.
  * Also, you can add spices accordingly based on the spice level.
  * Additionally, you can also add a mixture or sev to make the chivda tasty.
  * Finally, **the Murmura Chivda recipe** tastes great when it is crunchy.

# Recipe 154

## About Badam Burfi
An excellent and tasty Indian sweet recipe made with a combination of powdered almond and desiccated coconut in a one-string sugar syrup. **Badam Burfi,** known as Badam Katli, is an ideal festival recipe for offering Prasadam to beloved gods. It can also be a perfect sweet snack and be served and exchanged with friends and family. In addition, it is also considered a healthy alternative compared to other dry fruits and sweets, significant because of Almonds.
There are many different ways to make this classical **Badam Burfi Recipe**. The variations mainly differ from the supporting ingredients added to this classical dessert. The typical combination is coconut, but it is not limited. It can take other dry fruit powders like cashews, pasta, and dates. Adding these makes it richer and premium, with just badam powder. In addition, adding rava, besan, and even wheat powder can give it a crunchy texture.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Badam Burfi
!

## Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi with Tips & Tricks
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Badam Burfi Recipe | Almond Burfi Recipe | Badam Katli Recipe**
5 from 203 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 1 hour hr
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Total Time 1 hour hr 15 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 20 Servings

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup badam / almonds
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup hot water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬æ cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp saffron milk
  * ‚ñ¢ 4 cardamom / elachi, powdered
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large bowl soak almonds in hot water for 1 hour.
  * now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.
  * also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.
  * transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.
  * meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.
  * keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.
  * boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.
  * now add the prepared almond powder, saffron milk and cardamom powder.
  * mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.
  * continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan.
  * transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.
  * and allow to cool for 5 minutes.
  * grease your hand with little ghee and knead for a minute.
  * once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin,.
  * furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.
  * you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  * finally, serve badam burfi / badam katli on diwali or any festival.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Badam Burfi with Step-by-step Photos

### badam powder or almond meal recipe:
  1. firstly, in a large bowl soak ¬æ cup of almonds in 1 cup of hot water for 1 hour.  !
  2. now slowly peel the skin from badam and keep aside.  !
  3. also pat dry the badam making sure there is no moisture present.  !
  4. transfer the badam into a small blender and blend to coarse powder. keep aside.  !

### badam buri | almond barfi recipe:
  1. meanwhile, prepare the sugar syrup by adding ¬æ cup sugar and ¬Ω cup water.  !
  2. keeping the flame on low, stir continuously.  !
  3. boil the sugar syrup till it forms one string consistency.  !
  4. now add the prepared almond powder.  !
  5. also add saffron milk. to prepare saffron milk, soak few strands of saffron in warm milk for 10 minutes.  !
  6. additionally add cardamom powder for more flavours.  !
  7. mix continuously keeping flame on low to medium.  !
  8. once the mixture begins to boil, add a tbsp of . however, it is optional, but do add more flavour to burfi.  !
  9. continue to mix continuously till the mixture starts to leave the pan. if you prefer slightly hard burfi then continue to stir for longer time.  !
  10. transfer the badam dough onto the butter paper.  !
  11. add a tsp of **** to make smooth dough.  !
  12. and allow to cool for 5 minutes. do not rest more, as they will turn hard and wont be able to give shape.  !
  13. grease your hand with little  and knead for a minute. be careful as the dough will be very hot. try to knead when its hot, else it will be difficult. and do not over knead as badam will start releasing oil.  !
  14. once you get smooth dough, roll the dough with a rolling-pin, adjusting the thickness according to your choice.  !
  15. furthermore, cut the dough into square shape or the shape you wish for.  !
  16. you can also decorate with silver leaf / silver vark.
  17. finally, serve **badam burfi / badam katli** on diwali or any festival. !

## Notes
  * firstly, soak the badam well or blanch it for easy removal of skin.
  * also, make sure to get just 1 string consistency of sugar syrup. else it turns burfi hard and brittle.
  * most noteworthy, use nonstick pan for easy and efficient badam katlis.
  * and entire badam burfi has to be prepared on low flame.
  * finally, instead of butter paper, you can also use a plastic sheet or greased plate to prepare **badam burfi.**

# Recipe 155

####

####

####

## About Atta Besan Ladoo
It is a simple combination of 2 recipes, i.e. wheat and besan ladoo, combined to make a classic Indian dessert recipe. Traditionally, besan ladoo is prepared during festivals and religious ceremonies. However, it can have health concerns, as chickpea flour can upset your stomach. Hence, to mitigate this problem, a new Laddu recipe is prepared. One is the Atta Ladoo, commonly called the **Atta Besan Ladoo recipe**. It has the same taste and crunchiness as besan but carries the health benefits of wheat flour.
There are many ways to make a simple and healthy **Atta Besan Ladoo recipe**. The most common way is to prepare it with a combination of wheat and chickpea flour with a 1:1 ratio. This gets the best of both. However, the ratio can be altered to make a unique sweet recipe. In addition, adding roasted rava or semolina makes it crisp and crunchy. Further, adding assorted dry fruits with dry ingredients makes it a memorable and premium sweet dessert recipe.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Atta Ladoo
!

## Atta Ladoo Recipe | Atta Besan Ladoo - Wheat Laddu
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Atta Ladoo Recipe | Atta Besan Ladoo | Wheat Laddu Recipe**
5 from 376 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 30 minutes mins
Total Time 40 minutes mins
Course sweet
Cuisine Indian
Servings 15 ladoo
Calories 172 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup ghee
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp gond / edible gum
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup wheat flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup besan
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp rava / suji, fine
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp melon seeds
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup sugar
  * ‚ñ¢ silver vark, for decoration

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, heat ¬Ω cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond on low flame.
  * Fry till the gond puffs up and turns crystal.
  * Drain off the gond and keep aside. Make sure to fry the gond on low flame, or else the gond will not get cooked from inside and will remain sticky while eating.
  * Add 1 cup wheat flour, 1 cup besan, and 2 tbsp rava in the same ghee.
  * Keep roasting on low flame till the flour is well combined.
  * Now add 1 tbsp ghee, 2 tbsp melon seeds and roast well.
  * Roast until the flour turns golden brown and aromatic.
  * Also, thee has been released from the flour, indicating the flour has roasted well.
  * Transfer to the large plate and cool slightly.
  * Add fried gond and crush slightly.
  * Also, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well. Mix making sure all the ingredients are well combined.
  * In a mixer jar take 1 cup sugar and grind to a fine powder.
  * Once the besan atta mixture has cooled add in powdered sugar and mix well. Make sure to add the sugar powder when the mixture is warm, or the sugar will melt.
  * Mix well till the mixture is well combined.
  * Prepare the ladoo by shaping them gently.
  * Finally, decorate the Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe with vark and chopped cashews.

### Nutrition
Calories: 172kcalCarbohydrates: 26gProtein: 3gFat: 7gSaturated Fat: 4gPolyunsaturated Fat: 1gMonounsaturated Fat: 2gCholesterol: 15mgSodium: 6mgPotassium: 81mgFiber: 1gSugar: 14gVitamin A: 3IUVitamin C: 0.01mgCalcium: 6mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Atta Ladoo with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, heat ¬Ω cup ghee and fry 2 tbsp gond on low flame.  !
  2. Fry till the gond puffs up and turns crystal.  !
  3. Drain off the gond and keep aside. Make sure to fry the gond on low flame, or else the gond will not get cooked from inside and will remain sticky while eating.  !
  4. Add 1 cup wheat flour, 1 cup besan, and 2 tbsp rava in the same ghee.  !
  5. Keep roasting on low flame till the flour is well combined.  !
  6. Now add 1 tbsp ghee, 2 tbsp melon seeds and roast well.  !
  7. Roast until the flour turns golden brown and aromatic.  !
  8. Also, the has been released from the flour, indicating the flour has roasted well.  !
  9. Transfer to the large plate and cool slightly.  !
  10. Add fried gond and crush slightly.  !
  11. Also, add ¬Ω tsp cardamom powder and mix well. Mix making sure all the ingredients are well combined.  !
  12. In a mixer jar take 1 cup sugar and grind to a fine powder.  !
  13. Once the besan atta mixture has cooled add in powdered sugar and mix well. Make sure to add the sugar powder when the mixture is warm, or the sugar will melt.  !
  14. Mix well till the mixture is well combined. Prepare the ladoo by shaping them gently.  !
  15. Finally, decorate the **Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe** with vark and chopped cashews.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, make sure to roast the besan and atta well, else the flour will remain raw.
  * Also, adding rava will give crunchy texture to the ladoo.
  * Additonally, you can add nuts of your choice to make the ladoo healthy.
  * Finally, **Atta Besan Ladoo Recipe** tastes great when prepared with fresh homemade ghee.

# Recipe 156

####

####

## About Instant Ragi Dosa
It is a simple and healthy South Indian dosa recipe prepared with ragi, rice, and rava flour. Instant Ragi Dosa, commonly known as finger millet dosa, is known for its health benefits. In addition, millet-based dosa or recipes are also tagged as weight loss recipes due to their filling-in nature. Further, all millet-based recipes are naturally low in glycemic index and ideal for diabetes or cholesterol patients.
There are many different ways to make this Instant Ragi Dosa recipe, but the most common way is to make it instant. There is no planning, soaking, or fermentation in the instant recipe. However, it can also be made traditionally with soaking and grounding. Once the batter is prepared, it can be fermented and prepared as a soft or crisp dosa. In addition, the instant way can be prepared with just ragi flour, but it may not be tasty.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Instant Ragi Dosa
!

## Ragi Dosa Recipe Instant & Healthy | Finger Millet Dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
**Easy Ragi Dosa Recipe | How to Make Instant Ragi Dosa | Finger Millet Dosa | Ragi Dose**
5 from 271 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Soaking Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 15 Servings
Calories 55 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup rice flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup ragi flour
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup rava / semolina, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω carrot, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup rice flour, ¬Ω cup ragi flour, and ¬º cup rava.
  * Also, add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp salt and 3 cup water.
  * Whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.
  * Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω carrot, 2 chilli, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander and 1 inch ginger.
  * Also, add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency.
  * When the pan is super hot, pour the batter on the pan.
  * Spread 1 tsp oil and roast for 2 minutes or until the dosa turns crisp.
  * Finally, enjoy the Crispy Ragi Dosa Recipe with chutney.
  * notes:
  * Firstly, adjust the consistency of the batter by adding water as required. If the batter is thick, then the dosa will be soft.
  * also, the chutney tastes great when prepared spicy.
  * Additionally, you can add maida for the batter to help with binding.
  * Finally, the crispy Crispy Ragi Dosa Recipe tastes great when served hot with spicy chutney.

### Nutrition
Calories: 55kcalCarbohydrates: 12gProtein: 1gFat: 0.3gSaturated Fat: 0.1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 0.1gMonounsaturated Fat: 0.1gSodium: 160mgPotassium: 61mgFiber: 1gSugar: 1gVitamin A: 414IUVitamin C: 11mgCalcium: 10mgIron: 0.4mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Ragi Dosa with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, in a bowl take 1 cup rice flour, ¬Ω cup ragi flour, and ¬º cup rava.  !
  2. Also, add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp salt and 3 cup water.  !
  3. Whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.  !
  4. Now add ¬Ω onion, ¬Ω carrot, 2 chilli, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander, and 1 inch ginger.  !
  5. Also, add 1 cup water and mix well adjusting the consistency.  !
  6. When the pan is super hot, pour the batter on the pan.  !
  7. Spread 1 tsp oil and roast for 2 minutes or until the dosa turns crisp.  !
  8. Finally, enjoy the **Crispy Ragi Dosa Recipe** with chutney.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, adjust the consistency of the batter by adding water as required. If the batter is thick, then the dosa will be soft.
  * also, the chutney tastes great when prepared spicy.
  * Additionally, you can add maida for the batter to help with binding.
  * Finally, the crispy**Crispy Ragi Dosa Recipe** tastes great when served hot with spicy chutney.

## Onion Tomato Chutney Recipe | Tomato Onion Chutney Recipe
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Onion Tomato Chutney Recipe | Tomato Onion Chutney Recipe
5 from 200 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 5 minutes mins
Cook Time 10 minutes mins
Total Time 15 minutes mins
Course chutney
Cuisine Indian
Servings 6 Servings
Calories 118 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cloves garlic
  * ‚ñ¢ 10 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω onion, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 tomato, sliced
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt

#### !for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp urad dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 dried red chilli
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, in a pan heat 2 tbsp oil and roast 2 tbsp urad dal till turns aromatic.
  * Add 1 inch of ginger, 3 cloves of garlic, and 10 dried red chilies. Roast until the chilies puff up.
  * Further saute ¬Ω onion, till the onion softens and raw smell is lost.
  * Add 3 tomato, ¬º tsp turmeric, and cook until the tomato softens and turns mushy.
  * Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.
  * Add 1 tsp salt and grind to a smooth paste adding water as required.
  * Transfer the chutney to the large bowl and adjust the consistency by adding water as required.
  * To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp urad dal, 1 tsp mustard, 2 dried red chillies, a pinch of hing, and a few curry leaves.
  * Splutter the tempering and pour over the chutney.
  * Finally, enjoy Tomato Onion Chutney Recipe with dosa, idli, and rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 118kcalCarbohydrates: 7gProtein: 2gFat: 10gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 3gMonounsaturated Fat: 6gTrans Fat: 0.04gSodium: 404mgPotassium: 177mgFiber: 2gSugar: 2gVitamin A: 573IUVitamin C: 10mgCalcium: 16mgIron: 1mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Onion Tomato Chutney with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, heat 2 tbsp oil in a pan and roast 2 tbsp urad dal until it turns aromatic.  !
  2. Add 1 inch of ginger, three garlic cloves, and 10 dried red chilies. Roast until the chilies puff up.  !
  3. Further, saute ¬Ω onion till the onion softens and the raw smell is lost.  !
  4. Add three tomatoes and ¬º tsp turmeric, and cook until the tomato softens and turns mushy.  !
  5. Cool completely, and transfer to the mixer jar.  !
  6. Add 1 tsp salt and grind to a smooth paste, adding water as required.  !
  7. Transfer the chutney to the large bowl and adjust the consistency by adding water as required.  !
  8. To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add ¬Ω tsp urad dal, 1 tsp mustard, two dried red chillies, a pinch of hing, and a few curry leaves.  !
  9. Splutter the tempering and pour over the chutney.  !
  10. Finally, enjoy a **Tomato Onion Chutney Recipe** with dosa, idli, and rice.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, add a small piece of tamarind if the tomatoes are not tangy enough.
  * Also, you can add coconut while grinding the chutney. However, the shelf life of chutney will be reduced.
  * Additionally, use Kashmiri red chilli to give the chutney a bright red.
  * Finally, when prepared spicy and tangy, the **Tomato Onion Chutney Recipe** tastes excellent.

# Recipe 158
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/mango-dal-recipe-mamidikaya-pappu-raw-mango-pappu-recipe/

## About Mango Dal
It is a tangy and flavoured South Indian Dal recipe prepared with purposed-based raw sour mangoes and a thick cooked and mashed lentil. **Raw Mango Pappu** , commonly known as **Mamidikaya Pappu** in Telugu, is a popular delicacy from Andhra cuisine. It is typically served with hot steamed rice with a hot ghee topping and spicy mango pickle as a side or condiments. It can also be an excellent choice as a curry with a wide range of Indian flatbreads.
There are many different variations to this simple and easy **Raw Mango Dal** or **Mango Pappu Recipe**. The most common way is to make it with a combination of toor dal and raw mangoes with a thick consistency. The variations are mainly derived from its consistency. The same dal can also be made with a thin or semi-thick consistency. In addition, the dal can also be made with other types of lentils, like moong or masoor, for different textures and tastes.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Raw Mango Dal
!

## Mango Dal Recipe | Mamidikaya Pappu | Raw Mango Pappu
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy Mango Dal Recipe | Mamidikaya Pappu | Raw Mango Pappu
5 from 14 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 20 minutes mins
Total Time 30 minutes mins
Course Side Dish
Cuisine south indian
Servings 4 Servings
Calories 260 kcal

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x

#### for pressure cooking:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup toor dal
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 3 cup water

#### other ingredients:
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 raw mango, chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 6 chilli, slit
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º tsp turmeric
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped

#### for tempering:
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp oil
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp mustard
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp chana dal
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 dried red chilli, broke
  * ‚ñ¢ pinch hing
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves

### Instructions 
  * Firstly, take 1 cup toor dal, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp oil, and 3 cups water in a pressure cooker.
  * Pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked well.
  * Mash the dal slightly to get a silky smooth texture. Keep aside.
  * In a large kadai take 1 raw mango, 6 chilli, ¬º tsp turmeric, and 1 cup water.
  * Cover and boil for 10 minutes or until the mangoes are cooked well.
  * Add in pressure-cooked dal, 1 tsp salt, and mix well.
  * Simmer for 10 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed. Adjust the consistency as required.
  * To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp chana dal, 1 dried red chilli, pinch hing, and few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.
  * Pour the tempering over the dal and mix gently.
  * Finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy Mango Dal Recipe with hot steamed rice.

### Nutrition
Calories: 260kcalCarbohydrates: 38gProtein: 10gFat: 9gSaturated Fat: 1gPolyunsaturated Fat: 2gMonounsaturated Fat: 5gTrans Fat: 0.03gSodium: 647mgPotassium: 370mgFiber: 8gSugar: 12gVitamin A: 1276IUVitamin C: 122mgCalcium: 64mgIron: 3mg
Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Mango Dal Recipe with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, take 1 cup toor dal, ¬Ω tsp turmeric, 1 tsp oil, and 3 cups water in a pressure cooker.  !
  2. Pressure cook for 5 whistles or until the dal is cooked well.  !
  3. Mash the dal slightly to get a silky smooth texture. Keep aside.  !
  4. In a large kadai take 1 raw mango, 6 chilli, ¬º tsp turmeric, and 1 cup water.  !
  5. Cover and boil for 10 minutes or until the mangoes are cooked well.  !
  6. Add in pressure-cooked dal, 1 tsp salt, and mix well.  !
  7. Simmer for 10 minutes or until the flavors are well absorbed. Adjust the consistency as required.  !
  8. To prepare the tempering, heat 2 tbsp oil. Add 1 tsp cumin, 1 tsp mustard, 1 tsp chana dal, 1 dried red chilli, pinch hing, and few curry leaves. Splutter the tempering.  !
  9. Pour the tempering over the dal and mix gently.  !
  10. Finally, add 2 tbsp coriander and enjoy **Mango Dal Recipe** with hot steamed rice.  !

## Notes
  * Firstly, the amount of mango should be adjusted depending on the tanginess of mangoes.
  * Also, if you are running short of time, you can pressure cook the mangoes along with toor dal.
  * Additionally, you can use red chili powder and green chilli for a change in flavor.
  * Finally, **Mango Dal Recipe** tastes great when topped with ghee.

# Recipe 159
URL: https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/

####

####

#### 

00:02:12

####

####

####

## About Insatnt Rava Dosa:
It is a popular South Indian breakfast instant dosa recipe with essential ingredients like semolina, rice flour, and plain flour. **Rava Dosa** is a favourite dosa, particularly in metro cities like Bangalore and Chennai, and is served with spicy red and white coconut chutney. Unlike the traditional dosa recipe made with soaking and grounding, this dosa batter is made instantly by mixing water with all dry ingredients.
It is a popular choice, particularly in metro cities, for its unique characteristics. Firstly, it is super crisp, has a thin, flaky texture, and provides an enjoyable experience when served with spicy chutney or flavoured kurma recipes. There are many variations to this simple,e instant dosa recipe, but the texture and taste almost remain the same. Even though this recipe is straightforward, it needs some simple mandatory tips for the best results.

## Why does this Recipe Work?
Several key factors are highlights of this recipe, but the most important factors are
  1. **Super Crispy Texture** ‚Äì The traditional dosa varies with texture, but the suji ka dosa has a crisp, flaky texture, which makes it unique and special compared to all other dosa.
  2. **Instant Preparation** ‚Äì This rava dose requires no planning, soaking, or grounding. The dosa batter is prepared instantly by mixing water directly with dry flour and ingredients.
  3. **Versatility** ‚Äì The batter can easily experiment with various toppings, finely chopped vegetables, and herbs. Each additional ingredient adds a new flavour and a unique taste to it.
  4. **Suitable for Dietary requirements** ‚Äì The ingredients used in this **instant Rava Dosa** are essential and can easily match any dietary requirements. There are no dairy products, and hence, vegan safe and also for vegetarians.
  5. **Instant Rava Dosa Mix** ‚Äì The recipe can also be extended and prepared as an instant mix for future use. Avoid adding vegetables and herbs to the instant mix, as it may not be suitable for a longer shelf life.

### Video Recipe

## Recipe Card for Instant Rava Dosa
!

## Rava Dosa Recipe | Instant Crispy Suji Ka Dosa
HEBBARS KITCHEN
Easy rava dosa recipe | instant rava dosa | suji ka dosa | crispy rava dosa
4.95 from 340 votes
Email  
  
Prep Time 10 minutes mins
Cook Time 15 minutes mins
Resting Time 25 minutes mins
Total Time 25 minutes mins
Course Breakfast
Cuisine south indian
Servings 10 dosa

### Ingredients 
1x2x3x
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rava / semolina / suji, coarse
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω cup rice flour, fine
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬º cup maida / all purpose flour
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tbsp , optional
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp salt
  * ‚ñ¢ 2¬Ω cup water
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 chilli, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 inch ginger, grated
  * ‚ñ¢ ¬Ω tsp pepper, crushed
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 tsp cumin / jeera
  * ‚ñ¢ few curry leaves, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 2 tbsp coriander, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1 onion, finely chopped
  * ‚ñ¢ 1¬Ω water
  * ‚ñ¢ oil, for roasting

### Instructions 
  * firstly, in a large mixing bowl take ¬Ω cup rava, ¬Ω cup rice flour and ¬º cup maida.
  * also add 1 tbsp curd, 1 tsp salt and 2¬Ω cup water.
  * whisk and mix well making sure there are no lumps.
  * further add 1 chilli, 1 inch ginger, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 tsp cumin, few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander and 1 onion.
  * add 1¬Ω cup water and prepare a watery consistency batter.
  * rest the batter for 20 minutes making sure the rava has absorbed water.
  * mix well making sure the batter is thin watery consistency.
  * now carefully pour the dosa batter over very hot tawa.
  * lower the flame and cook until the dosa turns golden and crisp.
  * finally, fold the dosa and serve rava dosa immediately with tomato chutney or coconut chutney.


Tried this recipe?Mention  or tag !

## How to Make Rava Dosa with Step-by-step Photos
  1. Firstly, take ¬Ω cup rava, ¬Ω cup rice flour, and ¬º cup maida in a large mixing bowl. !
  2. Also add 1 tbsp curd, 1 tsp salt and 2¬Ω cup water. !
  3. Whisk and mix well, making sure there are no lumps. !
  4. Further add one chilli, 1-inch ginger, ¬Ω tsp pepper, 1 tsp cumin, a few curry leaves, 2 tbsp coriander, and one onion. !
  5. Add 1¬Ω cup water and prepare a watery consistency batter. !
  6. Rest the batter for 20 minutes, making sure the rava has absorbed water. !
  7. Mix well, making sure the batter is thin and watery consistent. !
  8. Now carefully pour the dosa batter over very hot tawa. Do not fill the holes, as the texture of the dosa will spoil. !
  9. Also, spread a tsp of oil uniformly. !
  10. Lower the flame and cook until the dosa turns golden and crisp. !
  11. Finally, fold the dosa and serve**it** immediately with  or . !

## Notes:
  * Firstly, prepare a flowing consistency batter, or the dosa will not be crisp.
  * Also, if you are vegan, then skip adding curd. However, adding curd gives a nice flavour.
  * Additionally, you can add dry coconut pieces and cashew pieces into the batter.
  * Finally, the **rava dosa recipe** tastes excellent when served hot and crispy.

## Faqs

### What is rava dosa? What goes well with rava dosa?
Rava dosa is a popular crepe south Indian recipe made of semolina, rice flour, and maida. they do not require any grinding or fermentation, making an instant dosa. The rava dosa batter is thin compared to regular urad dal dosa batter, which yields crispy and flaky dosa. it is served for morning breakfast or evening snacks with coconut chutney, spicy chutney, veg kurma, sagu, or sambar.

### How to get a crispy rava dosa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-12.jpeg> "crispy rava dosa")

### What are the ingredients of rava dosa and how to prepare rava dosa?
rava dosa is usually prepared with semolina, rice flour, maida, spices, and fresh herbs. First, take a bowl and add rava, rice flour, and maida to it. rava and rice flour should be in the same proportions, and maida should be half of the rava and rice flour. add salt, 1 tbsp of curd, and water to it. also, add chopped chilli, curry leaves, ginger, pepper, cumin seeds, and coriander leaves. add more water to prepare a flowing consistency batter. rest the batter for 20 minutes. sp that the rava absorbs water. pour the batter into the hot tawa and roast in low flame until the dosa leaves the tawa or turns golden brown and crisp.

### What are the other variants to prepare tasty rava dosa?
Adding chopped onions to the rava dosa batter makes onion rava dosa and adding aloo bhaji while roasting the dosa yields rava masala dosa just like traditional masala dosa. adding dry fruits to the dosa makes it a dry fruit rava dosa. the addition of finely chopped or grated veggies makes vegetable rava dosa. also, chopped cashew nuts and coconut pieces can be added to the batter, making the dosa more tasty and crunchy in every bite. adding curd to the dosa gives the golden colour and a good flavour to the dosa.

### Why does rava dosa stick to the tawa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-10.jpeg> "instant rava dosa")
Always use a heavy bottom pan or well-seasoned cast-iron tawa to make rava dosa. An iron skillet pan is the best for preparing dosas. Seasoned tawa is the one that is used earlier to prepare dosa. grease the pan well and rub it with a slice of onion before pouring each dosa. Also, do not use the same tawa when preparing roti or chapati. maintain the tawa separately for both. If the dosa sticks to the non-stick tawa, pour some batter into it and prepare a small dosa. After 2-3 dosas, the dosas won‚Äôt stick to the pan as the tawa would be hot.

### Why is my rava dosa soft and not crispy?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-9.jpeg> "instant rava dosa")
You need to use Bombay rava or fine rava. The batter should be thin and watery in consistency, not thick or medium. Medium-consistency batter also yields soft dosa. add water to the dosa batter to adjust the consistency. Adding more curd to the batter may yield soft dosas. The tawa should be very hot, and the flame should be low soon after pouring the batter into the tawa. Mix well every time you pour the batter on the tawa, and the rava and other flours settle down. Use a heavy bottom pan or cast iron tawa to prepare dosa so that it does not stick to the tawa and helps to get crispy dosa. also, serve dosa hot. else when they cool down, they turn soft.

### Should we flip over the dosa and roast on both sides in rava dosa?
Flipping of dosa is not required while roasting the rava dosa. When the dosa is cooked well, fold and remove it from the tawa. All the dosa needn‚Äôt be cooked on both sides. If the dosas are getting brown at the bottom and still moist on the top side, you may need to flip over the dosa and roast it on the other side until it turns crisp. So, as soon as the dosa is poured into the tawa, adjust the flame to low. cover and roast until the edges leave the tawa. Do not forcibly remove the dosa from the pan. A cooked dosa leaves the tawa, which indicates the cooking is done.

### How to pour the rava dosa batter into the tawa?
 ](https://hebbarskitchen.com/instant-rava-dosa-recipe-suji-ka-dosa/<https:/hebbarskitchen.com/wp-content/uploads/2019/02/rava-dosa-recipe-instant-rava-dosa-suji-ka-dosa-crispy-rava-dosa-7.jpeg> "rava dosa recipe")
The batter should be mainly thin or watery like flowing consistency. Only then is it possible to pour the batter. unlike traditional dosa, the batter is poured on the tawa, and the batter is not spread. pour it all over the tawa, beginning from the edges and towards the centre, and do not pour the batter in one place. fill the gaps by pouring the batter into them. cover and roast in low flame until it leaves the pan.

### What does my rava dosa break?
When you pour the batter into the tawa, make sure the batter is thin and flowing consistency. if it‚Äôs too skinny, the dosa might break. so add rice flour, maida, and rava according to their proportion and adjust the consistency, pour the batter into the pan.

### how to season the dosa tawa?
dosa tawa can be seasoned in the following ways: rub the tawa with gingelly oil and soak it in washed rice water for a week. rub the tawa with half the onion before spreading the dosas. heat the tawa, sprinkle salt, switch off the flame, wipe with a cloth and grease oil after it cools. clean the tawa with hot water and rub it with oil. Please keep it in the oven for one-hour upside down. Also, please do not wash the tawa when it is too hot, and do not put cold liquids on the cast iron tawa. avoid hard soaps, detergents, and steel scrubbers.

# Recipe 160
